---
title: 050

---
।।sūta uvāca।।  
adhaḥpramāṇamūrddhvañca varṇyamānaṃ nibodhata।  
pṛthivī vāyurākāśamāpo jyotiśca pañcamam।  
anantadhātavo hyete vyāpakāstu prakīrtitāḥ ।। 50.1 ।।  
  
jananī sarvabhūtānāṃ sarva bhūtadharā dharā।  
nānājanapadākīrṇā nānādhiṣṭānapattanā ।। 50.2 ।।  
  
nānānadanadīśailā naikajātisamākulā।  
anantā gīyate devī pṛthivī bahuvistarā ।। 50.3 ।।  
  
nadīnadasamudrasthāstathā kṣudrāśrayāḥ sthitāḥ।  
parvatākāśasaṃsthāśca antarbhūmigatāśca yāḥ ।। 50.4 ।।  
  
āpo'nantāśca vijñeyāstathāgniḥ sarvalaukikaḥ।  
anantaḥ paṭyate caiva vyāpakaḥ sarvasambhavaḥ ।। 50.5 ।।  
  
tathākāśamanālambaṃ ramyaṃ nānāśrayaṃ smṛtam।  
anantaṃ prathitaṃ sarvaṃ vāyuścākāśasambhavaḥ ।। 50.6 ।।  
  
āpaḥ pṛthivyāmudake pṛthivī copari sthitā।  
ākāśañcāparamadhaḥ punarbhūmiḥ punarjjalam ।। 50.7 ।।  
  
evamantamanantasya bhautikasya na vidyate।  
purā surairabhihitaṃ niścitantu nibodhata ।। 50.8 ।।  
  
bhūmirjalamathākāśamiti jñeyā paramparā।  
sthitireṣā tu vijñeyā saptame'smin rasātale ।। 50.9 ।।  
  
daśayojanasāhasramekabhaumaṃ rasātalam।  
sādhubhiḥ parivikhyātamekaikaṃ bahuvistaram ।। 50.10 ।।  
  
prathamamatalañcaiva sutalantu tataḥ param।  
tataḥ parataraṃ vidyādvitalaṃ bahuvistaram ।। 50.11 ।।  
  
tato gabhastalaṃ nāma parataśca mahātalam।  
śrītalañca tataḥ prāhuḥ pātālaṃ saptamaṃsmṛtam ।। 50.12 ।।  
  
kṛṣṇabhaumañca prathamaṃ bhūmibhāgañca kīrttitam।  
pāṇḍubhaumaṃ dvitīyantu tṛtīyaṃ raktamṛttikam ।। 50.13 ।।  
  
pītabhaumañcaturthantu pañcamaṃ śarkarātalam।  
ṣaṣṭhaṃ silāmayañcaiva sauvarṇaṃ saptamantalam ।। 50.14 ।।  
  
prathame tu tale khyātamasurendrasya mandiram।  
namucerindraśatrorhi mahānādasya cālayam ।। 50.15 ।।  
  
purañca śaṅkukarṇasya kabandhasya ca mandiram।  
niṣkulādasya ca puraṃ prahṛṣṭajanasaṅkulam ।। 50.16 ।।  
  
rākṣasasya ca bhīmasya śūladantasya cālayam।  
lohitākṣakaliṅgānāṃ nagaraṃ śvāpadasya tu ।। 50.17 ।।  
  
dhanañjayasya ca puraṃ māhendrasya mahātmanaḥ ।  
kāliyasya ca nāgasya nagaraṃ kalasasya ca ।। 50.18 ।।  
  
evaṃ purasahasrāṇiṃ nāgadānavarakṣasām।  
tale jñeyāni prathame kṛṣṇabhaume na saṃśayaḥ ।। 50.19 ।।  
  
dvitīye'pi tale viprā daityendrasya surakṣasaḥ।  
mahājambhasya ca tathā nagaraṃ prathamasya tu ।। 50.20 ।।  
  
hayagrīvasya kṛṣṇasya nikumbhasya ca mandiram।  
śaṅkhākhyeyasya ca puraṃ nagaraṃ gomukhasya ca ।। 50.21 ।।  
  
rākṣasasya ca nīlasya meghasya krathanasya ca।  
purañca kurupādasya mahoṣṇīṣasya cālayam ।। 50.22 ।।  
  
kambalasya ca nāgasya puramaśvatarasya ca।  
kadruputrasya ca puraṃ takṣakasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 50.23 ।।  
  
evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām।  
dvitīye'smin tale viprāḥ pāṇḍubhaume na saṃśayaḥ ।। 50.24 ।।  
  
tṛtīye tu talekhyātaṃ prahlādasya mahātmanaḥ।  
anuhlādasya ca puraṃ detyendrasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 50.25 ।।  
  
tārakākh‌yasya ca puraṃ puraṃ triśirasastathā।  
śiśumārasya ca puraṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulam ।। 50.26 ।।  
  
cyavanasya ca vijñeyaṃ rākṣasasya ca mandiram।  
rākṣasendrasya ca puraṃkumbhilasya kharasyaca ।। 50.27 ।।  
  
virādhasya ca krūrasya puramulkāmukhasya ca।  
hemakasya ca nāgasya tathā pāṇḍurakasya ca ।। 50.28 ।।  
  
maṇimantrasya ca puraṃ kapilasya ca mandiram।  
nandasya coragapaterviśālasya ca mandiram ।। 50.29 ।।  
  
evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām।  
tṛtīye'smistale viprāḥ pītabhaume na saṃśayaḥ ।। 50.30 ।।  
  
caturthe daityasiṃhasya kālanemermahātmanaḥ।  
gajakarṇasya ca puraṃ nagaraṃ kuñjarasya ca ।। 50.31 ।।  
  
rākṣasendrasya ca puraṃ sumālerbahuvistaram।  
muñjasya lokanāthasya vṛkavaktrasya cālayam ।। 50.32 ।।  
  
bahuyojanasāhasraṃ bahupakṣisamākulam ।  
nagaraṃ vainateyasya caturthe'smin rasātale ।। 50.33 ।।  
  
pañcame śarkarābhaume bahuyojanavistṛte।  
virocanasya nagaraṃ daityasiṃhasya dhīmataḥ ।। 50.34 ।।  
  
vaiḍhūryyasyāgnijihvasya hiraṇyākṣasya cālayam।  
purañca vidyujjihvasya rākṣasasya ca dhīmataḥ ।। 50.35 ।।  
  
mahāmeghasya ca puraṃ rākṣasendrasya śālinaḥ।  
karmmārasya ca nāgasya svastikasya jayasya ca ।। 50.36 ।।  
  
evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām।  
pañcame'pi tathā jñeyaṃ śarkarānilaye sadā ।। 50.37 ।।  
  
ṣaṣṭe tale daityapateḥ kesarernagarottamam।  
suparvvaṇaḥ sulomnaśca nagaraṃ mahiṣasya ca।  
rākṣasendrasya ca puramutkrośasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 50.38 ।।  
  
tatrāste surasāputraḥ śataśīrṣo mudā yutaḥ।  
kaśyapasya sutaḥ śrīmān vāsukirnāma nāgarāṭ ।। 50.39 ।।  
  
evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām ।  
ṣaṣṭe tale'smin vikhyāte śilābhaume rasātale ।। 50.40 ।।  
  
saptame tu tale jñeyaṃ pātāle sarvvapaścime ।  
puraṃ baleḥ pramuditaṃ naranārīsamākulam ।। 50.41 ।।  
  
asurāśīviṣaiḥ pūrṇamuddhṛtairddevaśatrubhiḥ।  
mucukundasya daityasya tatra vai nagaraṃ mahat ।। 50.42 ।।  
  
anekairditiputrāṇāṃ samudīrṇairmahāpuraiḥ।  
tathaiva nāganagaraiṛddhimadbhiḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। 50.43 ।।  
  
daityānāṃ dānavānāñca samudīrṇai rmahāpuraiḥ।  
udīrṇai rākṣasāvāsairanekaiśca samākulam ।। 50.44 ।।  
  
pātālānte ca viprendrā vistīrṇe bahuyojane।  
āste raktāravindākṣo mahātmā hyajarāmaraḥ ।। 50.45 ।।  
  
dhautaśaṅkhodaravapurnīlavāsā mahābhujaḥ।  
viśālabhogo dyutimāṃścitramālādharo balī ।। 50.46 ।।  
  
rukmaśrṛṅagāvadātena dīptāsyena virājatā।  
prabhurmukhasahasreṇa śobhate vai sa kuṇḍalī ।। 50.47 ।।  
  
sa jihvāmālayā devo lolajvālānalārciṣā।  
jvālāmālāparikṣiptaḥ kailāsa iva lakṣyate ।। 50.48 ।।  
  
sa tu netrasahasreṇa dviguṇena virājatā।  
bālasūryyābhitāmreṇa śobhate smigdhamaṇḍalaḥ ।। 50.49 ।।  
  
tasya kundenduvarṇasya akṣamālā virājate ।  
taruṇādi tyamāleva śvetaparvvatamūrddhani ।। 50.50 ।।  
  
jaṭākarālo dyutimān lakṣyate śayanāsane।  
vistīrṇa iva medinyāṃ sahasraśikharo giriḥ ।। 50.51 ।।  
  
mahābhogairmahābhāgai rmahānāgairmahābalaiḥ।  
upāsyate mahātejā mahānāgapatiḥ svayam ।। 50.52 ।।  
  
sa rājā sarvanāgānāṃ śeṣo nāma mahādyutiḥ।  
sā vaiṣṇavī hyahitanurmaryādāyāṃ vyavasthitā ।। 50.53 ।।  
  
saptaivamete kathitā vyavahāryā rasātalāḥ ।  
devāsuramahānāgarākṣasādhyuṣitāḥ sadā ।। 50.54 ।।  
  
ataḥparamanālokyamagamyaṃ siddhasādhubhiḥ।  
devā mānapyaviditaṃ vyavahāravivarjjitam ।। 50.55 ।।  
  
pṛthivyagnyambuvāyūnāṃ nabhasaśca dvijottamāḥ।  
mahattvamevamṛṣibhirvarṇyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 50.56 ।।  
  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sūryācandramasorgatim।  
sūryācandramasāvetau bhramantau yāvadeva tu।  
prakāśataḥ svabhābhistau maṇḍalābhyāṃ samāsthitau ।। 50.57 ।।  
  
saptānāñca samudrāṇāṃ dvīpānāntu sa vistaraḥ।  
vistarārddhaṃ pṛthivyāstu bhavedanyatra bāhyataḥ ।। 50.58 ।।  
  
paryāsapārimāṇyantu cāndrādityau prakāśataḥ।  
paryāsapārimāṇyena bhūmestulyaṃ divaṃ smṛtam ।। 50.59 ।।  
  
avati trīnimān lokān yasmāt sūryaḥ paribhraman।  
avadhātuḥ prakāśākhyo hyavanātsa raviḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 50.60 ।।  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ।  
mahitatvānmahīśabdo hyasmin varṣe nipātyate ।। 50.61 ।।  
  
asya bhāratavarṣasya viṣkambhantu suvistaram।  
maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasyātha yojanānāṃ nibodhata ।। 50.62 ।।  
  
navayojanasāhasro vistāro bhāskarasya tu।  
vistārātrriguṇaścāsya pariṇāho'tha maṇḍalam।  
viṣkambo maṇjalasyaiva bhāskarād dviguṇaḥ śaśī ।। 50.63 ।।  
  
ataḥ pṛthivyāṃ vakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ yojanaiḥ saha।  
saptadvīpasamudrāyā vistāro maṇjalañca yat ।। 50.64 ।।  
  
ityetadiha saṅkhyātaṃ purāṇaṃ parimāṇataḥ।  
tadvakṣyāmi prasaṅkhyāya sāmpratairabhimānibhiḥ ।। 50.65 ।।  
  
abhimānivyatītā ye tulyāste sāmpratairiha।  
devā ye vai hyatītāste rūpairnāmabhireva ca ।। 50.66 ।।  
  
tasmāttu sāmpratairdevairvakṣyāmi vasudhātalam।  
divastu sanniveśo vai sāmprataireva kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। 50.67 ।।  
  
śatārddha koṭivistārā pṛthivī kṛtsnataḥ smṛtā।  
tasyā vārdhapramāṇena merorvai cāturantaram ।। 50.68 ।।  
  
pṛthivyā vārdhavistāro yojanāgrātprakīrttitaḥ ।  
merumadhyāt prati diśaṃ koṭirekādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। 50.69 ।।  
  
tathā śatasahasrāṇi ekonanavatiḥ punaḥ।  
pañcāśacca sahasrāṇi pṛthivyā vārdhavistaraḥ ।। 50.70 ।।  
  
pṛthivyā vistaraṃ kṛtsnaṃ yojanaistannibodhata।  
tisraḥ koṭyastu vistāraḥ saṃkhyātaḥ sa caturdiśam ।। 50.71 ।।  
  
tathā śatasahasrāṇāmekonāśītirucyate।  
saptadvīpasamudrāyāḥ pṛthivyāstveṣa vistaraḥ ।। 50.72 ।।  
  
vistārāt triguṇañcaiva pṛthivyantasya maṇḍalam।  
gaṇitaṃ yojanāgrantu koṭyastvekādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। 50.73 ।।  
  
tathā śatasahasrantu sapta triṃśādhikāni tu।  
ityetadvai prasaṅkhyātaṃ pṛthivyantasya maṇḍalam ।। 50.74 ।।  
  
tārakāsanniveśasya divi yāvaddhi maṇḍalam।  
paryāsaḥ sanniveśasya bhūmastāvattu maṇḍalam ।। 50.75 ।।  
  
paryāsapārimāṇḍena bhūmestulyaṃ divaṃ smṛtam।  
saptānāmapi lokānāmetanmānaṃ prakīrtitam ।। 50.76 ।।  
  
paryāsapārimāṇḍena maṇḍalānugatena ca।  
uparyupari lokānāṃ chatravatparimaṇḍalam ।। 50.77 ।।  
  
saṃsthitirvihitā sarvā yeṣu tiṣṭhanti jantavaḥ।  
etadaṇḍakaṭāhasya pramāṇaṃ parikīrttitam ।। 50.78 ।।  
  
aṇḍasyāntastvime lokāḥ saptadvīpā ca medinī।  
bhūrlokasva bhuvaścaiva tṛtīyaḥ svariti smṛtaḥ ।  
maharloko janaścaiva tapaḥ satyaśca saptamaḥ ।। 50.79 ।।  
  
ete sapta kṛtā lokāśchatrākārā vyavasthitāḥ।  
svakairāvaraṇaiḥ sūkṣmairdhāryamāṇāḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। 50.80 ।।  
  
daśabhāgādhikābhiśca tābhiḥ prakṛtibhirbahiḥ।  
dhāryamāṇā viśeṣaiśca samutpannaiḥ parasparam ।। 50.81 ।।  
  
asyāṇḍasya samantācca sanniviṣṭo ghanodadhiḥ।  
pṛthivīmaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ ghanatoyena dhāryate ।। 50.82 ।।  
  
ghanodadhipareṇātha dhāryyate ghanatejasā।  
bāhyato ghanatejastu tiryyagūrddhvantu maṇḍalam ।। 50.83 ।।  
  
samantādvanavātena dhāryyamāṇaṃ pratiṣṭitam।  
ghanavātāttathākāśamākāśañca mahātmanā ।। 50.84 ।।  
  
bhūtādinā vṛtaṃ sarvvaṃ bhūtādhirmahatā vṛtaḥ ।  
vṛto mahānanantena pradhānenāvyayātmanā ।। 50.85 ।।  
  
purāṇi lokapālānāṃ pravakṣyāmi yathākramam ।  
jyotirgaṇapracārasya pramāṇaṃ parivakṣyate ।। 50.86 ।।  
  
meroḥ prācyāṃ diśi tathā mānasasyaiva mūrddhani।  
vasvokasārā māhendrī puṇyā hemapariṣkṛtā । 50.87 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇena punarmerormānasasyaiva mūrddhani।  
vaivasvato nivasati yamaḥ saṃyamane pure ।। 50.88 ।।  
  
pratīcyāntu punarmerormānasasyaiva mūrddhani।  
sukhā nāma purī ramyā varuṇasyātha dhīmataḥ ।। 50.89 ।।  
  
diśyuttarasyāṃ merostu mānasasyaiva mūrddhani।  
tulyā māhendrapuryyā tu somasyāpi vibhāvarī ।। 50.90 ।।  
  
mānasottarapṛṣṭe tu lokapālāścaturddiśam।  
sthitā dharmmavyavasthāyai lokasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca ।। 50.91 ।।  
  
lokapālopariṣṭāttu sarvvato dakṣiṇāyane।  
kāṣṭāgatasya sūryyasya gatiryā tāṃ nibodhata ।। 50.92 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇe prakrame sūryyaḥ kṣipteṣuriva sarpati।  
jyotiṣāñcakramādāya satataṃ parigacchati ।। 50.93 ।।  
  
madhyagaścāmarāvatyāṃ yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ।  
vaivasvate saṃyamane udayastatra ucyate ।। 50.94 ।।  
  
sukhāyāmarddharātrañca madhyagaḥ syādraviryadā।  
sukhāyāmatha vāruṇyāmuttiṣṭhan sa tu dṛśyate ।। 50.95 ।।  
  
vibhāyāmarddharātraṃ syānmāhendyrāmastameti ca।  
tadā dakṣiṇapūrvveṣāmaparāhno vidhīyate ।। 50.96 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇāpara deśyānāṃ pūrvvāhnaḥ parikīrttyate।  
teṣāmapararātrañca ye janā uttarāpathe ।। 50.97 ।।  
  
deśā uttarapūrvvā ye pūrvvarātrantu tān prati।  
evamevottareṣvarko bhavaneṣu virājate ।। 50.98 ।।  
  
sukhāyāmatha vāruṇyāṃ madhyāhne cāryyamā yadā।  
vibhāvaryyāṃ somapuryyāmuttiṣṭhati vibhāvasuḥ ।। 50.99 ।।  
  
rātryarddhaṃ cāmarāvatyāmastameti yamasya ca।  
somapuryāṃ vibhāyāntu madhyāhne syāddhivākaraḥ ।। 50.100 ।।  
  
mahendrasyāmarāvatyāmuttiṣṭhati yadā raviḥ।  
arddharātraṃ saṃyamane vāruṇyāmastameti ca ।। 50.101 ।।  
  
sa śīgrameti paryyeti bhāskaro'lātacakravat।  
bhraman vai bhramamāṇāni ṛkṣāṇi gagane raviḥ ।। 50.102 ।।  
  
evaṃ caturṣu dvīpeṣu dakṣiṇāntena sarpati।  
udayāstamanenāsāvuttiṣṭhati punaḥ punaḥ ।। 50.103 ।।  
  
pūrvvāhne cāparāhne tu dvau dvau devālayau tu saḥ।  
tapatyekantu madhyāhne taireva tu saraśmibhiḥ ।। 50.104 ।।  
  
udito varddhamānābhirāmadhyāhnaṃ tapan raviḥ।  
ataḥ paraṃ hrasantībhirgobhirastaṃ sa gacchati ।। 50.105 ।।  
  
udayāstamayābhyāṃ hismṛte pūrvāpare diśo।  
yāvatpurastāttapati tāvat pṛṣṭe tu pārśvayoḥ ।। 50.106 ।।  
  
yatrodyan dṛśyate sūryasteṣāṃ sa udayaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
yatra praṇāśamāyāti teṣāmastaḥ sa ucyate ।। 50.107 ।।  
  
sarveṣāmuttare merurlokālokastu dakṣiṇe।  
vidūrabhāvādarkasya bhūmerlekhāvṛtasya ca।  
hriyante raśmayo yasmāttena rātrau na dṛśyate ।। 50.108 ।।  
  
grahanakṣatratārāṇāṃ darśanaṃ bhāskarasya ca।  
ucchrāyasya pramāṇena jñeyamastamanodayam ।। 50.109 ।।  
  
śuklacchāyognirāpaśca kṛṣṇacchāyā ca medinī।  
vidūrabhāvādarkasya udyātasya viraśmitā।  
raktābāvo viraśmitvādraktatvāccāpyanuṣṇatā ।। 50.110 ।।  
  
lekhayāvasthitaḥ sūryo yatra yatra tu dṛśyate।  
ūrddhvaṃ gataḥ sahasrantu yojanānāṃ sa dṛśyate ।। 50.111 ।।  
  
prabhā hi saurī pādena astaṅgacchati bhāskare।  
agnimāviśate rātrau tasmāddūrāt prakāśate ।। 50.112 ।।  
  
uditastu punaḥ sūryaḥ astamāgneyamāviśat।  
saṃyukto vahninā sūryastataḥ sa tapate divā ।। 50.113 ।।  
  
prākāśyañca tathauṣṇyañca sūryāgneyī ca tejasī।  
parasparānupraveśādāpyāyete divāniśam ।। 50.114 ।।  
  
uttare caiva bhūmyarddhe tathā tasmiṃśca dakṣiṇe।  
uttiṣṭhati tathā sūrye rātrirāviśate tvapaḥ ।  
tasmāttāmrā bhavantyāpo divārātripraveśanāt ।। 50.115 ।।  
  
astaṃ yāti punaḥ sūrye dinaṃ vai praviśatyapaḥ।  
tasmācchuklā bhavantyāpo naktamahnaḥ praveśanāt ।। 50.116 ।।  
  
etena kramayogena bhūmyarddhe dakṣiṇottare।  
udayāstamane'rkasya ahorātraṃ viśatyapaḥ ।। 50.117 ।।  
  
dinaṃ sūryaprakāśākhyaṃ tāmasī rātrirucyate।  
tasmādvyavasthitā rātriḥ sūryāvekṣyamahaḥ smṛtam ।। 50.118।  
evaṃ puṣkaramadhyena yadā sarpati bhāskaraḥ।  
triṃśāṃ śakantu medinyā muhūrtenaiva gacchati ।। 50.119 ।।  
  
yojanāgrānmuhūrttasya imāṃ saṅkhyāṃ nibodhata।  
pūrṇaṃ śatasahasrāṇāmekatriṃśattu sā smṛtā ।। 50.120 ।।  
  
pañcāśattu tathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni tu।  
mauhūrttikī gatirhyeṣā sūryasya tu vidhīyate ।। 50.121 ।।  
  
etena gatiyogena yadā kāṣṭāntu dakṣiṇām।  
paryyāgacchettadādityo māghe kāṣṭāntameva hi ।। 50.122 ।।  
  
sarpate dakṣiṇāyāntu kāṣṭāyāṃ tannibodhata।  
navakoṭyaḥ prasaṅkhyātā yojanaiḥ parimaṇḍalam ।। 50.123 ।।  
  
tathā śatasahasrāṇi catvāriṃśacca pañca ca।  
ahorātrātpataṅgasya gatireṣā vidhīyate ।। 50.124 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇādvinivṛtto'sau viṣuvastho yadā raviḥ।  
kṣīrodasya samudrasya uttarāntā diśaścaran ।। 50.125 ।।  
  
maṇḍalaṃ viṣuvadyāpi yojanaistannibodhata।  
tisraḥ koṭyastu vistīrṇā viṣuvadyāpi sā smṛtā ।। 50.126 ।।  
  
tathā śatasahasrāṇāmaśītyekādhikā punaḥ ।  
śravaṇe cottarāṃ kāṣṭāñcitrabhānuryadā bhavet ।  
śākadvīpasya ṣaṣṭhasya uttarāntā diśaścaran ।। 50.127 ।।  
  
uttarāyāñca kāṣṭāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ maṇ‍ḍalasya ca।  
yojanāgrātprasaṅkhyātā koṭirekā tu sā dvijaiḥ ।। 50.128 ।।  
  
aśītirniyutānīha yojanānāṃ tathaiva ca।  
aṣṭapañcāśatañcaiva yojanānyadhikāni tu ।। 50.129 ।।  
  
nāgavīthyuttarāvīthī ajavīthī ca dakṣiṇā।  
mūlaṃ caiva tathāṣāḍe hyajavīthyudayāstrayaḥ।  
abhijitpūrvataḥ svātirnāgavīthyudayāstrayaḥ ।। 50.130 ।।  
  
kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ yacca tadvakṣye yojanaiḥ punaḥ।  
etacchatasahasrāṇāmekatriṃśottaraṃ śatam ।। 50.131 ।।  
  
trayastriṃśādhikāścānye trayastriṃśacca yojanaiḥ।  
kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ hyetadyojanāgrāt pratiṣṭitam ।। 50.132 ।।  
  
kāṣṭhayorlekhayoścaiva antare dakṣiṇottare ।  
te tu vakṣyāmi saṅkhyāya yojanaistannibodhata ।। 50.133 ।।  
  
ekaikamantarantasyā niyutānyekasaptatiḥ।  
sahasrāṇyatiriktāśca tato'nyā pañcasaptatiḥ ।। 50.134 ।।  
  
lekhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoścaiva bāhyābhyantarayoḥ smṛtam।  
abhyantarantu paryeti maṇḍalānyuttarāyaṇe ।। 50.135 ।।  
  
bāhyato dakṣiṇe caiva satatantu yathākramam।  
maṇḍalānāṃ śataṃ pūrṇamaśītyadhikamuttaram ।। 50.136 ।।  
  
carate dakṣiṇe cāpi tāvadeva vibhāvasuḥ।  
pramāṇaṃ maṇḍalasyātha yojanāgrānnibodhata ।। 50.137 ।।  
  
ekaviṃśadyojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi samāsataḥ।  
śate dve punarapyanye yojanānāṃ prakīrttite ।। 50.138 ।।  
  
ekaviṃśatibhiścaiva yojanairadhikairhi te।  
etatpramāṇamākhyātaṃ yojanairmaṇḍalaṃ hi tat ।। 50.139 ।।  
  
viṣkambho maṇḍalasyaiṣa tiryak sa tu vidhīyate।  
pratyahañcarate tāni sūryo vai maṇḍalakramam ।। 50.140 ।।  
  
kulālacakraparyanto yathā śīghraṃ nivarttate।  
dakṣiṇe prakrame sūryastathā śīghraṃ nivarttate ।। 50.141 ।।  
  
tasmāt prakṛṣṭāṃ bhūmiñca kālenālpena gacchati।  
sūryo dvādaśabhiḥ śīghraṃ muhūrtterdakṣiṇottare ।। 50.142 ।।  
  
trayodaśārddhamṛkṣāṇāmahnānucarate raviḥ।  
muhūrttaistāvadṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiścaran ।। 50.143 ।।  
  
kulālacakramadhyastu yathā mandaṃ prasarpati।  
tathodagayane sūryaḥ sarpate mandavikramaḥ ।। 50.144 ।।  
  
trayodaśārddhamarddhena ṛkṣāṇāṃ carate raviḥ।  
tasmāddīrgheṇa kālena bhūmimilpāṃ nigacchati ।। 50.145 ।।  
  
aṣṭādaśamuhūrttaistu uttarāyaṇapaścimam।  
aharbhavati taccāpi carate mandavikramaḥ ।। 50.146 ।।  
  
trayodaśārddhamardhena ṛkṣāṇāñcarate raviḥ।  
muhūrttaistāvadṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiścaran ।। 50.147 ।।  
  
tato mandataraṃ tābhyāñcakraṃ bhramati vai yathā।  
mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho dhruvo bhramati vai yathā ।। 50.148 ।।  
  
triṃśanmuhūrttāne vāhurahorātraṃ dhruvo bhraman ।  
ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramate maṇḍalāni saḥ ।। 50.149 ।।  
  
kulālacakranābhistu yathā tatraiva varttate।  
dhruvastathā hi vijñeyastatraiva parivarttate ।। 50.150 ।।  
  
ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramato maṇḍalāni tu।  
divā naktañca sūryasya mandā śīghrā ca vai gatiḥ ।। 50.151 ।।  
  
uttare prakrame tvindo rdivā mandā gatiḥ smṛtā।  
tathaiva ca punarnaktaṃ śīghrā sūryasya vai gatiḥ ।। 50.152 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇe prakrame caiva divā śīghraṃ vidhīyate ।  
gatiḥ sūryasya naktaṃ vai mandā cāpi tathā smṛtā ।। 50.153 ।।  
  
evaṃ gativiśeṣeṇa vibhajan rātryahāni tu।  
tathā vicarate mārgaṃ samena viṣameṇa ca ।। 50.154 ।।  
  
lokāloke sthitā ye te lokapālāścaturdiśam।  
agastyaścarate teṣāmupariṣṭājjavena tu ।  
bhajannasāvahorātramevaṅgativiśeṣaṇaiḥ ।। 50.155 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇe nāgavīthyāyāṃ lokālokasya cottaram।  
lokasantārako hyeṣa vaiśvānarapathādbahiḥ ।। 50.156 ।।  
  
pṛṣṭe yāvat prabhā sauhī purastāt samprakāśate।  
pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhatastāvallokālokasya sarvataḥ ।। 50.157 ।।  
  
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśorddvantūcchrito giriḥ।  
prakāśaścāprakāśaśca sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।। 50.158 ।।  
  
nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha।  
abhyantaraṃ prakāśante lokālokasya vai gireḥ ।। 50.159 ।।  
  
etāvāneva lokastu nirālokastvataḥ param।  
lokāloka ekadhā tu nirālokastvanekadhā ।। 50.160 ।।  
  
lokālokantu sandhatte yasmāt sūryaḥ parigraham।  
tasmātsandhyeti tāmāhuruṣāvyuṣṭyoryadantaram ।  
uṣā rātriḥ smṛtā viprairvyuṣṭiścāpi tvahaḥ smṛtam ।। 50.161 ।।  
  
sūryaṃ hi grasamānānāṃ sandhyākāle hi rakṣasām।  
prajāpatiniyogena śāpasteṣāṃ durātmanām ।  
akṣayatvañca dehasya prāpitā maraṇaṃ tathā ।। 50.162 ।।  
  
tisraḥ koṭyastu vikhyātā mandehā nāma rākṣasāḥ।  
prārthayanti sahasrāṃśumudayanti dine dine।  
tāpayanto durātmānaḥ sūryamicchanti khāditum ।। 50.163 ।।  
  
atha sūryasya teṣāñca yuddhamāsīt sudāruṇam।  
tato brahmā ca devāśca brāhmaṇāścaiva sattamāḥ।  
sandhyeti samupāsantaḥ kṣepayanti mahājalam ।। 50.164 ।।  
  
oṅkārabrahmasaṃyuktaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantritam।  
tena dahyanti te daityā vajrabhūtena vāriṇā ।। 50.165 ।।  
  
tataḥ punarmahātejā mahādyutiparākramaḥ.  
yojanānāṃ saha srāṇi ūrddhvamuttiṣṭhate śatam ।। 50.166 ।।  
  
tataḥ prayāti bhagavān brāhmaṇaiḥ parivāritaḥ।  
vālakhilyaiśca munibhiḥ kṛtārthaiḥ samarīcibhiḥ ।। 50.167 ।।  
  
kāṣṭā nimeṣā daśa pañca caiva triṃśacca kāṣṭā gaṇayet kalāntam ।  
triṃśat kalāścaiva bhavenmuhūrttastaistriṃśatā rātryahanī samete ।। 50.168 ।।  
  
hrāsavṛddhī tvaharbhāgairdivasānāṃ yathākramam।  
sandhyā muhūrtamānantu hrāse vṛddhau samā smṛtā ।। 50.169 ।।  
  
lekhāprabhṛtyathāditye trimuhūrttāgate tu vai।  
prātastanaḥ smṛtaḥ kālo bhāgastvahnaḥ sa pañcamaḥ ।। 50.170 ।।  
  
tasmāt prātastanātkālāt trimuhūrttastu saṅgavaḥ।  
madhyāhnastrimuhūrttastu tasmātkālācca saṅgavāt ।। 50.171 ।।  
  
tasmānmadhyandināt kālādaparāhna iti smṛtaḥ ।  
traya eva muhūrttāstu tasmāt kālācca madhyamāt ।। 50.172 ।।  
  
aparāhne vyatīpāte kāla- sāyāhna ucyate।  
daśapañcamuhūrttādvai muhūrttāstraya eva ca ।। 50.173 ।।  
  
daśapañcamuhūrttaṃ vai aharviṣuvati smṛtam।  
daśapañcamuhūrttādvai rātrindivamiti smṛtam ।। 50.174 ।।  
  
vardhdhate hrasate caiva ayane dakṣiṇottare।  
ahastu grasate rātriṃ rātristu grasate tvahaḥ ।। 50.175 ।।  
  
śaradvasantayormadhye viṣuvantadvibhāvyate।  
ahorātraṃ kalāścaiva sapta somaḥ samaśrute ।। 50.176 ।।  
  
tathā pañcadaśāhāni pakṣa ityābhidhīyate।  
dvau pakṣau ca bhavenmāso dvau māsāvantarāvṛtuḥ।  
ṛtutrayamayanaṃ syāddvai'yane varṣamucyate ।। 50.177 ।।  
  
nimeṣādikṛtaḥ kālaḥ kāṣṭāyā daśa pañca ca।  
kalāyāstriṃśataḥ kāṣṭā mātrāghītidvayātmikā ।। 50.178 ।।  
  
śataghnaikonakāstriṃśanmātrātriśat ṣaḍuttarā।  
dviṣaṣṭibhāk trayoviṃśanmātrāyāñca calā bhavet ।। 50.179 ।।  
  
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi śatānyaṣṭau ca vidyutiḥ।  
saptatiñcāpi tatraiva navatiṃ viddhi nisvaye ।। 50.180 ।।  
  
catvāryeva śatānyāhurvidyutau vaidhasaṃyuge।  
carāṃśo hyeṣa vijñeyo nālikā cātra kāraṇam ।। 50.181 ।।  
  
saṃvatsarādayaḥ pañca caturmānavikalpitāḥ।  
niścayaḥ sarvakālasya yuga ityabhidhīyate ।। 50.182 ।।  
  
saṃvatsarastu prathamo dvitīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ।  
idvatsarastṛtīyastu caturthaścānuvatsaraḥ।  
pañcamo vatsarasteṣāṃ kālastu parisaṃjñitaḥ ।। 50.183 ।।  
  
viṃśaśataṃ bhavetpūrṇaṃ parvaṇāṃ tu raveryugam।  
etānyaṣṭādaśastriṃśadudayo bhāskarasya ca ।। 50.184 ।।  
  
ṛtavastriṃśataḥ saurā ayanāni daśaiva tu।  
pañcatriṃśat śataṃ cāpi ṣaṣṭirmāsāśca bhāskaraḥ ।। 50.185 ।।  
  
triṃśadeva tvahorātraṃ sa tu māsaśca bhāskaraḥ।  
ekaṣaṣṭistvahorātrā danureko nibhāvyate ।। 50.186 ।।  
  
ahnāntu tryadhikāśītiḥ śataṃ cāpyadhikaṃ bhavet।  
mānaṃ taccitrabhānostu vijñeyaṃ bhuvanasya tu ।। 50.187 ।।  
  
saurasaumyaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ nakṣatraṃ sāvanaṃ tathā।  
nāmānyetāni catvāri yaiḥ purāṇaṃ vibhāvyate ।। 50.188 ।।  
  
khe tasyottarataścaiva śrṛṅgavānnāma parvataḥ।  
trīṇi tasya tu śrṛṅgāṇi spṛśantīva nabhastalam ।। 50.189 ।।  
  
taiścāpi śrṛṅgavānnāma sarvataścaiva viśrutaḥ।  
ekamārgaśca vistāro viṣkambhaścāpi kīrtitaḥ ।। 50.190 ।।  
  
tasya vai sarvataḥ śrṛṅgaṃ madhyamantaddhiraṇmayam।  
dakṣiṇaṃ rājatañcaiva śrṛṅgaṃ tu sphaṭikaprabham ।। 50.191 ।।  
  
sarvaratnamayaṃ caikaṃ śrṛṅgamuttaramuttamam।  
evaṃ kūṭaisribhiḥ śailaiḥ śrṛṅgavāniti viśrutaḥ ।। 50.192 ।।  
  
yattadviṣuvataṃ śrṛṅgantadarkaḥ pratipadyate।  
śaradvasantayormadhye madhyamāṃ gatimāsthitaḥ।  
ahastulyāmatho rātriṃ karoti timirāpahaḥ ।। 50.193 ।।  
  
haritāśca hayā divyāste niyuktā mahārathe।  
anuliptā ivābhānti pajharaktairgabhastibhiḥ ।। 50.194 ।।  
  
meṣānte ca tulānte ca bhāskarodayataḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
muhūrttā daśa pañcaiva ahorātriśca tāvatī ।। 50.195 ।।  
  
kṛttikānāṃ yadā sūryaḥ prathamāṃśagato bhavet ।  
viśākhānāṃ tathā jñeyaścaturthāṃśe niśākaraḥ।। 50.196 ।।  
  
viśākhāyāṃ yadā sūrya ścrateṃ'śaṃ tṛtīyakam।  
tadā candraṃ vijānīyāt kṛttikāśirasi sthitam ।। 50.197 ।।  
  
viṣuvantaṃ tadā vidyādevamāhurmaharṣayaḥ।  
sūryeṇa viṣuvaṃ vidyāt kālaṃ somena lakṣayet ।। 50.198 ।।  
  
samā rātrirahaścaiva yadā tadviṣuvadbhavet।  
tadā dānāni deyāni pitṛbhyo viṣuvatyapi।  
brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣeṇa mukhametattu daivatam ।। 50.199 ।।  
  
ūnarātrādhimāsau ca kalākāṣṭāmuhūrttakāḥ।  
paurṇamāsī tathā jñeyā amāvāsyā tathaiva ca।  
sinīvālī kuhūścaiva rākā cānumati stathā ।। 50.200 ।।  
  
tapastapasyau madhumādhavau ca śukraḥ śuciścāyanamuttaraṃ syāt।  
nabho nabhaśyo'tha iṣuḥ sahorjaḥ sahaḥsahasyāviti dakṣiṇaṃ syāt ।। 50.201 ।।  
  
saṃvatsarāstato jñeyāḥ pañcābdā brabmaṇaḥ sutāḥ।  
tasmāttu ṛtavo jñeyā ṛtavo hyantarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 50.202 ।।  
  
tasmādanumukhā jñeyā amāvāsyāsya parvaṇaḥ.  
tasmāttu viṣuvaṃ jñeyaṃ pitṛdaivahitaṃ sadā ।। 50.203 ।।  
  
evaṃ jñātvā na muhyeta daive pitrye ca mānavaḥ।  
tasmāt smṛtaṃ prajānāṃ vai viṣuvatsarvagaṃ sadā ।। 50.204 ।।  
  
ālokāntaḥ smṛto loko lokānto loka ucyate।  
lokapālāḥ sthitāstatra lokālokasya madhyataḥ ।। 50.205 ।।  
  
catvāraste mahātmānastiṣṭhantyābhūtasamplavāt।  
sudhāmā caiva vairājaḥ karddamaḥ śaṅ‌kṛpastathā।  
hiraṇyalomā parjjanyaḥ ketumān jātaniścayaḥ ।। 50.206 ।।  
  
nirdvandvā nirabhīmānā nistantrā niṣparigrahāḥ।  
lokapālāḥ sthitā hyete lokāloke caturdiśam ।। 50.207 ।।  
  
uttaraṃ yadagastyasya ajavīthyāśca dakṣiṇam।  
pitṛyāṇaḥ sa vai panthā vaiśvānarapathādbahiḥ ।। 50.208 ।।  
  
tatrāsate prajāvanto munayo hyagnihotriṇaḥ ।  
lokasya santānakarāḥ pitṛyāṇe pathi sthitāḥ ।। 50.209 ।।  
  
bhūtārambha kṛtaṃ karma āśiṣā ṛtvigucyate ।  
prārabhante lokakāmāsteṣāṃ panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ ।। 50.210 ।।  
  
calitante punarddharmaṃ sthāpayanti yuge yuge।  
santatyā tapasā caiva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca ।। 50.211 ।।  
  
jāyamānāstu pūrve vai paścimānāṃ gṛheṣu ca।  
paścimāścaiva jāyante pūrveṣāṃ nidhaneṣvapi।  
eva māvarttamānāste tiṣṭhantyābhūtasamplavāt ।। 50.212 ।।  
  
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munīnāṃ gṛhamedhinām।  
saviturddakṣiṇaṃ mārgaṃ śritā hyācandratārakam।  
kriyāvatāṃ prasaṅkhyeyā ye śmaśānāni bhejire ।। 50.213 ।।  
  
lokaśaṃvyavahāreṇa bhūtārambhakṛtena ca।  
icchādveṣaprakṛtyā ca maithunopagamena ca ।। 50.214 ।।  
  
tathā kāyakṛteneha sevanādviṣayasya ca।  
etaistaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhāḥ śmaśānāni hi bhejire।  
prajaiṣiṇaste munayo dvāpareṣviha jajñire ।। 50.215 ।।  
  
nāgavīthyuttare yacca saptarṣibhyaśca dakṣiṇam ।  
uttaraḥ savituḥ panthā devayānastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। 50.216 ।।  
  
yatra te vāsinaḥ siddhā vimalā brahmacāriṇaḥ।  
satatante jugupsante tasmānmṛtyurjjitastu taiḥ ।। 50.217 ।।  
  
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi teṣāmapyūrddhvaretasām।  
udakūpanthānamaryamṇaḥ śritā hyābhūtasamplavāt ।। 50.218 ।।  
  
ityetaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ śuddhaiste' matatvaṃ hi bhejire।  
ābhūtasamplavasthānamamṛtatvaṃ vibhāvyate ।। 50.219 ।।  
  
trailokyasthitikālo'yamapunarmārgagāminaḥ।  
brahmahatyāśvamedhābhyāṃ puṇyāpāpakṛto'param।  
ābhūtasamplavānte tu kṣīyante hyūrddhvaretasaḥ ।। 50.220 ।।  
  
ūrddhvottaramṛṣibhyastu dhruvo yatrāsti vai smṛtam।  
etadviṣṇupadaṃ divyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vyomni bhāsvaram ।। 50.221 ।।  
  
tatra gatvā na śocanti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam।  
dharmadhruvādyāstiṣṭhanti yatra te lokasādhakāḥ ।। 50.222 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte jyotiṣpracāro nāma pañcāśo'dyāyaḥ ।। 50 ।


---
title: 051

---
।।sūta uvāca।।  
svāyambhuve nisarge tu vyākhyātānyuttarāṇi tu।  
bhaviṣyāṇi ca sarvāṇi teṣāṃ vakṣyāmyanukramam ।। 51.1 ।।  
  
etacchrutvā tu munayaḥ papracchurlomaharṣaṇam।  
sūryācandramasoścāraṃ grahāṇāñcaiva sarvaśaḥ ।। 51.2 ।।  
  
।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
bhramante kathametāni jyotīṃṣi divi maṇḍalam।  
tiryagvyūhena sarvāṇi tathaivāsaṅkareṇa ca।  
kaśca bhrāmayate tāni bhramanti yadi vā svayam ।। 51.3 ।।  
  
etadveditumicchāmastanno nigada sattam।  
bhūtasammohanantvetacchrotumicchā pravarttate ।। 51.4 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca।।  
bhūtasammohanaṃ hyetad bruvato me nibodhata।  
pratyakṣamapi dṛsyaṃ yattat saṃmohayate prajāḥ ।। 51.5 ।।  
  
yo'sau caturdiśaṃ pucche śiśumāre vyavasthitaḥ।  
uttānapādaputro'sau meḍhībhūto dhruvo divi ।। 51.6 ।।  
  
sa hi bhraman bhrāmayate candrādityau grahaiḥ saha।  
bhramantamanugacchanti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat ।। 51.7 ।।  
  
dhruvasya manasā cāsau sarpate bhagaṇaḥ svayam।  
sūryācandramasau tārā nakṣatrāṇi grahaiḥ saha ।। 51.8 ।।  
  
vātānīkamayairbandhairdhruve baddhāni tāni vai।  
teṣāṃ yogasva bhedāśca kālacārastathaiva ca ।। 51.9 ।।  
  
astodayau tathotpātā ayane dakṣiṇottare।  
viṣuvad‌grahavarṇāśca dhruvātsarvaṃ pravarttate ।। 51.10 ।।  
  
varṣā dharmo himaṃ rātriḥ sandhyā caiva dinaṃ tathā ।  
śubhāśubhaṃ prajānāñca dhruvātsarvaṃ pravarttate ।। 51.11 ।।  
  
dhruveṇādhikṛtāṃścaiva sūryo'pāvṛttya tiṣṭhati।  
tadeṣa dīptakiraṇaḥ sa kālāgnirddivākaraḥ ।। 51.12 ।।  
  
parivartta kramādviprā bhābhirālokayan diśaḥ।  
sūryaḥ kiraṇajālena vāyuyuktena sarvaśaḥ।  
jagato jalamādatte kṛtsnasya dvijasattamāḥ ।। 51.13 ।।  
  
ādhityapītaṃ sūryāgneḥ somaṃ saṃkramate jalam।  
nāḍībhirvāyuyuktābhirlokādhānaṃ pravarttate ।। 51.14 ।।  
  
yatsomāt sravate sūryastadagreṣvavatiṣṭhate।  
meghā vāyunighātena visṛjanti jalambhuvi ।। 51.15 ।।  
  
ekamutkṣipyate caiva patate ca punarjjalam।  
nānāprakāramudakantadeva parivarttate ।। 51.16 ।।  
  
sandhāraṇārthaṃ bhūtānāṃ māyaiṣā viśvanirmitā।  
anayā māyayā vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। 51.17 ।।  
  
viśveśo lokakṛddevaḥ sahasrāṃśuḥ prajāpatiḥ।  
dhātā kṛtsnasya lokasya prabhu rviṣṇurdivākaraḥ ।। 51.18 ।।  
  
sarvalaukikamambho vai yatsomānnabhasaḥ snutam।  
somādhāraṃ jagatsarvametattathyaṃ prakīrtitam ।। 51.19 ।।  
  
sūryāduṣṇaṃ nisravate somācchītaṃ pravarttate।  
śītoṣṇavīryau dvāvetau yuktau dhārayato jagat ।। 51.20 ।।  
  
somādhārā nadī gaṅgā pavitrā vimalodakā।  
somaputrapurogāśca mahānadyo dvijottamāḥ ।। 51.21 ।।  
  
sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu āpo hyanugatāśca yāḥ ।  
teṣu sandahyamāneṣu jaṅgamasthāvareṣu ca।  
dhūmabhūtāstu tā āpo niṣkrāmantīha sarvaśaḥ ।। 51.22 ।।  
  
tena cābhrāṇi jāyante sthānamatrāmbhasāṃ smṛtam ।  
ārkantejo hi bhūtebhyo hyādatte raśmibhirjalam ।। 51.23 ।।  
  
samudrādvāyusaṃyogādvahantyāpo gabhastayaḥ।  
yatastvṛtuvaśāt kāle parivartto divākāraḥ।  
yacchatyapo hi meghebyaḥ śuklāḥ śuklagabhastibhiḥ ।। 51.24 ।।  
  
abhrasthā prapatantyāpo vāyunā samudīritāḥ।  
sarvabhūtahitārthāya vāyubhiśca samantataḥ ।। 51.25 ।।  
  
tato varṣati ṣaṇmāsān sarvabhūtavivṛddhaye।  
vāyavyaṃ stanitañcaiva vaidyutañcāgnisaṃbhavam ।। 51.26 ।।  
  
mehanācca miherddhātormeghatvaṃ vyañjayanti ca।  
na bhraśyanti yatastvāpastadabhraṃ kavayo viduḥ ।। 51.27 ।।  
  
meghānāṃ punarutpattistrividhā yonirucyate।  
āgneyā brahmajāścaiva pakṣajāśca pṛthagvidhāḥ।  
tridhā ghanāḥ samākhyātāsteṣāṃ vakṣyāmi sambhavam ।। 51.28 ।।  
  
āgneyāstvarṇajāḥ proktāsteṣāṃ tasmāt pravarttanam।  
śītadurdinavātā ye svaguṇāste vyavasthitāḥ ।। 51.29 ।।  
  
mahiṣāśca varāhāśca mattamātaṅgagāminaḥ।  
bhūtvā dharaṇimabhyetya vicaranti ramanti ca ।। 51.30 ।।  
  
jīmūtā nāma te meghā etebyo jīvasambhavāḥ।  
vidyudguṇavihīnāśca jaladhārāvalambinaḥ ।। 51.31 ।।  
  
mūkā ghanā mahākāyā pravāhasya vaśānugāḥ।  
krośamātrācca varṣanti krośārddhādapi vā punaḥ ।। 51.32 ।।  
  
parvatāgranitambeṣu varṣanti ca ramanti ca।  
balākāgarbhadāścaiva balākāgarbhadhāriṇaḥ ।। 51.33 ।।  
  
brahmajānāma te meghā brahmaniḥśvāsasambhavāḥ।  
te hi vidyudguṇopetāḥ stanayanti svanapriyāḥ ।। 51.34 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ śabdapraṇādena bhūmiḥ svāṅgaruhodghamā।  
rājñī rājñābhiṣikteva punaryauvanamaśrute।  
teṣviyaṃ prītimāsaktā bhūtānāṃ jīvitodbhavā ।। 51.35 ।।  
  
jīmūtā nāma te meghāstebhyo jīvasya sambhavaḥ।  
dvitīyaṃ pravahaṃ vāyuṃ meghāste tu samāśritāḥ ।। 51.36 ।।  
  
ete yojanamātrācca sārddhārddhānniṣkṛtādapi।  
vṛṣṭisargastathā teṣāṃ dhārāsārāḥ prakīrttitāḥ।  
puṣkarāvarttakā nāma ye meghāḥ pakṣasambhavāḥ ।। 51.37 ।।  
  
śakreṇa pakṣāśchinnā ye parvatānāṃ mahojasām।  
kāmagānāṃ pravṛddhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ śivamicchatā ।। 51.38 ।।  
  
puṣkarā nāma te meghā bṛhantastoya matsarāḥ।  
puṣkarāvarttakāstena kāraṇeneha śabditāḥ ।। 51.39 ।।  
  
nānārūpadharāścaiva mahāghoratarāśca te।  
kalpāntavṛṣṭeḥ sraṣṭāraḥ saṃvarttāgnerniyāmakāḥ ।। 51.40 ।।  
  
varṣantyete yugānteṣu tṛtīyāste prakīrttitāḥ।  
anekarūpasaṃsthānāḥ pūrayanto mahītalam ।  
vāyuṃ paraṃ vahantaḥ syurāśritāḥ kalpasādhakāḥ ।। 51.41 ।।  
  
yānyasyāṇḍakapālasya prākṛtasyābhavaṃstadā।  
tasmādbrahmā samutpannaścaturvaktraḥ svayambhuvaḥ।  
tānyevāṇḍakapālasya sarve meghāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।। 51.42 ।।  
  
teṣāmāpyāyanaṃ dhūmaḥ sarveṣāmaviśeṣataḥ ।  
teṣāṃ śreṣṭhastu parjjanyaścatvāraścaiva diggajāḥ ।। 51.43 ।।  
  
gajānāṃ parvatānāñca megānāṃ bhogibhiḥ saha।  
kulamekaṃ pṛthagbhūtaṃ yonirekā jalaṃ smṛtam ।। 51.44 ।।  
  
parjanyo diggajāścaiva hemante śītasambhavāḥ।  
tuṣāravṛṣṭiṃ varṣanti sarvasasyavivṛddhaye ।। 51.45 ।।  
  
śreṣṭhaḥ parivaho nāma teṣāṃ vāyurapāśrayaḥ।  
yo'sau bibhartti bhagavān gaṅgāmākāśagocarām।  
divyāmatijalāṃ puṇyāṃ vidyāṃ svargapathisthitām ।। 51.46 ।।  
  
tasyāviṣpandajantoyaṃ diggajāḥ pṛthubhiḥ karaiḥ।  
śīkaraṃ sampramuñcanti nīhāra iti sa smṛtaḥ ।। 51.47 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇena giriryo'sau hemakūṭa iti smṛtaḥ।  
udag himavataḥ śailāduttarasya ca dakṣiṇe।  
puṇḍraṃ nāma samākhyātaṃ nagaraṃ tatra vai smṛtam ।। 51.48 ।।  
  
tasminnipatitaṃ varṣaṃ yattuṣārasamudbhavam ।  
tatastadāvaho vāyurhimaśailāt samudvahan।  
ānayatyātmayogena siñcamāno mahāgirim ।। 51.49 ।।  
  
himavantamatikramya vṛṣṭiśeṣaṃ tataḥ param।  
ihābhyeti tataḥ paścādaparāntavivṛddhaye ।। 51.50 ।।  
  
meghāvāpyāyataścaiva sarvametat prakīrttitam ।  
sūrya eva tu vṛṣṭināṃ sraṣṭā samupadiśyate ।। 51.51 ।।  
  
dhruveṇā veṣṭitaḥ sūryastābyāṃ vṛṣṭiḥ pravarttate।  
dhruveṇāveṣṭito vāyurvṛṣṭiṃ saṃharate punaḥ ।। 51.52 ।।  
  
grahānniḥsṛtya sūryāttu kṛtsne nakṣatramaṇḍale ।  
vārasyānte viśatyarkaṃ dhruveṇa pariveṣṭitam ।। 51.53 ।।  
  
ataḥ sūryarathasyātha sanniveśaṃ nibodhata।  
saṃsthitainaikacakreṇa pañcāreṇa trinābhinā ।। 51.54 ।।  
  
hiraṇmayena bhagavān parvaṇā tu mahaujasā।  
naṣṭavartmāndhakāreṇa ṣaṭ‌prakāraikaneminā।  
cakreṇa bhāsvatā sūryaḥ syandanena prasarppati ।। 51.55 ।।  
  
daśa yojanasāhasro vistārāyāmataḥ smṛtaḥ।  
dviguṇo'sya rathopasthādīṣādaṇḍapramāṇataḥ ।। 51.56 ।।  
  
sa tasya brahmaṇā sṛṣṭo ratho hyarthavaśena tu।  
asaṅgaḥ kāñcano divyo yuktaḥ paramagairhayaiḥ ।। 51.57 ।।  
  
chandobhirvājirūpaistu yataḥ śukrastataḥ sthitaḥ।  
varuṇasyandanasteha lakṣaṇaiḥ sadṛśastu saḥ।  
te nā'sau sarpativyomni bhāsvatā tu divākaraḥ ।। 51.58 ।।  
  
athemāni tu sūryasya pratyaṅgāni rathasya tu।  
saṃvatsarasyāvayavaiḥ kalpitāni yathā kramam ।। 51.59 ।।  
  
ahastu nābhiḥ sūryasya ekacakraḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ।  
ārāḥ pañcarttavastasya nemiḥ ṣaḍhṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 51.60 ।।  
  
rathanīḍaḥ smṛto hyabdastvayane kūbarāvubhau ।  
muhūrtā bandhurāstasya śamyā tasya kalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 51.61 ।।  
  
tasya kāṣṭāḥ smṛtā ghoṇā īṣādaṇḍaḥ kṣaṇāṃstu vai।  
nimeṣāścānukarṣo'sya īṣā cāsya lavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 51.62 ।।  
  
rātrirvarūtho gharmo'sya dhvaja ūrddhvasamucchritaḥ।  
yugākṣakoṭī te tasya arthakāmāvubhau smṛtau ।। 51.63 ।।  
  
saptāśvarūpāśchandāṃsi vahante vāmato dhurām।  
gāyatrī caiva triṣṭupū ca anuṣṭub jagatī tathā ।। 51.64 ।।  
  
paṅktiśca bṛhatī caiva uṣṇik caiva tu saptamam।  
akṣe cakraṃ nibaddhantu dhruve tvakṣaḥ samarpitaḥ ।। 51.65 ।।  
  
sahacakro bhramatyakṣaḥ sahākṣo bhramati dhruvaḥ।  
akṣaḥ sahaiva cakreṇa bhramate'sau dhruveritaḥ ।। 51.66 ।।  
  
evamartha vaśāttasya sanniveśo rathasya tu।  
tathā saṃyogabhāgena saṃsiddho bāsvaro rathaḥ ।। 51.67 ।।  
  
tenā'sau taraṇirdevastarasā sarpate divi।  
yugākṣakoṭisambaddhau raśmī dvau syandanasya hi ।। 51.68 ।।  
  
dhruveṇa bhramato raśmī vicakrayugayostu vai।  
bhramato maṇḍalāni syuḥ khecarasya rathasya tu ।। 51.69 ।।  
  
yugākṣakoṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya tu।  
dhruveṇa saṃgṛhīte vai dvicakraśvetarajjuvat ।। 51.70 ।।  
  
bhramantamanugacchetāṃ dhruvaṃ raśmī tu tāvubhau ।  
yugākṣa koṭī te tasya vātormī syandanasya tu ।। 51.71 ।।  
  
kīlāsakto yathā rajjurbhramate sarvato diśam।  
hrasatastasya raśmī tau maṇḍaleṣūttarāyaṇe ।। 51.72 ।।  
  
varddhete dakṣiṇe caiva bhramato maṇḍalāni tu।  
dhruveṇa saṃgṛhītau tu rasmī vai nayato ravim ।। 51.73 ।।  
  
ākṛṣyete yadā tau vai dhruveṇa samadhiṣṭitau।  
tadā so'bhyantaraṃ sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ।। 51.74 ।।  
  
aśītimaṇḍalaśataṃ kāṣṭhayorubhayoścaran ।  
dhruveṇa mucyamānābhyāṃ raśmibhyāṃ punareva tu ।। 51.75 ।।  
  
tathaiva bāhyataḥ sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu।  
udveṣṭayan sa vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati ।। 51.76 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprekte jyotiṣpracāro nāmaikapañcā śo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 51 ।


---
title: 052

---
।।sūta uvāca।।  
sa ratho'dhiṣṭito devairādityaiṛṣibhistathā।  
gandharvairapsarobhiśca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ ।। 52.1 ।।  
ete vasanti vai sūrye dvau dvau māsau krameṇa tu।  
dhātāryamā pulastyaśca pulahaśca prajāpatiḥ ।। 52.2 ।।  
urago vāsukiścaiva saṅkīrṇāraśca tāvubhau।  
tumbururnāradaścaiva gandharvau gāyatāṃ varau ।। 52.3 ।।  
kratusthalyapsarāścaiva tathā vai puñjikasthalī।  
grāmaṇī rathakṛcchraśca taporyaścaiva tāvubhau ।। 52.4 ।।  
rakṣo hetiḥ prahetiśca yātudhānāvudāhṛtau।  
madhumādhavayoreṣa gaṇo vasati bhāskare ।। 52.5 ।।  
vāsantau graiṣmikau māsau mitraśca varuṇaśca ha।  
ṛṣiratrirvasiṣṭhaśca takṣako rambha eva ca ।। 52.6 ।।  
menakā sahajanyā ca gandharvau ca hahā huhūḥ।  
rathasvanaśca grāmaṇyo rathacitraśca tāvubhau ।। 52.7 ।।  
pauruṣeyo dhavaścaiva yātudhānāvudāhṛtau।  
ete vasanti vai sūrye māsayoḥ śuciśukrayoḥ ।। 52.8 ।।  
tataḥ sūrye punastvanyā nivasantīha devatāḥ।  
indraścaiva vivasvāṃśca aṅgirā bhṛgureva ca ।। 52.9 ।।  
elāparṇastathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālaśca tāvubhau।  
viśvāvasūgrasenau ca prātaścaivāruṇaśca ha ।। 52.10 ।।  
pramloceti ca vikhyātā nimloceti ca te ubhe।  
yātudhānastathā sarpo vyāghraḥ śvetaśca tāvubhau।  
nabhonabhasyayoreṣa gaṇo vasati bhāskare ।। 52.11 ।।  
śaradṛ-tau punaḥ śubhrā vasanti muni devatāḥ।  
parjjanyaścātha pūṣā ca bharadvājaḥ sagautamaḥ ।। 52.12 ।।  
viśvāvasuśca gandharvāstathaiva surabhiśca yaḥ।  
viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te śubhalakṣaṇe ।। 52.13 ।।  
nāga airāvataścaiva viśrutaśca dhanañjayaḥ।  
senajicca suṣeṇaśacava senānīrgrāmaṇīśca tau ।। 52.14 ।।  
āpo vātaśca tāvetau yātudhānāvubhau smṛtau।  
vasantyete tu vai sūrye māsayośca iṣorjayoḥ ।। 52.15 ।।  
haimantikau tu dvau māsau vasanti tu divākare।  
aṃśo bhagaśca dvāvetau kaśyapaśca ṛtuśca ha ।। 52.16 ।।  
bhujaṅgaśca mahāpajhaḥ sarpaḥ karkoṭakastathā।  
citrasenaśca gandharva ūrṇāyuścaiva tāvubhau ।। 52.17 ।।  
urvaśī vipracittiśca tathaivāpsarasau śubhe।  
tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiśca senānīrgrāmaṇīśca tau ।। 52.18 ।।  
vidyutsphūrjjaśca tāvugrau yātudhānāvudāhṛtau।  
sahe caiva sahasye ca vasantyete divākare ।। 52.19 ।।  
tataḥ śaiśirayośvāpi māsayornivasanti vai।  
tvaṣṭā viṣṇurjamadagnirviśvāmitrastathaiva ca ।। 52.20 ।।  
kādraveyau tathā nāgau kambalāśvatarāvubhau।  
gandharvo dhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryavarccāstathaiva ca ।। 52.21 ।।  
tilottamāpsarāścaiva devī rambā manoramā।  
ṛtajitsatyajiccaiva grāmaṇyau lokaviśrutau ।। 52.22 ।।  
brahmopetastathā dakṣo yajñopetaśca sa smṛtaḥ।  
ete devā vasantyarke dvau māsau tu krameṇa tu ।। 52.23 ।।  
sthānābhimānino hyete gaṇā dvādaśa saptakāḥ।  
sūryamāpyāyayantyete tejasā teja uttamam ।। 52.24 ।।  
prathitaistairvacobistu stuvanti munayo ravim।  
gandharvāpsarasaścaiva gītanṛtyairupāsate ।। 52.25 ।।  
grāmaṇīyakṣabhūtāstu kurvate bhīmasaṃgraham।  
sarpā vahanti sūryañca yātudhānānuyānti ca।  
vālakhilyā nayantyastaṃ paricāryodayādravim ।। 52.26 ।।  
eteṣāmeva devānāṃ yatāvīryaṃ yathātapaḥ।  
yathāyogaṃ yathāsatyaṃ yathādharmaṃ yatābalam ।। 52.27 ।।  
yathā tapatyasau sūryasteṣāṃ siddhastu tejasā।  
ityete vai vasantīha dvau dvau māsau divākare ।। 52.28 ।।  
ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ pannagāpsarasāṅgaṇāḥ ।  
grāmaṇyaśca tathā yakṣā yātudhānāśca bhūriśaḥ ।। 52.29 ।।  
ete tapanti varṣanti bhānti vānti sṛjanti ca।  
bhūtānāmaśubhaṃ karma vyapohantīha kīrtitāḥ ।। 52.30 ।।  
mānavānāṃ śubhaṃ hyete haranti duritātmanām।  
duritaṃ hi pracārāṇāṃ vyapohanti vkacit vkacit ।। 52.31 ।।  
vimāne'vasthitā divye kāmagā vātaraṃhasaḥ।  
ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti divasānugāḥ ।। 52.32 ।।  
varṣantaśca tapantaśca hlādayantaśca vai prajāḥ।  
gopāyanti tu bhūtāni sarvānīhāmanukṣayāt ।। 52.33 ।।  
sthānābhimānināmetat sthānaṃ manvantareṣu vai।  
atītānāgatānāṃ vai varttante sāmpratantu ye ।। 52.34 ।।  
evaṃ vasanti vai sūrye saptakāste caturddiśam।  
caturddaśasu sargeṣu gaṇā manvantareṣu ca ।। 52.35 ।।  
grīṣme hime ca varṣāsu muñcamānā gharmaṃ himañca varṣañca dinaṃ niśāñca।  
kālena gacchatyṛtuvaśāt parivṛttaraśmi rdevān pitṝṃśca manujāṃśca tarpayan vai ।। 52.36 ।।  
prīṇāti devānamṛtena sūryaḥ somaṃ suṣumnena vivarddhayitvā ।  
śukle tu pūrṇaṃ divasakrameṇa taṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe vibudhāḥ pibanti ।। 52.37 ।।  
pītantu somaṃ dvikālāvaśiṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇakṣaye raśmibhistaṃ kṣarantam।  
sudhāmṛtaṃ tatpitaraḥ pibanti devāśca saumyāśca tathaiva kavyam ।। 52.38 ।।  
sūryeṇa gobhistu samuddhṛtābhiradbhiḥ punaścaiva samuddhṛtābhiḥ।  
vṛṣṭyātivṛddhābhirathauṣadhībhirmartyāḥ kṣudhantvannapānairjayanti ।। 52.39 ।।  
amṛtena tṛptistvarddhamāsaṃ surāṇāṃ māsārddhatṛptiḥ svadhayā pitṝṇām।  
annena śaśvattu dadhāti martyān sūryaḥ svayaṃ tacca bibharti gobhiḥ ।। 52.40 ।।  
ayaṃ haristairharibhisturaṅgamairayan hi cāpo haratīti raśmibhiḥ।  
visargakāle visṛjaṃśca tāḥ punarbibharti śaśvat savitā carācaram ।। 52.41 ।।  
harirharidbhirhriyate turaṅgamaiḥ pibatyathāpo haribhiḥ sahasradhā।  
tataḥ pramuñcatyapi tāstvasau hariḥ sa muhyamāno haribhisturaṅgamaiḥ ।। 52.42 ।।  
ityeṣa ekacakreṇa sūryastūrṇaṃ rathena tu।  
bhadraistairakṣatairaśvaiḥ sarpate'sau divi kṣaye ।। 52.43 ।।  
ahorātrādrathaināsau ekacakreṇa tu bhraman।  
saptadvīpasamudrāntaṃ saptabhiḥ saptabhirhayaiḥ ।। 52.44 ।।  
chandobhiraśvarūpaistairyataścakrantataḥ sthitaiḥ।  
kāmarūpaiḥ sakṛdyuktairamitaistairmanojavaiḥ ।। 52.45 ।।  
haritairavyayaiḥ piṅgairīśvarairbrahmavādibhiḥ।  
aśīti maṇḍalaśataṃ bhramantyabdena te hayāḥ ।। 52.46 ।।  
bāhyamabhyantarañcaiva maṇḍalaṃ divasakramāt ।  
kalpādau samprayuktāste vahantyābhūtasamplavāt।  
āvṛtā vālakhilyaiste bhramante rātryahāni tu ।। 52.47 ।।  
prathitairvacobhaṅiragryaiḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ।  
saivyate gītavṛtyaiśca gandharvairapsarogaṇaiḥ।  
pataṅgaḥ pata gairaśvairbhramamāṇo divaspatiḥ ।। 52.48 ।।  
vīthyāśrayāṇi carati nakṣatrāṇi tathā śaśī।  
hrāsavṛddhī tathaivāsya raśmīnāṃ sūryavat smṛte ।। 52.49 ।।  
tricakrobhayapārśvastho vijñeyaḥ śaśino rathaḥ।  
apāṃ garbhasamutpanno rathaḥ sāśvaḥ sasārathiḥ।  
śatāraiśca tribhiścakrairyuktaḥ śulkairhayottamaiḥ ।। 52.50 ।।  
daśa bhistu kṛśairdivyairasaṅgaistairmanojavaiḥ।  
sakṛdyukte rathe tasmin vahante cāyugakṣayāt ।। 52.51 ।।  
saṃgṛhīte rathe tasmin śvetaścakṣuḥśravāstu vai।  
aśvā stamekavarṇāste vahante śaṅkhavarccasam ।। 52.52 ।।  
yayuśca trimanāścaiva vṛṣo rājīvalo hayaḥ।  
asvo vāmasturaṇyaśca haṃso vyomī mṛgastathā ।। 52.53 ।।  
ityete nāmabhiḥ sarve daśa candramaso hayāḥ ।  
ete candramasaṃ devaṃ vahanti divasakṣayāt ।। 52.54 ।।  
devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ saumyaḥ pitṛbhiścaiva gacchati।  
somasya śukla pakṣādau bhāskare purataḥ sthite।  
āpūryate purasyāntaḥ satataṃ divasakramāt ।। 52.55 ।।  
devaiḥ pītaṃ kṣaye somamāpyāyayati nityadā।  
pītaṃ pañcadaśāhantu raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ ।। 52.56 ।।  
āpūrayan suṣumnena bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt ।  
suṣumnāpyāyamānasya śuklā varddhanti vai kalāḥ ।। 52.57 ।।  
tasmāddhrasanti vai kṛṣṇe śukla āpyāyayanti ca।  
ityevaṃ sūryavīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ ।। 52.58 ।।  
paurṇamāsyāṃ sa dṛśyeta śuklaḥ sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।  
evamāpyāyitaḥ somaḥ śuklapakṣe dinakramāt ।। 52.59 ।।  
tato dvitīyāprabhṛti bahulasya caturddaśī।  
apāṃ sāramayasyendo rasamātrātmakasya ca।  
pibantyambumayaṃ devā madhu saumyaṃ sudhāma yam ।। 52.60 ।।  
sambhṛtañcārddhamāsena amṛtaṃ sūryatejasā ।  
bhakṣārthamamṛtaṃ saumyaṃ paurṇamāsyāmupāsate ।। 52.61 ।।  
ekarātraṃ suraiḥ sarvaiḥ pitṛbhiśca maharṣibhiḥ।  
somasya kṛṣṇapakṣādau bhāskarābhimukhasya ca ।। 52.62 ।।  
prakṣīyate purasyāntaḥ pīyamānāḥ kalāḥ kramāt।  
kṣīyante tasmāt kṛṣṇe yāḥ śukle hyāpyāyayanti tāḥ ।। 52.63 ।।  
evaṃ dinakramātīte vibudhāstu niśākaram ।  
pītvā'rddhamāsaṅgacchanti amāvāsyāṃ surottamāḥ ।  
pitaraścopatiṣṭhanti amāvāsyāṃ niśākaram ।। 52.64 ।।  
tataḥ pañcadaśe bhāge kiñcicchiṣṭe kalātmake।  
aparāhne pitṛgaṇairjaghanyaḥ paryupāsyate ।। 52.65 ।।  
pibanti dvikalākālaṃ śiṣṭā tasya tu yā kalā।  
niḥsṛtaṃ tadamāvāsyāṅgabhastibhyaḥ svadhāmṛtam।  
tāṃ svadhāṃ māsatṛptyai tu pītvā gacchanti te'mṛtam ।। 52.66 ।।  
saumyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāstathaiva ca।  
kavyāścaiva tu ye proktāḥ pitaraḥ sarva eva te ।। 52.67 ।।  
saṃvatsarāstu vai kavyāḥ pañcābdā ye dvijaiḥ smṛtāḥ।  
saumyāstu ṛtavo jñeyā māsā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ।  
agniṣvāttārtavaścaiva pitṛsargā hi vai dvijāḥ ।। 52.68 ।।  
pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānasya pañcadaśyāṃ kalā tu vai।  
yāvanna kṣīyate tasya bhāgaḥ pañcadaśa stu saḥ ।। 52.69 ।।  
amāvasyāntadā tasya antamāpūryate param।  
vṛddhikṣayau vai pakṣādau ṣoḍaśyāṃ śaśinaḥ smṛtau ।। 52.70 ।।  
evaṃ sūryanimittaiṣā kṣayavṛddhi rniśākare।  
tārāgrahāṇāṃ vakṣyāmi svarbhānośca rathaṃ punaḥ ।। 52.71 ।।  
toyatejomayaḥ śubhraḥ somaputrasya vai rathaḥ।  
yukto hayaiḥ piśaṅgaistu aṣṭābhirvātaraṃhasaiḥ ।। 52.72 ।।  
savarūthaḥ sānukarṣaḥ sūto divyo rathe mahān।  
sopāsaṅgapatākastu sadhvajo meghasannibhaḥ ।। 52.73 ।।  
bhārgavasya rathaḥ śrīṇāṃstejasā sūryasannibhaḥ।  
pṛthivīsambhavairyukto nānāvarṇairhayottamaiḥ ।। 52.74 ।।  
śvetaḥ piśaṅgaḥ sāraṅgo nīlaḥ pīto vilohitaḥ।  
kṛṣṇaśca haritaścaiva pṛṣataḥ pṛṣṇireva ca।  
daśabhi stairmahābhāgairakṛśairvātavegitaiḥ ।। 52.75 ।।  
aṣṭāśvaḥ kāñcanaḥ śrīmān somasyāpi ratho'bhavat।  
asaṅgairlauhitairaśvaiḥ sarvagairagnisambhavaiḥ।  
sarpate'sau kumāro vai ṛjuvakrānucakragaḥ ।। 52.76 ।।  
tatastvāṅgiraso vidvān devācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ।  
śoṇairaśvaiḥ kāñcanena syandanena prasarpati ।। 52.77 ।।  
yuktastu vājibhirdivyairaṣṭābhirvātasammitaiḥ।  
nakṣatre'bdannivasati savegastena gacchati ।। 52.78 ।।  
tataḥ śanaiśvaropyaśvaiḥ śabalairvyomasambhavaiḥ।  
kārṣṇāyasaṃ samāruhya syandanaṃ yāti vai śanaiḥ ।। 52.79 ।।  
svarbhānostu tathaivāśvāḥ kṛṣṇā hyaṣṭau manojavāḥ।  
rathantamomayantasya sakṛdyuktā vahantyuta ।। 52.80 ।।  
ādityānniḥsṛto rāhuḥ somaṃ gacchati parvasu।  
ādityameti somācca punaḥ saureṣu parvasu ।। 52.81 ।।  
atha keturathasyāśvā aṣṭāṣṭau vātaraṃhasaḥ।  
palāladhūmasaṅkāśāḥ śabalā rāsabhāruṇāḥ ।। 52.82 ।।  
ete vāhā grahāṇāṃ vai mayā proktā rathaiḥ saha।  
sarve dhruvanibaddhāste prabaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ ।। 52.83 ।।  
ete vai bhrāmyamāṇāstu yathā yogaṃ bhramanti vai।  
vāyavyābhiradṛśyābhiḥ prabaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ ।। 52.84 ।।  
paribhramanti tadbaddhāścandrasūryagrahā divi।  
bhramantamanugacchanti dhruvante jyotiṣāṃ gaṇāḥ ।। 52.85 ।।  
yathā nadyudake naustu salilena sahohyate।  
tathā devālayā hyete uhyante vātaraśmibhiḥ।  
tasmātsarveṇa dṛsyante vyomni devagaṇāstu te ।। 52.86 ।।  
yāvantyaścaiva tārāstu tāvanto vātaraśmayaḥ।  
sarvā dhruvanibaddhāstā bramantyo bhrāmayanti tam ।। 52.87 ।।  
tailapīḍākaraṃ cakraṃ bhramadbhrāmayate yathā।  
tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vāyabaddhāni sarvaśaḥ ।। 52.88 ।।  
alātacakravadyānti vātacakreritāni tu।  
tasmājjyotīṃṣi vahate pravahaṃstena sa smṛtaḥ ।। 52.89 ।।  
evaṃ dhruvanibaddho'sau sarpate jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ।  
saiṣa tārāmayojñeyaḥ śiśumāro dhruvo divi।  
yadahnā kurute pāpaṃ dṛṣṭavā taṃ niśi mucyate ।। 52.90 ।।  
yāvatyaścaiva tārāstāḥ śiśūmārāśritā divi।  
tāvantyeva tu varṣāṇi jīvantyabhyadhikāni tu ।। 52.91 ।।  
śāśvataḥ śiśumāro'sau vijñeyaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ।  
uttānapādastasyātha vijñeyo hyuttaro hanuḥ ।। 52.92 ।।  
yajño'dharastu vijñeyo dharmo mūrddhānamāśritaḥ।  
hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ sādhyaḥ aśvinau pūrvapādayoḥ ।। 52.93 ।।  
varuṇaścāryamā caiva paścime tasya sasthini।  
śiśraḥ saṃvatsarastasya mitro'pāne samāśritaḥ ।। 52.94 ।।  
pucche'gniśca mahendraśca marīciḥ kaśyapo dhruvaḥ।  
tārakāḥ śiśumāraśca nāstameti catuṣṭayam ।। 52.95 ।।  
nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇeḥ saha।  
unmukhābhimukhāḥ sarve cakrībhūtāśritā divi ।। 52.96 ।।  
dhruveṇādhiṣṭitāḥ sarve dhruvameva pradakṣiṇam ।  
prayāntīha varaṃ śreṣṭhamedhībhūtaṃ dhruvandivi ।। 52.97 ।।  
dhruvāgnikaśyapānāntu varasvāsau dhruvaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
eka eva bhramatyeṣa meruparvatamūrddhani ।। 52.98 ।।  
jyotiṣāñcakrametaddhi sadā karṣatyavāṅmukhaḥ।  
merumālokayatyeṣa prayātīha pradakṣiṇam ।। 52.99 ।।  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte dhruvacaryā nāma dvipañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 52 ।


---
title: 053

---
।। śāṃśapāyana uvāca ।।  
etacchrutvā tu munayaḥ punaste saṃśayānvitāḥ।  
papracchuruttaraṃ bhūyastadā te lomaharṣaṇam ।। 53.1 ।।  
।।ṛṣaya ucuḥ ।।  
yadetaduktambhavatā gṛhāṇyetāni viśritam।  
kathaṃ devagṛhāṇi syuḥ kathaṃ jyotīṃṣi varṇaya ।। 53.2 ।।  
etatsarvaṃ samācakṣva jyotiṣāñcaiva niścayam।  
śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ tadā sūtaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। 53.3 ।।  
asminnarthe mahāprājñairyaduktaṃ jñānabuddhibhiḥ।  
tadvo'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi sūryācandramasorbhavam।  
yathā devagṛhāṇīha sūryācandramasorgṛham ।। 53.4 ।।  
ataḥ paraṃ trividhāgnervakṣye'hantu samudbhavam।  
divyasya bhautikasyāgnerathāgneḥ pārthivasya ca ।। 53.5 ।।  
vyuṣṭāyāntu rajanyāṃ vai brahmaṇo'vyaktajanmanaḥ।  
avyākṛtamidantvāsīnnaiśena tamasāvṛtam ।। 53.6 ।।  
caturbhūtāvaśiṣṭe'smin pārthivaḥ so'gnirucyate।  
yaścādau tapate sūrye śuciragnistu sa smṛtaḥ ।। 53.7 ।।  
vaidyutākhyastu vijñeyasteṣāṃ vakṣye'tha lakṣaṇam।  
vaidyuto jāṭharaḥ sauro hyapāṅgarbhāstrayo'gnayaḥ।  
tasmādapaḥ piban sūryo gobhidīrpyatyasau divi ।। 53.8 ।।  
vaidyutena samāviṣṭo vārkṣo nādbhiḥ praśāmyati ।  
mānavānāñca kukṣistho nādbhiḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ ।। 53.9 ।।  
arcciṣmān paramaḥ so'gniḥ prabhavo jāṭharaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
yaścāyaṃ maṇḍalī śuklo nirūṣmā saṃprakāśate ।। 53.10 ।।  
prabhā hi saurī pādena hyastaṃ yāti divākare।  
agnimāviśate rātrau tasmād‌dūrāt prakāśate ।। 53.11 ।।  
udyantañca punaḥ sūryamauṣṇyamāgneyamāviśat।  
pādena pārthivasyāgnestasmādagnistapatyasau ।। 53.12 ।।  
prakāśaśca tathauṣṇyañca saurāgneye tu tejasī।  
parasparānupraveśādāpyāyete divāniśam ।। 53.13 ।।  
uttare caiva bhūmyarddhe tasmādasmiṃśca dakṣiṇe।  
uttiṣṭhati punaḥ sūrye rātrirāviśate tvapaḥ।  
tasmāttāmrā bhavantyāpo divārātripraveśanāt ।। 53.14 ।।  
astaṃ yāti punaḥ sūrye aharvai praviśatyapaḥ।  
tasmānnaktaṃ punaḥ śuklā āpo viśyanti bhāskare ।। 53.15 ।।  
etena kramayogena bhūmyarddhe dakṣiṇottare ।  
udayāstamaye nityamahorātraṃ viśatyapaḥ ।। 53.16 ।।  
yaścāsau tapate sūrye pibannambho gabhastibhiḥ।  
pārthivo hi vimiśro'sau divyaḥ śuciriti smṛtaḥ ।। 53.17 ।।  
sahasrapādaḥ so'gnistu vṛttaḥ kumbhanibhaḥ śuciḥ।  
ādatte tattu raśmīnāṃ sahasreṇa samantataḥ ।। 53.18 ।।  
nādeyīścaiva sāmudrīḥ kaupyāścaiva sadhānvanīḥ।  
sthāvarā jaṅgamāścaiva yaśca sūryo hiraṇmayaḥ।  
tasya raśmisahasrantu varṣaśītoṣṇaniḥsravam ।। 53.19 ।।  
tāsāñcatuḥśatā nāḍyo varṣanti citramūrttayaḥ।  
vandanāścaiva vandyaśca ṛtanā nūtanāstathā।  
amṛtā nāmataḥ sarvvā raśmayo vṛṣṭisarjanāḥ ।। 53.20 ।।  
himavāhāśca tābhyo'nyā raśmayastriśatāḥ punaḥ।  
dṛśyā medhyāśca vāhyāśca hrādinyo himasarjanāḥ ।। 53.21 ।।  
candrāstā nāmataḥ sarvāḥ pītābhāstu gabhastayaḥ।  
śuklāśca kakubhaścaiva gāvo viśvabhṛtastathā ।। 53.22 ।।  
śuklāstā nāmataḥ sarvāstriśatā gharmasarjanāḥ।  
samaṃ bibharti tābhistu manuṣyapitṛdevatāḥ ।। 53.23 ।।  
manuṣyānauṣadheneha svadhayā ca pitṝnapi।  
amṛtena surān sarvāṃstrīṃstribhistarpayatyasau ।। 53.24 ।।  
vasante caiva grīṣme ca sataiḥ sutapate tribhiḥ।  
varṣāsvatho śaradi ca caturbhiḥ samprakarṣati ।। 53.25 ।।  
hemante śiśire caiva himaṃ sa sṛja te tribhiḥ।  
oṣadhīṣu balandhatte svadhayā ca pitṝnapi।  
sūryo'maratvamamṛtatrayantriṣu niyacchati ।। 53.26 ।।  
evaṃ raśmisahasrantat sauraṃ lokārtha sādhakam।  
bhidyate ṛtumāsādya jalaśītoṣṇaniḥsravam ।। 53.27 ।।  
ityetanmaṇḍalaṃ śuklaṃ bhāsvaraṃ sūryasaṃjñitam।  
nakṣatragrahasomānāṃ pratiṣṭāyonireva ca।  
ṛkṣacandragrahāḥ sarve nijñeyāḥ sūryasambhavāḥ ।। 53.28 ।।  
nakṣatrādhipatiḥ somo graharājo divākaraḥ।  
śeṣāḥ pañcagrahā jñeyā īśvarāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ ।। 53.29 ।।  
paṭyate cāgnirāditya audakaścandramāḥ smṛtaḥ।  
śeṣāṇāṃ prakṛtiṃ samyagvarṇyamānāṃ nibodhata ।। 53.30 ।।  
surasenāpati skandaḥ paṭyate'ṅgārako grahaḥ ।  
nārāyaṇaṃ budhaṃ prāhurdevaṃ jñānavido viduḥ ।। 53.31 ।।  
rudro vaivasvataḥ sākṣāddharmo loke prabhuḥ svayam।  
mahāgraho dvijaśreṣṭo mandagāmī śanaiścaraḥ ।। 53.32 ।।  
devāsuragurū dvau tu bhānumantau mahāgrahau।  
prajāpatisutāvetāvubhau śukrabṛhaspatī।  
daityo mahendraśca tayorādhipatye vinirmitau ।। 53.33 ।।  
ādityamūlamakhilaṃ trilokaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ।  
bhavatyasya jagatkṛtsnaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। 53.34 ।।  
rudrendropendracandrāṇāṃ viprendrāstridivaukasām।  
dyutirdyutimatāṃ kṛtsnā yattejaḥ sārvalaukikam ।। 53.35 ।।  
sarvātmā sarvalokeśo mūlaṃ paramadaivatam।  
tataḥ saṃjāyate sarvaṃ tatra caiva pralīyate ।। 53.36 ।।  
bāvābhāvau hi lokānāmādityānniḥ sṛtau purā।  
jagajjñeyo graho viprā dīptimān sugrāho raviḥ ।। 53.37 ।।  
yatra gacchanti nidhanaṃ jāyante ca punaḥ punaḥ।  
kṣaṇā muhūrttā divasā niśāḥ pakṣāśca kṛtsnaśaḥ।  
māsāḥ saṃvatsarāścaiva ṛtavo'ndayugāni ca ।। 53.38 ।।  
tadādityādṛte teṣāṃ kālasaṃkhyā na vidyate।  
kālādṛte na nigamo na dīkṣā nāhnikakramaḥ ।। 53.39 ।।  
ṛtunāmavibhāgaśca puṣpamūlaphalaṃ kutaḥ।  
kutaḥ sasyābhiniṣpattirguṇauṣadhigaṇādi vā ।। 53.40 ।।  
abhāvo vyavahārāṇāṃ devānāṃ divi ceha ca।  
jagatpratāpanamṛte bhāskaraṃ vāritaskaram ।। 53.41 ।।  
sa eva kālaścāgniśca dvādaśātmā prajāpatiḥ।  
tapatyeṣa dvijaśreṣṭāstrailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। 53.42 ।।  
sa eṣa tejasāṃ rāśiḥ samastaḥ sārvalaukikaḥ।  
uttamaṃ mārgamāsthāya vāyobhābhiridañjagat।  
pārśvamūrddhvamadhaścaiva tāpayatyeṣa sarvaśaḥ ।। 53.43 ।।  
raveraśmisahasraṃ yat prāṅmayā samudāhṛtam ।  
teṣāṃ śreṣṭāḥ punaḥ sapta raśmayo grahayonayaḥ ।। 53.44 ।।  
suṣumno harikeśaśca viśvakarmā tathaiva ca।  
viśvaśravāḥ punaśvānyaḥ sampadvasurataḥ param ।  
arvāvasuḥ punaścānyomayā cātra prakīrttitaḥ ।। 53.45 ।।  
suṣumnaḥ sūryaraśmistu kṣīṇaṃ śaśinamedhayan।  
tiryagūrddhvaprabhāvo'sau suṣumnaḥ parikīrtyate ।। 53.46 ।।  
harikeśaḥ purastvādyā ṛkṣayoniḥ prakīrtyate।  
dakṣiṇe viśvakarmā tu raśmirvarddhayate budham ।। 53.47 ।।  
viśvaśravāstu yaḥ paścāt śukrayoniḥ smṛto budhaiḥ।  
sampadvasuśca yo raśmiḥ sā yonirlohitasya ca ।। 53.48 ।।  
ṣaṣṭhastvarvāvasū raśmiryonistu sa bṛhaspateḥ।  
śanaiścaraṃ punaścāpi raśmirāpyāyate svarāṭ ।। 53.49 ।।  
evaṃ sūryaprabhāveṇa grahanakṣatratārakāḥ।  
varddhante viditāḥ sarvā viśvañcaidaṃ punarjagat ।  
nakṣīyante punastāni tasmānnakṣatratā smṛtā ।। 53.50 ।।  
kṣetrāṇyetāni vai pūrvamāpatanti gabhastibhiḥ।  
teṣāṃ kṣetrāṇyathādatte sūryo nakṣatratāṅgataḥ ।। 53.51 ।।  
tīrṇānāṃ sukṛteneha sukṛtānte grahāśrayāt ।  
tārāṇāṃ tārakā hyetāḥ śuklatvāccaiva tārakāḥ ।। 53.52 ।।  
divyānāṃ pārthivānāñca naiśānāñcaiva sarvaśaḥ ।  
ādānānnityamādityastamasāṃ tejasāṃ mahān ।। 53.53 ।।  
suvati spandanārthe ca dhātureṣa vibhāvyate।  
savanāttejaso'pāñca tenāsau savitā mataḥ ।। 53.54 ।।  
bahvarthaścandra ityeṣa hlādane dhāturiṣyate ।  
śuklatve cāmṛtatve ca śītatve ca vibhāvyate ।। 53.55 ।।  
suryācandramasordivye maṇḍale bhāsvare khage।  
jvalattejomaye śukle vṛttakumbhanibhe śubhe ।। 53.56 ।।  
ghanatoyātmakaṃ tatra maṇḍalaṃ śaśinaḥ smṛtam।  
ghanatejomayaṃ śuklaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasya tu ।। 53.57 ।।  
viśanti sarvadevāstu sthānānyetāni sarvaśaḥ।  
manvantareṣu sarveṣu ṛkṣasūryagrahāśrayāḥ ।। 53.58 ।।  
tāni devagṛhāṇyeva tadākhyāste bhavanti ca।  
sauraṃ sūryo viśasthānaṃ saumyaṃ somastathaiva ca ।। 53.59 ।।  
śaukraṃ śukro viśasthānaṃ ṣoḍaśārcciḥ pratāpavān।  
bṛhadbṛhaspatiścaiva lohitaścaiva lauhitaḥ ।  
śānaiścaraṃ tathā sthānaṃ deva ścaiva śanaiścaraḥ ।। 53.60 ।।  
ādityaraśmisaṃyogāt saṃprakāśātmikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
navayojanasāhasro viṣkambhaḥ savituḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 53.61 ।।  
triguṇastasya vistāro maṇḍalañca pramāṇataḥ।  
dviguṇaḥ sūryavistārādvistāraḥ śaśinaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 53.62 ।।  
tulyastayostu svarbhānurbhūtvādhastāt prasarpati।  
uddhṛtya pārthivacchāyāṃ nirmito maṇḍalākṛtiḥ ।। 53.63 ।।  
svarbhānostu bṛhat sthānannirmitaṃ yattamomayam।  
ādityāttacca niṣkramya somaṃ gacchati parvasu ।। 53.64 ।।  
ādityameti somācca punaḥ somañca parvasu।  
svarbhāsānudate yasmāttataḥ svarbhānurucyate ।। 53.65 ।।  
candrasya ṣoḍaśo bhāgo bhārgavaśca nidhīyate।  
viṣkambhānmaṇḍalāccaiva yojanāgrāt pramāṇataḥ ।। 53.66 ।।  
bhārgavātpādahīnastu vijñeyo vai bṛhaspatiḥ।  
buhaspateḥ pādahīnau kujasaurāvubhau smṛtau ।  
vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva pādahīnastayorbudhaḥ ।। 53.67 ।।  
tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi svapuṣmantīha yāni vai।  
budhena samatulyāni vistārānmaṇḍalādatha ।। 53.68 ।।  
prāyaśaścandrayogāni vidyādṛkṣāṇi tattvavit।  
tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparam ।। 53.69 ।।  
śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve caiva yojane।  
pūrvāparanikṛṣṭāni tārakāmaṇḍalāni tu।  
yojanānyarddhamātrāṇi tebhyo hrasvaṃ na vidyate ।। 53.70 ।।  
upariṣṭātrayasteṣāṃ grahā ye dūrasarpiṇaḥ।  
sauro'ṅgirāśca vakraśca jñeyā mandavicāriṇaḥ ।। 53.71 ।।  
tebhyo'dhastāttu catvāraḥ punaranye mahāgrahāḥ।  
sūryaḥ somo budhaścaiva bhārgavaścaiva śīghragāḥ ।। 53.72 ।।  
yāvantya stārakāḥ koṭyastāvadṛkṣāṇi sarvaśaḥ।  
vīthīnāṃ niyamāccaivamṛkṣamārgo vyavasthitaḥ ।। 53.73 ।।  
gatistāstveva sūryasya nīcoccatve'yanakramāt।  
uttarāyaṇa mārgastho yadā parvasu candramāḥ।  
baudhaṃ baudho'tha svarbhānuḥ svarbhānoḥ sthānamāsthitaḥ ।। 53.74 ।।  
nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nakṣatrāṇi viśantyuta।  
gṛhāṇye tāni sarvāṇi jyotīṃṣi sukṛtātmanām ।। 53.75 ।।  
kalpādau saṃpravṛttāni nirmitāni svayambhuvā।  
sthānānyetāni tiṣṭhanti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। 53.76 ।।  
manvantareṣu sarveṣu devatāyatanāni vai।  
abhimānino'vatiṣṭanti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। 53.77 ।।  
atītaistu sahātītā bhāvyābhāvyaiḥ surāsuraiḥ ।  
varttante varttamānaiśca sthānāni svaiḥ suraiḥ saha ।। 53.78 ।।  
asmin manvantare caiva grahā vaimānikāḥ smṛtāḥ।  
vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vaivasvate'ntare ।। 53.79 ।।  
tviṣimāndharmaputrastu somadevo vasuḥ smṛtaḥ।  
śukro devastu vijñeyo bhārgavo'surarājakaḥ ।। 53.80 ।।  
bṛhattejāḥ smṛto devo devācāryo'ṅgiraḥsutaḥ।  
budho manoharaścaiva tviṣiputrastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। 53.81 ।।  
agnirvikalpāt saṃjajñe yuvā'sau lohitādhipaḥ।  
nakṣatrṛkṣagāminyo dākṣāyaṇyaḥ smṛtāstu tāḥ ।। 53.82 ।।  
svarbhānuḥ siṃhikāputro bhūtasantāpano'suraḥ।  
somarkṣagrahasūrye tu kīrtitāstvabhimāninaḥ ।। 53.83 ।।  
sthānānyetānyathoktāni sthāninyaścaiva devatāḥ।  
śuklamagnimayaṃ sthānaṃ sahasrāṃśorvivasvataḥ ।। 53.84 ।।  
sahasrāṃśostviṣaḥ sthānamammayaṃ śuklameva ca।  
atha śyāmaṃ manojñasya pañcaraśmergṛhaṃ smṛtam ।। 53.85 ।।  
śukrasyāpyammayaṃ sthānaṃ sadma ṣoḍaśaraśmivat।  
navaraśmestu yūno hi lohitasthānamammayam ।। 53.86 ।।  
hariścāpyaṃ bṛhaccāpi dvādaśāṃśorbṛhaspateḥ।  
aṣṭa raśmergṛhaṃ proktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ buddhasya ammayam ।। 53.87 ।।  
svarbhānostāmasaṃ sthānaṃ bhūtasantāpanālayam।  
vijñeyāstārakāḥ sarvāstvammayāstvekaraśmayaḥ ।। 53.88 ।।  
āśrayāḥ puṇyakīrtīnāṃ suśuklāścaiva varṇataḥ।  
ghanatoyātmikā jñeyāḥ kalpādau vedanirmitāḥ ।। 53.89 ।।  
uccatvāddṛśyate śīghramabhivyaktairgabhastibhiḥ।  
tathā dakṣiṇamārgastho nīvivīthīsamākṣitaḥ ।। 53.90 ।।  
bhūmilekhāvṛtaḥ sūryaḥ pūrṇāmāvāsyayostathā।  
nadṛśyate yathākālaṃ śāghrato'stamupaiti ca ।। 53.91 ।।  
tasmāduttaramārgastho hyamāvāsyāṃ niśākaraḥ।  
dṛśyate dakṣiṇe mārge niyamāddṛśyate na ca ।। 53.92 ।।  
jyotiṣāṃ gatiyogena sūryācandramasāvubhau।  
samānakālāstamayau viṣuvatsu samodayau ।। 53.93 ।।  
uttarāsu ca vīthīṣu vyantarāstamayodayau।  
pūrṇāmāvāsyayorjñeyau jyotiścakrānuvarttinau ।। 53.94 ।।  
dakṣiṇāyanamārgastho yadā bhavati raśmivān।  
tadā sarvagrahāṇāṃ sa sūryo'dhastāt prasarpati ।। 53.95 ।।  
vistīrṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā tasyorddhvañcarate śaśī।  
nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ somādūrddhvaṃ prasarpati ।। 53.96 ।।  
nakṣatrebhyo budhaśvorddhvaṃ budhādūrddhvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ।  
tasmācchanaiścaraścorddhvaṃ tasmātsaptarṣimaṇḍalam ।  
ṛṣīṇāñcaiva saptānāṃ dhruva ūrddhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ ।। 53.97 ।।  
dviguṇeṣu sahasreṣu yojanānāṃ śateṣu ca।  
tārāgrahāntarāṇi syurupariṣṭādyathākramam ।। 53.98 ।।  
grahāśca candrasūryau tu divi divyena tejasā।  
nityamṛkṣeṣu yujyanti gacchanti niyamakramāt ।। 53.99 ।।  
grahanakṣatrasūryāstu nīcoccamṛdvavasthitāḥ।  
samāgame ca bhede ca paśyanti yugapat prajāḥ ।। 53.100 ।।  
parasparasthitāḥ hyete yujyante ca parasparam।  
asaṅkareṇa vijñeyasteṣāṃ yogastu vai budhaiḥ ।। 53.101 ।।  
ityeṣa sanniveśo vaḥ pṛthivyāṃ jyautiṣasya ca।  
dvīpānāmudnadhīnāṃ ca parvatānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। 53.102 ।।  
varṣāṇāṃ ca nadīnāñca yeṣu teṣu vasanti vai।  
ete caiva grahāḥ pūrvaṃ nakṣatreṣu samutthitāḥ ।। 53.103 ।।  
vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vai cākṣuṣe'ntare।  
viśākhāsu samutpanno grahāṇāṃ prathamo grahaḥ ।। 53.104 ।।  
tviṣimān dharmmaputrastu somo viśvāvasustathā।  
śītaraśmiḥ samutpannaḥ kṛttikāsu niśākaraḥ ।। 53.105 ।।  
ṣoḍaśārcirbhṛgoḥ putraḥ śukraḥ sūryādanantaram।  
tārāgrahāṇāṃ pravarastiṣyakṣetre samutthitaḥ ।। 53.106 ।।  
grahaścāṅgirasaḥ putro dvādaśārccirbṛhaspatiḥ।  
phālgunīṣu samutpannaḥ sarvāsu ca jagadguruḥ ।। 53.107 ।।  
navārcirlohitāṅgastu prajāpatisuto grahaḥ ।  
āṣāḍhāsviha pūrvāsu samutpanna iti śrutiḥ ।। 53.108 ।।  
revatīṣveva saptārci stathā sauraśanaiścaraḥ।  
rohiṇīṣu samutpannau grahau candrārkamarddanau ।। 53.109 ।।  
ete tārāgrahāścaiva boddhavyā bhārgavādaya।  
janmanakṣatrapīḍāsu yānti vaiguṇyatāṃ yataḥ।  
spṛśante tena doṣeṇa tatastā grahabhaktiṣu ।। 53.110 ।।  
sarvagrahāṇāmeteṣāmādirāditya ucyate।  
tārāgrahāṇāṃ śukrastu ketūnāñcaiva dhūmavān ।। 53.111 ।।  
dhruvaḥ kālo grahāṇāṃ tu vibhaktānāṃ caturdiśam ।  
nakṣatrāṇāṃ śraviṣṭā syādayanānāṃ tathottaram ।। 53.112 ।।  
varṣāṇāñcāpi pañcānāmādyaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ।  
ṛtūnāṃ śiśirañcāpi māsānāṃ māgha eva ca ।। 53.113 ।।  
pakṣāṇāṃ śuklapakṣastu tithīnāṃ pratipattathā।  
ahorātravibhāgānāmahaścāpi prakīrtitam ।। 53.114 ।।  
muhūrttānāṃ tathaivādirmuhūrtto rudradaivataḥ।  
akṣṇoścāpi nimeṣādiḥ kālaḥ kālavido mataḥ ।। 53.115 ।।  
śravaṇāntaṃ śraviṣṭādiyugaṃ syāt pañcavārṣikam।  
bhānorgativiśeṣeṇa cakravat parivarttate ।। 53.116 ।।  
divākaraḥ smṛtastasmātkālastaṃ viddhi ceśvaram।  
caturvanidhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ pravarttakanivarttakaḥ ।। 53.117 ।।  
ityeṣa jyotiṣāmeva sanniveśo'rthaniścayāt।  
lokasaṃvyavahārārthamīśvareṇa vinirmitaḥ ।। 53.118 ।।  
utpannaḥ śravaṇenāsau saṃkṣiptaśca dhruve tathā।  
sarvato'nteṣu vistīrṇo vṛkṣākāra iti sthitiḥ ।। 53.119 ।।  
buddhipūrvambhagavatā kalpādau saṃprakīrtitaḥ।  
sāśrayaḥ so'bhimānī ca sarvasya jyotirātmakaḥ।  
viśvarūpaḥ pradhānasya pariṇāmo'yamadbhutaḥ ।। 53.120 ।।  
naiva śakyaṃ prasaṃkhyātuṃ yāthātathyena kenacit।  
gatāgataṃ manuṣyeṣu jyotiṣāṃ māṃsacakṣuṣā ।। 53.121 ।।  
āgamādanumānācca pratyakṣādupapattitaḥ।  
parīkṣya nipuṇaṃ bhaktyā śraddhātavyaṃ vipaścitā ।। 53.122 ।।  
cakṣuḥ śāstraṃ jalaṃ lekhyaṃ gaṇitaṃ buddhisattamāḥ।  
pañcaite hetavo jñeyā jyotirgaṇavicintane ।। 53.123 ।।  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte jyotiḥsanniveśo nāma tripañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 53 ।।


---
title: 054

---
।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
kasmin deśe mahāpuṇyametadākhyānamuttamam।  
vṛttaṃ brahmapurogāṇāṃ kasmin kāle mahādyute।  
etadākhyāhi naḥ samyag yathā vṛttaṃ tapodhana ।। 54.1 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca।।  
yathā śrutaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ vāyunā jagadāyunā।  
kathyamānaṃ dvijaśreṣṭāḥ satre varṣasahasrake ।। 54.2 ।।  
  
nīlatā yena kaṇṭhasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ।  
tadahaṃ kīrttayiṣyāmi śrṛṇudhvaṃ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।। 54.3 ।।  
  
uttare śailarājasya sarāṃsi sarito hradāḥ।  
puṇyodyāneṣu tīrtheṣu devatāyataneṣu ca।  
giriśrṛṅgeṣu tuṅgeṣu gahvaropavaneṣu ca ।। 54.4 ।।  
  
devabhaktā mahātmāno munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ।  
stuvanti ca mahādevaṃ yatra yathāvidhi ।। 54.5 ।।  
  
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedaiśca nṛtyagītārccanādibhiḥ।  
oṅkāreṇa namaskārairarccayanti sadā śivam ।। 54.6 ।।  
  
pravṛtte jyotiṣāṃ cakre madhyavyāpte divākare।  
devatā niyatātmānaḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti tāṃ kathām ।  
atha niyamapravṛttāśca prāṇaśeṣavyavasthitāḥ ।। 54.7 ।।  
  
namaste nīlakaṇṭāya ityuvāca sadāgatiḥ।  
tacchutvā bhāvitātmāno munayaḥ śaṃśitavratāḥ।  
vālakhilyeti vikhyātāḥ pataṅgasahacāriṇaḥ ।। 54.8 ।।  
  
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munīnāmūrddhvaretasām।  
tasmāt pṛcchanti vai vāyuṃ vāyuparṇāmbubhojanāḥ ।। 54.9 ।।  
  
।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
nīlakaṇṭeti yat proktaṃ tvayā pavanasattama।  
etadduhyaṃ pavitrāṇāṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛtāṃ varāḥ ।। 54.10 ।।  
  
tadvayaṃ śrotumicchāmastvatprasādātprabhañjana।  
nīlatā yena kaṇṭhasya kāraṇenāmbikāpateḥ ।। 54.11 ।।  
  
śrotumicchā mahe samyak tava vakrādviśeṣataḥ।  
yāvadvācaḥ pravarttante sārthāstāśca tvayeritāḥ ।। 54.12 ।।  
  
varṇasthānagate vāyau vāgvidhiḥ saṃpravartate।  
jñānaṃ pūrvamathotsāha stvatto vāyo pravartate ।। 54.13 .  
tvayi niṣpandamāne tu śeṣā varṇapravṛttayaḥ।  
yatra vāco nivartante dehabandhāśca durlabhāḥ ।। 54.14 ।।  
  
tatrāpi te'sti sadbhāvaḥ sarvagastvaṃ sadānila।  
nānyaḥ sarvagato devastvadṛteśasti samīraṇa ।। 54.15 ।।  
  
eṣa vai jīvalokaste pratyakṣaḥ sarvato'nila।  
vettha vācaspatiṃ devaṃ manonāyakamīsvaram ।। 54.16 ।।  
  
brūhi tatkaṇṭhadeśasya kiṃ kṛtā rūpavikriyā।  
śrutvā vākyantatasteṣāmṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmānām।  
pratyuvāca mahātejā vāyurloka namaskṛtaḥ ।। 54.17 ।।  
  
।।vāyuruvāca।।  
purā kṛtayuge vipro vedanirṇayatatparaḥ।  
vasiṣṭo nāma dharmātmā mānaso vai prajāpateḥ ।। 54.18 ।।  
  
prapaccha kārtikeyaṃ vai mayūravaravāhanam।  
mahiṣāsuranārīṇāṃ nayanāñjanataskaram ।। 54.19 ।।  
  
mahāsenaṃ mahātmānaṃ meghastanitaniḥsvanam।  
umāmanaḥpraharṣeṇa bālakaṃ chajharūpiṇam ।। 54.20 ।।  
  
krauñcajīvitaharttāraṃ pārvatīhṛdi nandanam।  
vasiṣṭhaḥ pṛcchate bhaktyā kārtikeyaṃ mahābalam ।। 54.21 ।।  
  
।।vasiṣṭha uvāca।।  
namaste haranandāya umāgarbha namo 'stu te।  
namaste agnigarbhāya gaṅgāgarbha namo'stu te ।। 54.22 ।।  
  
namaste śaragarbhāya namaste kṛttikāsuta।  
namo dvādaśanetrāya ṣaṇmukhāya namo'stu te ।। 54.23 ।।  
  
namaste śaktihastāya divyaghaṇṭāpatākine।  
evaṃ stutvā mahāsenaṃ papraccha śikhivāhanam ।। 54.24 ।।  
  
yadetaddṛśyate varṇaṃ śubhaṃ śubhrāñjanaprabham।  
tatkimarthaṃ samutpannaṃ kaṇṭe kundendusaṃprabhe ।। 54.25 ।।  
  
etadāptāya bhaktāya dāntāya brūhi pṛcchate।  
kathāṃ maṅgalasaṃyuktāṃ pavitrāṃ pāpanāśinīm ।  
matpriyārthaṃ mahābhāga vaktumarhasyaśeṣataḥ ।। 54.26 ।।  
  
śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasya vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ।  
pratyuvāca mahātejāḥ surāribalasūdanaḥ ।। 54.27 ।।  
  
śrṛṇuṣva vadatāṃ śreṣṭha kathyamānaṃ vaco mama।  
umotsaṅganiviṣṭena mayā pūrvaṃ yathāśrutam ।। 54.28 ।।  
  
pārvatyā saha saṃvādaḥ śarvasya ca mahātmanaḥ।  
tadahaṅkīrttayiṣyāmi tvatpriyārthaṃ mahāmune ।। 54.29 ।।  
  
kailāsaśikhare ramye nānādhātuvicitrite।  
nānādrumalatākīrṇe cakravākopaśobhite ।। 54.30 ।।  
  
ṣaṭ‌padodgītabahule dhārāsampātanādite।  
mattakrauñcamayūrāṇāṃ nādairudghuṣṭakandare ।। 54.31 ।।  
  
apsarogaṇasaṅkīrṇe kinnaraiścopaśobhite ।  
jīvañjīvakajātīnāṃ vīrudbhirupaśobhite ।। 54.32 ।।  
  
kokilārāvamadhure siddha cāraṇasevite।  
saurabhaiyīninādāḍhye adhastanitaniḥsvane ।। 54.33 ।।  
  
vināyakabhayodvigne kuñjarairyuktakandare।  
vīṇāvāditranirghoṣaiḥ śrotrendriyamanoramaiḥ ।। 54.34 ।।  
  
dolālambitasampāte vanitāsaṅghasevite।  
dhvajairlambitadolānāṃ ghaṇṭānāṃ ninadākule ।। 54.35 ।।  
  
mukhamardalavāditrairbalināṃ sphoṭitaistathā।  
krīḍāravavicārāṇāṃ nirghoṣaiḥ pūrṇamandire ।। 54.36 ।।  
  
hāsaiḥ santrāsajananairvikarālamukhaistathā।  
dehagandhairvicitraiśca prakrīḍitagaṇeścaraiḥ ।। 54.37 ।।  
  
vajrasphaṭikasopāna citrapaṭṭiśilātalaiḥ।  
vyādhrasiṃhamukhaiśacavānyairgajavājimukhaistathā ।। 54.38 ।।  
  
biḍālavadanaiścograiḥ kroṣṭukākāramūrtibhiḥ ।  
hrasvairdīrghaiḥ kṛśaiḥ sthūlairlambodara mahodaraiḥ ।। 54.39 ।।  
  
hrasvajaṅghaiśca lamboṣṭaistālajaṅghaistathāparaiḥ।  
gaukarṇairekakarṇaiśca mahākarṇairakarṇakaiḥ ।। 54.40 ।।  
  
bahupādairmahāpādairekapādairapādakaiḥ।  
bahuśīrṣairmahāśīrṣairekaśīrṣairaśīrṣakaiḥ ।। 54.41 ।।  
  
bahunetrairmahānetrairekanaitrairanaitrakaiḥ ।  
evaṃvidhairmahāyogibhūtairbhūtapatirvṛtaḥ ।। 54.42 ।।  
  
viśuddhamuktāmaṇiratnabhūṣite śilātale hemamaye manorame।  
sukhopaviṣṭaṃ madanāṅganāśanaṃ provāca vākyaṃ girirājaputrī ।। 54.43 ।।  
  
।।devyuvāca।।  
bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa govṛṣāṅkitaśāsana।  
tava kaṇṭe mahādeva bhrājate'mbudaśannibham ।। 54.44 ।।  
  
nātyulbaṇaṃ nātiśubraṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam।  
kimidaṃ dīpyate deva kaṇṭe kāmāṅga nāśana ।। 54.45 ।।  
  
ko hetuḥ kāraṇaṃ kiñca kaṇṭe nīlatvamīśvaraḥ ।  
etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ brūhi kautūhalaṃ hime ।। 54.46 ।।  
  
śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ pārvatīpriyaḥ ।  
kathāṃ maṅgalasaṃyuktāṃ kathayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ ।। 54.47 ।।  
  
mathyamāne'mṛte pūrvaṃ kṣīrode suradānavaiḥ।  
agre samutthitaṃ tasmin viṣaṃ kālānalaprabham ।। 54.48 ।।  
  
taṃ dṛṣṭvā surasaṅghāśca daityāścaiva varānane।  
viṣaṇṇavadanāḥ sarve gatāste brahmaṇo'ntikam ।। 54.49 ।।  
  
dṛṣṭvā suragaṇān bhītān brahmo vāca mahādyutiḥ।  
kimarthaṃ bho mahābhāgā bhītā udvignacetasaḥ ।। 54.50 ।।  
  
mayāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ bhavatāṃ samprakalpitam।  
kena vyāvarttitaiśvaryā yūyaṃ vai surasattamāḥ ।। 54.51 ।।  
  
trailokyasyeśvarā yūyaṃ sarve vai vigatajvarāḥ।  
prajāsarge na so'stīha ājñāṃ yo me nivarttayet ।। 54.52 ।।  
  
vimānagāminaḥ sarve sarve svacchandagāminaḥ।  
adhyātme cādhibhūte ca adhidaive ca nityaśaḥ।  
prajāḥ karmavipākena śaktā yūyaṃ pravarttitum ।। 54.53 ।।  
  
tatkimarthaṃ bhayodvignā mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā iva।  
kiṃ duḥkhaṃ kena santāpaḥ kulo vā bhayamāgatam।  
etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ śīgramākhyātumarhatha ।। 54.54 ।।  
  
śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasya brahmaṇo vai mahātmanaḥ।  
ūcuste ṛṣibhiḥ sārdhdhaṃ suradaityendradānavāḥ ।। 54.55 ।।  
  
surāsurairmathyamāne pāthodhau ca mahātmabhiḥ।  
bhujaṅgabhṛṅgasaṅkāśaṃ nīlajīmūtasannibham।  
prādurbhūtaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ saṃvartāgnisamaprabham ।। 54.56 ।।  
  
kālamṛtyurivodbhūtaṃ yugāntādityavarcasam।  
trailokyotsādi sūryābhaṃ prasphurantaṃ samantataḥ ।। 54.57 ।।  
  
viṣeṇottiṣṭhamānena kālānalasamatviṣā।  
nirdagdho raktagaurāṅgaḥ kṛtakṛṣṇo janārdanaḥ ।। 54.58 ।।  
  
dṛṣṭvā taṃ raktagaurāṅgaṃ kṛtakṛṣṇaṃ janārdanam।  
bhītāḥ sarve vayaṃ devāstvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। 54.59 ।।  
  
surāṇāmasurāṇāñca śrutvā vākyaṃ pitāmahaḥ।  
pratyuvāca mahātejā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। 54.60 ।।  
  
śrṛṇudhvaṃ devatāḥ sarve ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ।  
yattadagre samutpannaṃ mathyamāne mahodadhau ।। 54.61 ।।  
  
viṣaṃ kālānalaprakhyaṃ kālakūṭeti viśrutam।  
yena prodbhūtamātreṇa kṛtakṛṣṇo janārdanaḥ ।। 54.62 ।।  
  
tasya viṣṇurahañcāpi sarve te surapuṅgavāḥ।  
na śaknuvanti vai soḍhuṃ vegamanye tu śaṅkarāt ।। 54.63 ।।  
  
ityuktvā pajhagarbhābhaḥ pajhayonirayonijaḥ ।  
tataḥ stotuṃ samārabdho brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। 54.64 ।।  
  
namastubhyaṃ virūpākṣa namaste'nekacakṣuṣe।  
namaḥ pinākahastāya vajrahastāya vai namaḥ ।। 54.65 ।।  
  
namastrailokyanāthāya bhūtānāmpataye namaḥ।  
namaḥ surārisaṃhartre tāpasāya tricakṣuṣe ।। 54.66 ।।  
  
brahamaṇe caiva rudrāya viṣṇave caiva te namaḥ।  
sāṅkhyāya caiva yogāya bhūtagrāmāya vai namaḥ ।। 54.67 ।।  
  
manmatāṅgavināśāya kālakālāya vai namaḥ।  
rudrāya ca sureśāya devadevāya te namaḥ। 54.68।  
kapardine karālāya śaṅkarāya kapāline।  
virūpāyaikarūpāya śivāya varadāya ca ।। 54.69 ।।  
  
tripuraghnāya vandyāya mātṝṇāmpataye namaḥ।  
buddhāya caiva śuddhāya muktāya kevalāya ca ।। 54.70 ।।  
  
namaḥ kamalahastāya digvāsāya śikhaṇḍine ।  
loka trayavalidhātre ca candrāya varuṇāya ca ।। 54.71 ।।  
  
agrāya caiva cogrāya viprāyānekacakṣuṣe।  
rajase caiva sattvāya tamase'vyaktayonaye ।। 54.72 ।।  
  
nityāyānityarūpāya nityānityāya vai namaḥ।  
vyaktāya caivāvyaktāya vyaktāvyaktāya vai namaḥ ।। 54.73 ।।  
  
cintyāya caivācintyāya cintyācintyāya vai namaḥ।  
bhaktānāmārtināśāya naranārāyaṇāya ca ।। 54.74 ।।  
  
umāpriyāya śarvāya nandicakrāṅkitāya ca।  
pakṣamāsārddhamāsāya namaḥ saṃvatsarāya ca ।। 54.75 ।।  
  
bahurūpāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine'tha varūthine।  
namaḥ kapālahastāya digvāsāya śikhaṇiḍane ।। 54.76 ।।  
  
dhvajine rathine caiva yamine brahmacāriṇe।  
ṛgyajuḥ sāmavedāya puruṣāyeśvarāya ca।  
ityevamādicaritaistubhyaṃ deva namo'stu te ।। 54.77 ।।  
  
।।śrīmahādeva uvāca।।  
evaṃ stutastato devaiḥ praṇipatya varānane ।। 54.78 ।।  
  
jñātvā tu bhaktiṃ mama devadevo gaṅgājalāplāvitakeśadeśaḥ।  
sūkṣmo'tiyogātiśayādacintyo na hi pluto vyaktamupaiti candraḥ ।। 54.79 ।।  
  
evaṃ bhagavatā pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā।  
stuto'haṃ vividhaiḥ stotrai rvedavedāṅgasambhavaiḥ ।। 54.80 ।।  
  
tataḥ prīto hyahaṃ tasmai brahmaṇe sumahātmane।  
tato'haṃ sūkṣmayā vācā pitāmahamathābruvam ।। 54.81 ।।  
  
bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa lokanātha jagatpate।  
kiṃ kārye te mayā brahman karttavyaṃ vada suvrata ।। 54.82 ।।  
  
śrutvā vākyaṃ tato brahmā pratyuvācāmbujekṣaṇaḥ ।  
bhūtabhavyabhavannātha śrūyatāṃ kāraṇeśvara ।। 54.83 ।।  
  
surāsurairmathyamāne payodhāvambujekṣaṇa।  
bhagavanmegha saṅkāśaṃ nīlajīmūtasannibham ।। 54.84 ।।  
  
prādurbhūtaṃ viṣaṅghoraṃ saṃvarttāgnisamaprabham।  
kālamṛtyurivodbhūtaṃ yugāntādityavarccasam ।। 54.85 ।।  
  
trailokyotsādi sūryābhaṃ visphurantaṃ samantataḥ।  
agre samutthitaṃ tasmin viṣaṅkālānalaprabham ।। 54.86 ।।  
  
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tuṃ vayaṃ sarve bhītāḥ sambhrāntacetasaḥ।  
tat pibasva mahādeva lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।  
bhavānagryasya bhoktā vai bhavāṃśvaiva varaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 54.87 ।।  
  
tvāmṛte'nyo mahādeva viṣaṃ soḍhuṃ na vidyate ।  
nāsti kaścit pumān śaktastrailokyeṣu ca gīyate ।। 54.88 ।।  
  
evaṃ tasya vacaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭinaḥ।  
bāḍhamityeva tadvākyaṃ pratigṛhya varānane ।। 54.89 ।।  
  
tato'haṃ pātumārabdho viṣamantakasannibham।  
pibato me mahāghoraṃ viṣaṃ surabhayaṅkaram।  
kaṇṭhaḥ samabhavattūrṇaṃ kṛṣṇo me varavarṇini ।। 54.90 ।।  
  
taṃdṛṣṭvo tpalapatrābhaṃ kaṇṭe saktamivoragam ।  
takṣakaṃ nāgarājānaṃ lelihānamiva sthitam ।। 54.91 ।।  
  
athovāca mahātejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।  
śobhase tvaṃ mahādeva kaṇṭenānena suvrata ।। 54.92 ।।  
  
tatastasya vacaḥ śrutvā mayā girivarātmaje।  
paśyatāṃ devasaṅgānāṃ daityānāñca varānane ।। 54.93 ।।  
  
yakṣagandharvabhūtānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām।  
dhṛtaṃ kaṇṭe viṣaṃ ghoraṃ nīlakaṇṭastato hyaham ।। 54.94 ।।  
  
tat kālakūṭaṃ viṣamugratejaḥ kaṇṭe mayā parvatarājaputri।  
niveśyamānaṃ suradaityasaṅgho dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayamājagāma ।। 54.95 ।।  
  
tataḥ suragaṇāḥ sarve sadaityoragarākṣasāḥ।  
ūcuḥ prāñcalayo bhūtvā mattamātaṅgagāmini ।। 54.96 ।।  
  
aho balaṃ vīryaparākramaste aho punaryogabalaṃ tavaiva।  
aho prabhutvaṃ tava devadeva gaṅgājalāsphālitamuktakeśa ।। 54.97 ।।  
  
tvameva viṣṇuścaturānanastvaṃ tvameva mṛtyu rvaradastvameva।  
tvameva sūryo rajanīkaraśca tvameva bhūmiḥ salilaṃ tvameva ।। 54.98 ।।  
  
tvameva yajño niyamastvameva tvameva bhūtaṃ bhavitā tvameva।  
tvameva cādi rnidhanaṃ tvameva sthūlaśca sūkṣmaḥ puruṣastvameva ।। 54.99 ।।  
  
tvameva sūkṣmasya parasya sūkṣmastvameva vahniḥ pavanastvameva।  
tvameva sarvasya carācarasya lokasya karttā pralaye ca goptā ।। 54.100 ।।  
  
itīdamuktvā vacanaṃ surendrāḥ pragṛhya somaṃ praṇipatya mūrdnā।  
gatā vimānairanigṛhya vegairmahātmano merumupetya sarve ।। 54.101 ।।  
  
ityetatparamaṃ guhyaṃ puṇyātpuṇyamahattaram।  
nīlakaṇṭeti yat proktaṃ vikhyātaṃ lokaviśrutam ।। 54.102 ।।  
  
svayaṃ svayambhuvā proktāṃ puṇyāṃ pāpapraṇāśanīm।  
yastu dhārayate nityamenāṃ brahmodbhavāṃ kathām।  
tasyāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi phalaṃ vai vipulaṃ mahat ।। 54.103 ।।  
  
viṣaṃ tasya varārohe sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamantathā।  
gātraṃ prāpya ca suśroṇi kṣipraṃ tat pratihanyate ।। 54.104 ।।  
  
śamayatyaśubhaṃ ghoraṃ duḥsvapnañcāpakarṣati।  
strīṣu vallabhatāṃ yāti sabhāyāṃ pārthivasya ca ।। 54.105 ।।  
  
vivāde jayamāpnoti yuddhe śūratvameva ca।  
gacchataḥ kṣemamadhvānaṃ gṛhe ca nityasampadaḥ ।। 54.106 ।।  
  
śarīrabhede vakṣyāmi gatiṃ tasya varānane।  
nīlakaṇṭo haricchamaśruḥ śaśāṅkāṅkitamūrddhajaḥ ।। 54.107 ।।  
  
tryakṣastriśūlapāṇiśca vṛṣayānaḥ pinākadhṛk।  
nandhitulyabalaḥ śrīmān nanditulyaparākramaḥ ।। 54.108 ।।  
  
vicaratyacirāt sarvān sarvalokānmamājñayā ।  
na hanyate gatistasya anilasya yathāmbare।  
mama tulyabalo bhūtvā tiṣṭhatyābhūtasamplavam ।। 54.109 ।।  
  
mama bhaktā varārohe ye ca śrṛṇvanti mānavāḥ।  
teṣāṃ gatiṃ pravakṣyāmi iha loke paratra ca ।। 54.110 ।।  
  
brāhmaṇo vedamāpnoti kṣatriyo jayate mahīm।  
vaiśyastu labhate lābhaṃ śūdraḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt ।। 54.111 ।।  
  
vyādhito mucyate rogādbaddho mucyeta bandhanāt।  
gurviṇī labhate putraṃ kanyā vindati satpatim।  
naṣṭañca labhate sarvamihaloke paratra ca ।। 54.112 ।।  
  
gavāṃ śatasahasrasya samyagdattasya yat phalam।  
tat phalaṃ bhavati śrutvā vibhordivyāmimāṃ kathām ।। 54.113 ।।  
  
pādaṃ vā yadi vāpyarddhaṃ ślokaṃ ślokārddhameva vā।  
yastu dhārayate nityaṃ rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। 54.114 ।।  
  
kathāmimāṃ puṇyaphalādiyuktāṃ nivedya devyāḥ śaśibaddha mūrddhajaḥ।  
vṛṣasya pṛṣṭena sahomayā prabhurjagāma kiṣkindhaguhāṃ guhapriyaḥ ।। 54.115 ।।  
  
krāntaṃ mayā pāpaharaṃ mahāpadaṃ nivedya tebhyaḥ pradadau prabhañjanaḥ।  
adhītya sarvaṃ tvakhilaṃ sulakṣaṇaṃ jagāma ādityapathaṃ dvijottamaḥ ।। 54.116 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyu prokte nīlakaṇṭhastavo nāma catuḥ pañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 54 ।


---
title: 055

---
।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
guṇakarmaprabhāvaiśca ko'dhiko vadatāṃ varaḥ।  
śrotumicchāmahe samyagāścaryaṃ guṇavistaram ।। 55.1 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca।।  
atrāpyudāharantīmamiti hāsaṃ purātanam ।  
mahādevasya māhātmyaṃ vibhutvañca mahātmanaḥ ।। 55.2 ।।  
  
pūrvaṃ trailokyavijaye viṣṇunā samudāhṛtam।  
baliṃ baddhvā mahaujāstu trailokyādhi patiḥ purā ।। 55.3 ।।  
  
praṇaṣṭeṣu ca daityeṣu prahṛṣṭe ca śacīpatau।  
athājagmuḥ prabhuṃ draṣṭuṃ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।। 55.4 ।।  
  
yatrāste viśvarūpātmā kṣīrodasya samī pataḥ।  
siddhabrahmarṣayo yakṣā gandharvāpsarasāṅgaṇāḥ ।। 55.5 ।।  
  
nāgā devarṣayaścaiva nadyaḥ sarve ca parvatāḥ।  
abhigamya mahātmānaṃ stuvanti puruṣaṃ harim ।। 55.6 ।।  
  
tvaṃ dhātā tvañca karttā'sya tvaṃ lokān sṛjasi prabho।  
tvatprasādācca kalyāṇaṃ prāptaṃ trailokyamavyayam।  
asurāśca jitāḥ sarve balirbaddhaśca vai tvayā ।। 55.7 ।।  
  
eva muktaḥ surairviṣṇuḥ siddhaiśca paramarṣibhiḥ।  
pratyuvāca tato devān sarvāṃstān puruṣottamaḥ ।। 55.8 ।।  
  
śrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi kāraṇaṃ surasattamāḥ।  
yaḥ sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ kālaḥ kālakaraḥ prabhuḥ ।। 55.9 ।।  
  
yena hi brahmaṇā sārddhaṃ sṛṣṭā lokāśca māyayā।  
tasyaiva ca prasādena ādau siddhatvamāgatam ।। 55.10 ।।  
  
purā tamasi cāvyakte trailokye grāsite mayā।  
udarastheṣu bhūteṣu loke'haṃ śayitastadā ।। 55.11 ।।  
  
sahasraśīrṣā bhūtvā ca sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt।  
śaṅkhacakragadā pāṇiḥ śayito vimale'mbhasi ।। 55.12 ।।  
  
etasminnantare dūrāt paśyāmi hyamitaprabham।  
śatasūryapratīkāśaṃ jvalantaṃ svena tejasā ।। 55.13 ।।  
  
caturvakraṃ mahā yogaṃ puruṣaṃ kāñcanaprabham।  
kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ devaṃ kamaṇḍaluvibhūṣitam।  
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa prāpto'sau puruṣottamaḥ ।। 55.14 ।।  
  
tato māmabravīdbrahmā sarvaloka namaskṛtaḥ।  
kastvaṃ kuto vā kiñceha tiṣṭhase vada me vibho ।। 55.15 ।।  
  
ahaṃ karttā'smi lokānāṃ svayambūrviśvatomukhaḥ।  
evamuktastadā dena brahmaṇāhamuvāca tam ।। 55.16 ।।  
  
ahaṃ karttā ca lokānāṃ saṃharttā ca punaḥ punaḥ।  
evaṃ sambhāṣamāṇābhyāṃ parasparajayaiṣiṇām।  
uttarāṃ diśamāsthāya jvālā dṛṣṭāpyadhiṣṭitā ।। 55.17 ।।  
  
jvālāntatastāmālokya vismittau ca tadānayoḥ ।  
tejasā caiva tenātha sarvaṃ jyotiḥkṛtaṃ jalam ।। 55.18 ।।  
  
varddhamāne tadā vahnāvatyantaparamādbhute।  
atidudrāva tāṃ jvālāṃ brahmā cāhañca satvaraḥ ।। 55.19 ।।  
  
divaṃ bhūmiñca viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhantaṃ jvālamaṇḍalam।  
tasya jvālasya madhye tu paśyāvo vipulaprabham ।। 55.20 ।।  
  
prādeśamātramavyaktaṃ liṅgaṃ paramadīpitam।  
na ca tatkāñcanaṃ madhye na śailaṃ na ca rājatam ।। 55.21 ।।  
  
anirddeśyamacintyañca lakṣyālakṣyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ।  
mahaujasaṃ mahāghoraṃ varddhamānaṃ bhṛśaṃ tadā।  
jvālāmālāyataṃ nyastaṃ sarvabhūtabhayaṅkaram ।। 55.22 ।।  
  
asya liṅgasya yo'ntaṃ vai gacchate mantrakāraṇam।  
ghora rūpiṇamatyarthaṃ bhindantamiva rodasī ।। 55.23 ।।  
  
tato māmabravīdbrahmā adho gaccha tvatandritaḥ।  
antamasya vijānīmo liṅgasya tu mahātmanaḥ ।। 55.24 ।।  
  
ahamūrddhvaṃ gamiṣyāmi yāvadanto'sya dṛśyate।  
tadā tau samayaṃ kṛtvā gatāvūrddhvamadhaśca ha ।। 55.25 ।।  
  
tato varṣasahasrantu ahaṃ punaradho gataḥ।  
na ca paśyāmi tasyāntaṃ bhītaścāhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। 55.26 ।।  
  
tathā brahmā ca śrāntaśca na cāntantasya paśyati।  
samāgato mayā sārddhaṃ tatraiva ca mahāmbhasi ।। 55.27 ।।  
  
tato vismayamāpannāvubhau tasya mahātmanaḥ ।।  
  
māyayā mohitau tena naṣṭasaṃjñau vyavasthitau ।। 55.28 ।।  
  
tato dhyānagatantatra īśvaraṃ sarvatomukham।  
prabhavaṃ nidhaऩñcaiva lokānāṃ prabhumavyayam ।। 55.29 ।।  
  
brahmāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā tasmai śarvāya śūline।  
mahābhairavanādāya bhīmarūpāya daṃṣṭriṇe।  
avyaktāya mahāntāya namaskāraṃ prakurmahe ।। 55.30 ।।  
  
namo'stu te lokasureśa deva namo'stu te bhūtapate mahāṃśca।  
namo'stu te śāśvata siddhayone namo'stu te sarvajagatpratiṣṭha ।। 55.31 ।।  
  
parameṣṭī paraṃ brahma akṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam।  
śreṣṭhastvaṃ vāmadevaśca rudraḥ skandaḥ śivaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 55.32 ।।  
  
tvaṃ yajñastvaṃ vaṣaṭ‌kārastvamoṅkāraḥ paraṃ padam।  
svāhākāro namaskāraḥ saṃskāraḥ sarvakarmaṇām ।। 55.33 ।।  
  
svadhākāraśca jāpyaśca vratāni niyamāstathā।  
vedā lokāśca devāśca bhagavāneva sarvaśaḥ ।। 55.34 ।।  
  
ākāśasya ca śabdastvaṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavāvyayam।  
bhūmergandho rasaśvāpāṃ tejorūpaṃ maheśvara ।। 55.35 ।।  
  
vāyoḥ ruparśaśca devaśca vapuścandramasastathā ।  
budho jñānañca deveśa prakṛtau bījameva ca ।। 55.36 ।।  
  
tvaṃ karttā sarvabhūtānāṃ kālo mṛtyuryamo'ntakaḥ।  
tvaṃ dhārayasi lokāstrīṃstvameva sṛjasi prabho ।। 55.37 ।।  
  
pūrveṇa vadanena tvamindratvañca prakāśase।  
dakṣiṇena ca vakreṇa lokān saṃkṣīyase prabho ।। 55.38 ।।  
  
paścimena tu vakreṇa varuṇatvaṃ karoṣi vai।  
uttareṇa tu vakreṇa saumyatvañca vyavasthitam ।। 55.39 ।।  
  
rājase bahudhā deva lokānāṃ prabhavāvyayaḥ।  
ādityā vasavo rudrā marutaścāśvinīsutau ।। 55.40 ।।  
  
sādhyā vidyādharā nāgāśvāraṇāśca tapodhanāḥ.  
vālakhilyā mahātmānastapaḥ siddhāśca suvratāḥ ।। 55.41 ।।  
  
tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśa ye cānye niyatavratāḥ।  
umā sītā sinī vālī kuhūrgāyatrireva ca ।। 55.42 ।।  
  
lakṣmīḥ kīrttirdhṛtirmedhā lajjā kṣāntirvapuḥ svadhā।  
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā caiva vācāṃ devī sarasvatī।  
tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśa sandhyā rātristathaiva ca ।। 55.43 ।।  
  
sūryāyutānāmayutaprabhā ca namo'stu te candrasahasragocara।  
namo'stu te parvatarūpadhāriṇe namo'stu te sarvaguṇākarāya ।। 55.44 ।।  
  
namo'stu te paṭṭiśarūpadhāriṇe namo'stu te carmavibhūtidhāriṇe ।  
namo'stu te rudrapinākapāṇaye namo'stu te sāyakacakradhāriṇe ।। 55.45 ।।  
  
namo'stu te bhasmavibhūṣitāṅga namo'stu te kāmaśarīranāśana।
