namo'stu te deva hiraṇyavāsase namo'stu te deva hiraṇyabāhave ।। 55.46 ।।  
  
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyarūpa namo'stu te deva hiraṇyanābha।  
namo'stu te netrasahasracitra namo'stu te deva hiraṇyaretaḥ ।। 55.47 ।।  
  
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyavarṇa namo'stu te deva hiraṇyagarbha।  
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyacīra namo'stu te deva hiraṇyadāyine ।। 55.48 ।।  
  
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyamāline namo'stu te deva hiraṇyavāhine।  
namo'stu te deva hiraṇyacīra namo'stu te bhairavanādanādine ।। 55.49 ।।  
  
namo'stu te bhairavavegavega namo'stu te śaṅkara nīlakaṇṭha।  
mano'stu te divyasahasrabāho namo'stu te narttanavādanapriya ।। 55.50 ।।  
  
evaṃ saṃstūyamānastu vyakto bhūtvā mahāmatiḥ।  
bhāti devo mahāyogī sūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ ।। 55.51 ।।  
  
abhibhāṣyastadā hṛṣṭo mahādevo maheśvaraḥ।  
vakrakoṭisahasreṇa grasamāna ivāparam ।। 55.52 ।।  
  
ekagrīvastvekajaṭo nānābhūṣaṇbhūṣitaḥ।  
nānācitravicitrāṅgo nānāmālyānulepanaḥ ।। 55.53 ।।  
  
pinākapāṇirbhagavān vṛṣabhāsanaśūladhṛk ।  
daṇḍakṛṣṇājinadharaḥ kapālī ghorarūpadhṛk ।। 55.54 ।।  
  
vyālayajñopavītī ca surāṇāmabhayaṅkaraḥ।  
dundubhisvananirghoṣaparjanyaninadopamaḥ।  
mukto hāsastadā tena nabhaḥ sarvamapūrayat ।। 55.55 ।।  
  
tena śabdena mahatā vayaṃ bhītā mahātmanaḥ।  
tadovāca mahāyogī prīto'haṃ surasattamau ।। 55.56 ।।  
  
paśyetāñca mahāmāyāṃ bhayaṃ sarvaṃ pramucyatām ।  
yuvāṃ prasūtau gātreṣu mama pūrvasanātanau ।। 55.57 ।।  
  
ayaṃ me dakṣiṇo bāhurbrahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।  
vāmo bāhuśca me viṣṇurnityaṃ yuddheṣu tiṣṭhati।  
prīto'haṃ yuvayoḥ samyagvaraṃ dajhi yathepsitam ।। 55.58 ।।  
  
tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasau praṇatau pādayoḥ punaḥ ।  
ūcatuśca mahātmānau punareva tadānaghau ।। 55.59 ।।  
  
yadi prītiḥ samutpannā yadi deyo varaśca nau।  
bhaktirbhavatu nau nityaṃ tvayi deva sureśvara ।। 55.60 ।।  
  
।।bhagavānuvāca।।  
evamastu mahābhāgau sṛjatāṃ vividhāḥ prajāḥ।  
evamuktvā sa bhagavāṃstatraivāntaradhīyata ।। 55.61 ।।  
  
evameṣa mayokto vaḥ prabhāvastasya yoginaḥ।  
tena sarvamidaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ hetumātrā vayantviha ।। 55.62 ।।  
  
etaddhi rūpamajñātamavyaktaṃ śivasaṃjñitam।  
acintyaṃ tadadṛśyañca paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣaḥ ।। 55.63 ।।  
  
tasmai devādhipatyāya namaskāraṃ prayuṅkta ha।  
yena sūkṣmamacintyañca paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣaḥ ।। 55.64 ।।  
  
mahādeva namaste'stu maheśvara namo'stu te।  
surāsuravara śreṣṭha manohaṃsa namo'stu te ।। 55.65 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca।।  
etacchrutvā gatāḥ sarve surāḥ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam।  
namaskāraṃ prayuñjānāḥ śaṅkarāya mahātmane ।। 55.66 ।।  
  
imaṃ stavaṃ paṭedyastu īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ।  
kāmāṃśca labhate sarvān pāpebhyastu vimucyate ।। 55.67 ।।  
  
etatsarvaṃ sadā tena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā।  
mahādevaprasādena uktaṃ brahma sanātanam।  
etadvaḥ sarvamākhyātaṃ mayā māheśvaraṃ balam ।। 55.68 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte liṅgodbhavastavo nāma pañcapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 55 ।


---
title: 056

---
।।śāṃśapāyana uvāca ।।  
agātkathamamāvāsyāṃ māsi māsi divaṃ nṛpaḥ।  
ailaḥ purūravāḥ sūta kathaṃ vā'tarpayat pitṝn ।। 56.1 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca।।  
tasya cāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi prabhāvaṃ śāṃśapāyana।  
ailasyādityasaṃyogaṃ somasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।। 56.2 ।।  
  
apāṃsāramayasyendoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ।  
hrāsavṛddhī pitṛmataḥ pakṣasya ca vinirṇayaḥ ।। 56.3 ।।  
  
somāccaivāmṛtaprāptiḥ pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ tathā।  
kavyāgneścāttasomānāṃ pitṝṇāñcaiva darśanam ।। 56.4 ।।  
  
yathā purūravāścaila tarpayāmāsa vai pitṝn।  
etatsarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi parvāṇi ca yathākramam ।। 56.5 ।।  
  
yadā tu candrasūryau tau nakṣatreṇa samāgatau।  
amāvāsyānnivasata ekarātraikamaṇḍale ।। 56.6 ।।  
  
sa gacchati tadā draṣṭuṃ divākaraniśākarau।  
amāvasyāmamāvāsyāṃ mātāmahapitāmahau।  
abhivādya tadā tatra kālāpekṣaḥ pratīkṣyate ।। 56.7 ।।  
  
prasīdamānāt somācca pitrarthaṃ tatparisravāt।  
ailaḥ purūravā vidvān māsi māsi prayatnataḥ।  
uvāste pitṛmantaṃ taṃ sasomaṃ sa divāsthitaḥ ।। 56.8 ।।  
  
dvilavaṃ kuhumātraṃ tu te ubhe tu vicārya saḥ।  
sinīvālīpramāṇena sinīvālīmupāsakaḥ ।। 56.9 ।।  
  
kuhūmātrāṃ kalāñcaiva jñātvopāste kuhuṃ punaḥ।  
sa tadā bhānumatyeka kālāvekṣī prapaśyati ।। 56.10 ।।  
  
sudhāmṛtaṃ kutaḥ somāt prasravenmāsatṛptaye।  
daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva sudhāmṛtaparisravaiḥ ।। 56.11 ।।  
  
kṛṣṇapakṣe tadā pītvā duhyamānaṃ tathāṃśubhiḥ।  
sadyaḥ pakṣaratā tena saumyena madhunā ca saḥ ।। 56.12 ।।  
  
nirvāpaṇārthaṃ dattena pitreṇa vidhinā nṛpaḥ।  
sudhāmṛtena rājendrastarpayāmāsa vai pitṝn।  
saumyā barhiṣadaḥ kāvyā agniṣvāttāstathaiva ca ।। 56.13 ।।  
  
ṛturagnistu yaḥ proktaḥ sa tu saṃvatsaro mataḥ।  
jajñire hyṛtavastasmādṛtubhyaścārttavāśca ye । 56.14 ।।  
  
ārttavā hyarddhamāsākhyāḥ pitaro hyabdasūnavaḥ।  
ṛtuḥ pitāmahā māsā ṛtuścaivābhdasūnavaḥ ।। 56.15 ।।  
  
prapitāmahāstu vai devāḥ pañcābdā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ।  
saumyāstu saumyajā jñeyāḥ kāvyā jñeyāḥ kaveḥ sutāḥ ।। 56.16 ।।  
  
upahūtāḥ smṛtāḥ devāḥ somajāḥ somapāstathā।  
ājyapāstu smṛtāḥ kāvyāstṛpyanti pitṛjātayaḥ ।। 56.17 ।।  
  
kāvyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāśca te tridhā।  
gṛhasthā ye ca yajvānā ṛturbarhiṣado dhruvam ।। 56.18 ।।  
  
gṛhasthāścāpi yajvānā agniṣvāttāstathārttavāḥ।  
aṣṭakāpatayaḥ kāvyāḥ pañcābdāstānnibodhata ।। 56.19 ।।  
  
eṣāṃ saṃvatsaro hyagniḥ sūryastu parivatsaraḥ।  
soma īdvatsaraḥ prokto vāyuścaivānuvatsaraḥ ।। 56.20 ।।  
  
rudrastu vatsarasteṣāṃ pañcābdā ye yugātmakāḥ।  
leśāśvaivoṣmapāścaiva divākīrtyāśca te smṛtāḥ ।। 56.21 ।।  
  
ete pibantyamāvāsyāṃ māsi māsi sudhāṃ divi ।  
tāṃstena tarpayāmāsa yāvadāsīt purūravāḥ ।। 56.22 ।।  
  
yasmāt prasravate somānmāsi māsi nibodhata।  
tasmāt sudhāmṛtaṃ dvai pitṝṇāṃ somapāyinām ।। 56.23 ।।  
  
evaṃ tadamṛtaṃ saumyaṃ sudhā ca madhu caiva ha ।  
kṛṣṇapakṣe yathā cendoḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa kramāt ।। 56.24 ।।  
  
pibantyambumayīrde vāstrayastriṃśattu chandajāḥ।  
pītvā ca māsaṃ gacchanti caturddaśyāṃ sudhāmṛtam ।। 56.25 ।।  
  
ityevaṃ pīyamānastu daivataiśca niśākaraḥ।  
samāgacchadamāvāsyāṃ bhāge pañcadaśe sthitaḥ ।। 56.26।  
suṣumnāpyāyitañcaiva amāvāsyāṃ yathākramam।  
pibanti dvikalaṃ kālaṃ pitaraste sudhāmṛtam ।। 56.27 ।।  
  
tataḥ pītakṣaye some sūryo'sāvekaraśminā।  
āpyāyayatsuṣumnena pitṝṇāṃ somapāyinām ।। 56.28 ।।  
  
niḥśeṣāyāṃ kalāyāntu somamāpyāyayat punaḥ।  
suṣumnāpyāyamānasya bhāgaṃ bhāga mahaḥkramāt।  
kalāḥ kṣīyanti tāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ śuklāścāpyāyayanti ca ।। 56.29 ।।  
  
evaṃ sūryasya vīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ।  
dṛśyate paurṇamāsyāṃ vai śuklaḥ sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ।  
saṃsiddhirevaṃ somasya pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ।। 56.30 ।।  
  
ityeṣa pitṛmān somaḥ smṛta idvatsaraḥ kramāt ।  
krāntaḥ paṃcadaśaiḥ sārddhaṃ sudhā mṛtaparisravaiḥ ।। 56.31 ।।  
  
ataḥ parvāṇi vakṣyāmi parvaṇāṃ sandhayastathā।  
granthimanti yathā parvāṇīkṣuveṇvorbhavantyuta ।। 56.32 ।।  
  
tathārddhamāsaparvāṇi śuklakṛṣṇāni vai viduḥ।  
pūrṇāmāvāsyayorbhedairgranthiryā sandhayaśca vai ।  
arddhamāsāstu parvāṇi tṛtīyāprabhṛtīni tu ।। 56.33 ।।  
  
agnayādhānakriyā yasmāt kriyate parvasandhiṣu।  
sāyāhne pratipaccaiva sa kālaḥ paurṇamāsikaḥ ।। 56.34 ।।  
  
vyatīpāte sthite sūrye lesorddhantu yugāntare।  
yugāntarodite caiva lekhorddhaṃ śaśinaḥ kramāt ।। 56.35 ।।  
  
paurṇamāse vyatīpāte yadīkṣete parasparam।  
yasminkāle sa sīmānte sa vyatīpāta eva tu ।। 56.36 ।।  
  
kālaṃ sūryasya nirddeśaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṅkhyā tu sarpati।  
sa vai pathaṃ kriyākālaḥ kālātsadyo vidhīyate ।। 56.37 ।।  
  
pūrṇendoḥ pūrṇapakṣe tu rātrisandhiṣu pūrṇimā।  
yasmāttāmanupaśyanti pitaro daivataiḥ saha।  
tasmādanumatirnāma pūrṇimā prathamā smṛtā ।। 56.38 ।।  
  
atyarthaṃ bhrājate yasmāt paurṇamāsyānniśākaraḥ।  
rañjanāccaiva candrasya rāketi kavayo viduḥ ।। 56.39 ।।  
  
amā vasetāmṛkṣe tu yadā candradivākarau।  
ekāṃ pañcadaśīṃ rātrimamāvāsyā tataḥ smṛtā ।। 56.40 ।।  
  
tato'parasya tairvyaktaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ niśākaraḥ।  
yadīkṣate vyatīpāte divā pūrṇe parasparam।  
candrārkāvaparāhne tu pūrṇātmānau tu pūrṇimā ।। 56.41 ।।  
  
vicchinnāṃ tāmamāvāsyāṃ paśyataśca samāgatau।  
anyonyaṃ candrasūryau tau yadā taddarśa ucyate ।। 56.42 ।।  
  
dvau dvau lavāvamāvāsyāṃ yaḥ kālaḥ parvasandhiṣu।  
dvākṣaraṃ kuhumātraṃ tu evaṃ kālastu sa smṛtaḥ।  
naṣṭacandrā pyamāvāsyā madhyasūryeṇa saṅgatā ।। 56.43 ।।  
  
divasārddhena rātryarddhaṃ sūryaṃ prāpya tu candramāḥ.  
sūryeṇa sahasā muktiṃ gatvā prātastanotsavau ।  
dvau kālau saṅgamaścaiva madhyāhne niṣpatedraviḥ ।। 56.44 ।।  
  
pratipacchuklapakṣasya candramāḥ sūryamaṇḍalāt।  
nirmucyamānayormadhye tayormaṇḍalayostu vai ।। 56.45 ।।  
  
sa tadā hyāhuteḥ kālo darśasya ca vaṣaṭkriyā।  
etadṛtumukhaṃ jñeyamamāvāsyāsya parvaṇaḥ ।। 56.46 ।।  
  
divā parvaṇyamāvāsyāṃ kṣīṇendau bahule tu vai।  
tasmāddivā hyamāvāsyāṃ gṛhyate'sau divākaraḥ।  
gṛhyate vai divā hyasmādamāvāsyāṃ divikṣayaiḥ ।। 56.47 ।।  
  
kalānāmapi vai tāsāṃ bahumānyājaḍātmakaiḥ।  
tithīnāṃ nāma dheyāni vidvadbhiḥ saṃjñitāni vai ।। 56.48 ।।  
  
darśayetāmathānyonyaṃ sūryācandramasāvubhau ।  
niṣkrāmatyatha tenaiva kramaśaḥ sūryamaṇḍalāt ।। 56.49 ।।  
  
dvilavena hyaho rātraṃ bhāskaraṃ spṛśate śaśī।  
sa tadā hyāhuteḥ kālo darśasya ca vaṣaṭ‌kriyā ।। 56.50 ।।  
  
kuheti kokirenokto yaḥ kālaḥ paricihnitaḥ।  
tatkālasaṃjñitā yasmādamāvāsyā kuhuḥ smṛtā ।। 56.51 ।।  
  
sinīvālīpramāṇena kṣīṇaśeṣo niśākaraḥ।  
amāvāsyāṃ viśatyarkaṃ sinīvālī tataḥ smṛtā ।। 56.52 ।।  
  
parvaṇaḥ parvakālastu tulyo vai tu vaṣaṭ‌kriyā।  
candrasūryavyatīpāte ubhe te pūrṇime smṛte ।। 56.53 ।।  
  
pratipatpañcadaśyośca parvakālo dvimātrakaḥ।  
kālaḥ kuhusinīvālyoḥ samudro dvilavaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 56.54 ।।  
  
arkāgnimaṇḍale some parvakālaḥ kalāśrayaḥ।  
evaṃ sa śukrapakṣo vai rajanyāḥ parvasandhiṣu ।। 56.55 ।।  
  
sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ śrīmāṃścandramā uparajyate।  
yasmādāpyāyate somaḥ pañcadaśyāntu pūrṇimā ।। 56.56 ।।  
  
daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva kalābhirdivasakramāt।  
tasmāt kalā pañcadaśī some nāsti tu ṣoḍaśī।  
tasmātsomasya bhavati pañcadaśyāṃ mahākṣayaḥ ।। 56.57 ।।  
  
ityete pitaro devāḥ somapāḥ somavarddhanāḥ।  
ārttavā ṛtavo yasmātte devā bhāvayanti ca ।। 56.58 ।।  
  
ataḥ pitṝn pravakṣyāmi māsaśrāddhabhujastu ye।  
teṣāṃ gatiñca sattvañca gatiṃ śrāddhasya caiva hi ।। 56.59 ।।  
  
na mṛtānāṃ gatiḥ śakyā vijñātuṃ punarāgatiḥ।  
tapasāpi prasiddhena kiṃ punarmāṃsacakṣuṣā ।। 56.60 ।।  
  
śrāddhadevān pidṝnetān pitaro laukikāḥ smṛtāḥ।  
devāḥ saumyāśca yajvānaḥ sarve caiva hyayonijāḥ ।। 56.61 ।।  
  
devāste pitaraḥ sarve devāstān bhāvayantyuta।  
manuṣyāḥ pitaraścaiva tebhyo'nye laukikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 56.62 ।।  
  
pitā pitāmahaścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ।  
yajvāno ye tu some na somavantastu te smṛtāḥ ।। 56.63 ।।  
  
ye yajvānaḥ smṛtāsteṣāṃ te vai barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ।  
karmasveteṣu yuktāste tṛpyantyādehasambhavāt ।। 56.64 ।।  
  
agniṣvāttāḥ smṛtāsteṣāṃ homino yājyayājinaḥ।  
ye vāpyāśramadharmeṇa prasthāneṣu vyavasthitāḥ ।। 56.65 ।।  
  
ante ca naiva sīdanti śraddhāyuktena karmaṇā।  
brahmacaryeṇa tapasā yajñena prajayā ca vai ।। 56.66 ।।  
  
śraddhayā vidyayā caiva pradānena ca saptadhā।  
karmasveteṣu ye yuktā bhavantyā devapātanāt ।। 56.67 ।।  
  
devaistaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ sārddhaṃ sūkṣmakaiḥ somapāyakaiḥ।  
svargatā divi modante pitṛmantamupāsate ।। 56.68 ।।  
  
prajāvatāṃ praśaṃsaiva smṛtā siddhā kriyāvatām।  
teṣāṃ nivāpadattānnaṃ tatkulīnaiśca bāndhavaiḥ ।। 56.69 ।।  
  
māsaṃ śrāddhabhujastṛpti labhante somalaukikāḥ।  
ete manuṣyāḥ pitaro māsi śrāddha bhujastu te ।। 56.70 ।।  
  
tebhyo'pare tu ye cānye saṅkīrṇāḥ karmayoniṣu।  
bhraṣṭāścāśramadharmebhyaḥ svadhāsvāhāvivarjitāḥ ।। 56.71 ।।  
  
bhinnadehā durātmanaḥ pretabhūtā yamakṣaye।  
svakarmāṇyeva śocanti yātanāsthānamāgatāḥ ।। 56.72 ।।  
  
dīrghāyuṣo'tiśuṣkāśca vivarṇāśca vivāsasaḥ।  
kṣutpipāsāparītāśca vidravanti itastataḥ ।। 56.73 ।।  
  
saritsarastaḍāgāni vāpiścaiva jalepsavaḥ।  
parānnāni ca lipsante kampamānāstatastataḥ ।। 56.74 ।।  
  
sthāneṣu pācyamānāśca yātāyāteṣu teṣu vai।  
śālmalau vaitaraṇyāñca kumbhīpākeṣu teṣu ca ।। 56.75 ।।  
  
karambhavālukāyāñca asipatravane tathā।  
śilāsampeṣaṇe caiva pātyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।। 56.76 ।।  
  
tatra sthānāni teṣāṃ vai duḥkhānāmapyanākavat।  
teṣāṃ lokāntarasthānāṃ vividhairnāmagotrataḥ ।। 56.77 ।।  
  
bhūmyāpasavyadarbheṣu dattvā piṇḍatrayantu vai।  
pati tāṃstarpayante ca pretasthāneṣvadhiṣṭitāḥ ।। 56.78 ।।  
  
aprāptā yātanāsthānaṃ sṛṣṭā ye bhuvi pañcadhā।  
paścādisthāvarānteṣu bhūtānāṃ teṣu karmasu ।। 56.79 ।।  
  
nānārūpāsu jātīṣu tiryagyoniṣu cātiṣu।  
yadāhārā bhavantyete tāsu tāsviha yoniṣu।  
tasmistasmiṃstadāhāraṃ śrāddhadattopatiṣṭhati ।। 56.80 ।।  
  
kāle nyāyāgataṃ pātraṃ vidhinā pratipāditam।  
prāpnotyannaṃ yathā dattaṃ bandhuryatrāvatiṣṭhate ।। 56.81 ।।  
  
yathā goṣu pranaṣṭāsu vatso vindati mātaram।  
tathā śrāddhe tadiṣṭānāṃ mantraḥ prāpayate pitṝn ।। 56.82 ।।  
  
evaṃ hyavikalaṃ śrāddhaṃ śrāddhadattantu mantrataḥ।  
sanatkumāraḥ provāca paśyan divyena cakṣuṣā।  
gatāgatijñaḥ pretānāṃ mantraḥ prāpayate pitṝn ।। 56.83 ।।  
  
bahvīkāsvoṣmapāścaiva divākīrtyāśca te smṛtāḥ।  
kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svaprāya śarvarī ।। 56.84 ।।  
  
itye te pitaro devā devāśca pitaraśca vai।  
ṛtārttavā aneke tu anyonyapitaraḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 56.85 ।।  
  
ete tu pitaro devā mānuṣāḥ pitaraśca ye।  
prīteṣu teṣu prīyante śraddhāyuktena karmaṇā ।। 56.86 ।।  
  
ityevaṃ pitaraḥ proktāḥ pidṝṇāṃ somapāyinām।  
etat pitṛmatatvaṃ hi purāṇe niścayo mataḥ ।। 56.87 ।।  
  
ityarkapitṛ somānāmailasya ca samāgamaḥ।  
sudhāmṛtasya cāvāptiḥ pitṝṇāñcaiva tarpaṇam ।। 56.88 ।।  
  
pūrṇimāvāsyayoḥ kālaḥ pitṝṇāṃ sthānameva ca।  
samāsātkīrttitastubhyameṣa sargaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। 56.89 ।।  
  
vaiśvarūpyantu sarvasya kathitañcaikadeśikam।  
na śakyaṃ parisaṅkhyātuṃ śraddheyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ।। 56.90 ।।  
  
svāyambhuvasya hītyeṣa sargaḥ krānto mayātra vai।  
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmyaham ।। 56.91 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pitṛvarṇanaṃ nāma ṣacpañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 56 ।


---
title: 057

---
।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
caturyugāni yānyāsan pūrvaṃ svāyambhuve'ntare ।  
teṣāṃ nisargaṃ tattvañca śrotumicchāmi vistarāt ।। 57.1 ।।  
।।sūta uvāca।।  
pṛthivyādiprasaṅgena yanmayā prāgudāhṛtam।  
teṣāñcaturyugaṃ hyetat pravakṣyāmi nibodhata ।। 57.2 ।।  
saṅkhyayeha prasaṅkhyāya vistārāccaiva sarvaśaḥ।  
yugañca yugabhedañca yugadharmantathaiva ca ।। 57.3 ।।  
yugasandhyaṃśakañcaiva yugasandhānameva ca।  
ṣaṭ‌prakārayugākhyānāṃ pravakṣyāmīha tattvataḥ ।। 57.4 ।।  
laukikena pramāṇena vibuddho'bdastu mānuṣaḥ।  
tenābdena prasaṅkhyāya vakṣyāmīha caturyugam ।। 57.5 .  
nimeṣakālaḥ kāṣṭā ca kalāścāpi muhūrttakāḥ।  
nimeṣakālatulyaṃ hi vidyāllaghvakṣarañcayat ।। 57.6 ।।  
kāṣṭā nimeṣā daśa pañca caiva triṃśacca kāṣṭā gaṇayet kalāstāḥ।  
triṃśat kalāścaiva bhavenmuhūrttāstatrtriṃśatā rātryahanī samete ।। 57.7 ।।  
ahorātre vibhajate sūryo mānuṣadaivike।  
tatrāhaḥ karmaceṣṭāyāṃ rātriḥ svapnāya kalpyate ।। 57.8 ।।  
pitrye rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ।  
kṛṣṇa pakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī ।। 57.9 ।।  
triṃśacca mānuṣā māsāḥ pitryo māsaśca sa smṛtaḥ।  
śatāni trīṇi māsānāṃ ṣaṣṭayā cāpyadhikāni vai।  
pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate ।। 57.10 ।।  
mānuṣeṇaiva mānena varṣāṇāṃ yacchataṃ bhavet ।  
pidṝṇāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi saṅkhayātānīha tāni vai।  
catvāra ścādhikā māsāḥ pitre caiveha kīrttitāḥ ।। 57.11 ।।  
lokikenaiva mānena abdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
etaddivyamahorātraṃ śāstre'smin niśvayo mataḥ ।। 57.12 ।।  
divye rātryahanī varṣaṃ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।  
ahastatrodagayanaṃ rātriḥ syāddakṣiṇāyanam ।। 57.13 ।।  
ye te rātryahanī divye prasaṅkhayāte tayoḥ punaḥ।  
triṃśacca tāni varṣāṇi divyo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। 57.14 ।।  
mānuṣañca śataṃ viddhi divyamāsāstrayastu te।  
daśa caiva tathāhāni divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 57.15 ।।  
trīṇi parṣaśatānyeva ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi yāni ca।  
divyaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrttitaḥ ।। 57.16 ।।  
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ।  
triṃśadyāni tu varṣāṇi mataḥ saptarṣivatsaraḥ ।। 57.17 ।।  
nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।  
anyāni navatiścaiva krauñcaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 57.18 ।।  
ṣaṭ‌triṃśattu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।  
varṣāṇāntu śataṃ jñeyaṃ divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 57.19 ।।  
trīṇyeva niyutānyeva varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi ca।  
ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi saṅkhyātāni tu saṅkhyayā।  
divyavarṣasahasrantu prāhuḥ saṅkhyāvido janāḥ ।। 57.20 ।।  
ityevamṛṣibhirgītaṃ divyayā saṅkhyayānvitam।  
divyenaiva pramāṇena yugasaṅkacāprakalpanam ।। 57.21 ।।  
catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni kavayo viduḥ।  
pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatastretā vidhīyate।  
dvāparaśca kali ścaiva yugānyetāni kalpayet ।। 57.22 ।।  
catvāryāhuḥ sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāntu kṛtaṃ yugam।  
tatra tāvacchatī sandhyā sandhyāṃśaśca tathāvidhaḥ ।। 57.23 ।।  
ita rāsu ca sandhyāsu sandhyāṃśeṣu ca vai triṣu ।  
ekāpāyena varttante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca ।। 57.24 ।।  
tretā trīṇi sahasrāṇi saṅkhyaiva parikīrtyate।  
tasyāstu triśatī sandhyā sandhyāṃśaśca tathāvidhaḥ ।। 57.25 ।।  
dvāparaṃ dve sahasre tu yugamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।  
tasyāpi dviśatī sandhyā sandhayāṃśaḥ sandhyayā samaḥ ।। 57.26 ।।  
kaliṃ varṣasahasrantu yugamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ।  
tasyāpyekaśatī sandhyā sandhyayā samaḥ ।। 57.27 ।।  
eṣā dvādaśasāhasrī yugākhyā parikīrttitā।  
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparañca kaliścaiva catuṣṭayam ।। 57.28 ।।  
atra saṃvatsarāḥ sṛṣṭā mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ।  
kṛtasya tāvadvakṣyāmi varṣāṇāṃ tatpramāṇataḥ ।। 57.29 ।।  
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyatra caturdaśa tu saṅkhyayā।  
catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi kalikālayugasya tu ।। 57.30 ।।  
evaṃ saṅ‌khyātakālaśca kāleṣviha viśeṣataḥ।  
evaṃ caturyugaḥ kālo vinā sandhyāṃśakaiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 57.31 ।।  
catvāriṃśatrtrīṇi caiva niyutāni ca saṅkhyayā ।  
viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi sasandhyāṃśaścaturyugaḥ ।। 57.32 ।।  
evaṃ caturyugākhyā tu sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ।  
kṛtatretādiyuktā sā manorantaramucyate ।। 57.33 ।।  
manvantarasya saṅkhyā tu varṣāgreṇa nibodhata।  
triṃśatkoṭyastu varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitāḥ ।। 57.34 ।।  
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu।  
viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi kālo'yaṃ sādhikāṃ vinā ।। 57.35 ।।  
manvantarasya saṅkhyaiṣā saṅkhyāvidbhirdvijaiḥ smṛtā।  
manvantarasya kālo'yaṃ yugaiḥ sārddhaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 57.36 ।।  
catuḥ sahasrayuktaṃ vai prathamantat kṛtaṃ yugam।  
tretāvaśiṣṭaṃ vakṣyāmi dvāparaṃ kalimeva ca ।। 57.37 ।।  
yugapatsamavetārtho dvidhā vaktuṃ na śakyate।  
kramāgataṃ mayā hyetattubhyaṃ proktaṃ yugadvayam।  
ṛṣivaṃśaprasaṅgena vyākulatvāttathaiva ca ।। 57.38 ।।  
tatra tretāyugasyādau manuḥ saptarṣayaśca te।  
śrautaṃ smārttañca dharmañca brahmaṇā ca pracoditam ।। 57.39 ।।  
dārāgnihotrasaṃyogamṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃjñitam।  
ityādilakṣaṇaṃ śrautaṃ dharmaṃ saptarṣayo'bruvan ।। 57.40 ।।  
parasparāgataṃ dharmaṃ smārttañcācāralakṣaṇam।  
varṇāśramācārayutaṃ manuḥ svāyambhuvo'bravīt ।। 57.41 ।।  
satyena brahmacaryeṇa śrutena tapasā ca vai।  
teṣāṃ sutaptatapasāmārṣeyeṇa krameṇa tu ।। 57.42 ।।  
saptarṣīṇāṃ manoścaiva ādye tretāyugasya tu ।  
abuddhipūrvakaṃ teṣāmakriyāpūrvameva ca ।। 57.43 ।।  
abhivyaktāstu te mantrāstārakādyairnidarśanaiḥ।  
ādikalpe tu devānāṃ prādurbhūtāstu te svayam ।। 57.44 ।।  
praṇāśe tvatha siddhīnāmapyāsāñca pravarttanam।  
āsan mantrā vyatīteṣu ye kalpeṣu sahasraśaḥ।  
temantrā vai punasteṣāṃ pratibhāsasamutthitāḥ ।। 57.45 ।।  
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni mantrāścātharvaṇāni ca।  
saptarṣibhistu te proktāḥ smārtaṃ dharmaṃ manurjagau ।। 57.46 ।।  
tretādau saṃhitā vaidāḥ kevalā dharmaśeṣataḥ।  
saṃrodhādāyuṣaścaivavyasyante dvāpareṣu te ।। 57.47 ।।  
ṛṣayastapasā devāḥ kalau ca dvāpareṣu vai।  
anādinidhanā divyāḥ pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭāḥ svayambhuvā ।। 57.48 ।।  
sadharmāḥ saprajāḥ sāṅgā yathādharmaṃ yuge yuge।  
vikrīḍante samānārthā vedavādā yathāyugam ।। 57.49 ।।  
ārambhayajñā kṣatrasya haviryajñā viśāmpateḥ।  
paricāra yajñāḥ śūdrāstu japayajñā dvijottamāḥ ।। 57.50 ।।  
tathā pramuditā varṇāstretāyāṃ dharmapālitāḥ।  
kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ samṛddhāḥ sukhinastathā ।। 57.51 ।।  
brāhmaṇānanuvarttante kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyān viśaḥ।  
vaiśyānuvartinaḥ śūdrāḥ parasparamanuvratāḥ ।। 57.52 ।।  
śubhāḥ pravṛttayasteṣāṃ dharmā varṇāśramāstathā।  
saṅkalpitena manasā vācoktena svasarmaṇā।  
tretāyuge tvavikalaḥ karmmārambhaḥ prasiddhyati ।। 57.53 ।।  
āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpamārogyaṃ dharmaśīlatā।  
sarvasādhāraṇā hyete tretāyāṃ vai bhavantyuta ।। 57.54 ।।  
varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā tathākarot ।  
punaḥ prajāstu tā mohāttān dharmānna hyapālayan ।। 57.55 ।।  
parasparavirodhena manuntāḥ punaranvayuḥ।  
manuḥ svāyambhuvo dṛṣṭvā yāthātathyaṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। 57.56 ।।  
dhātā tu śatarūpāyāḥ pumān sa udapādayat।  
priyavratottānapādau pradhamantau mahīpatī ।। 57.57 ।।  
tataḥ prabhṛti rājāna utpannā daṇḍadhāriṇaḥ।  
prajānāṃ rañjanāccaiva rājānastvabhavannṛṣāḥ ।। 57.58 ।।  
pracchannapāpā ye jetumaśakyā manujā bhuvi।  
dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya teṣāṃ śāstre tapo mayā ।। 57.59 ।।  
varṇānāṃ pravibhāgāśca tretāyāṃ saṃprakīrtitāḥ।  
saṃhitāśca tato mantrā ṛṣabhirbrahmaṇaistu te ।। 57.60 ।।  
yajñaḥ pravartitaścaiva tadā hyevantu daivataiḥ।  
yāmaiḥ śuklairjapaiścaiva sarvasambhārasaṃvṛtaiḥ ।। 57.61 ।।  
sārddhaṃ viśvabhujā caiva devendreṇa mahaujasā।  
svāyambhuve'ntare devairyajñāste prāk pravartitāḥ ।। 57.62 ।।  
satyaṃ japastapo dānaṃ tretāyāṃ dharma ucyate।  
kriyā dharmaśca hrasate satyadharmaḥ pravarttate ।। 57.63 ।।  
prajāyante tataḥ śūrā āyuṣmanto mahābalāḥ।  
nyastadaṇḍamahābhāgā yajvāno brahmavādinaḥ ।। 57.64 ।।  
padma patrāyatākṣāśca pṛthūraskāḥ susaṃhitāḥ।  
siṃhāntakā mahāsattvā mattamātaṅgagāminaḥ ।। 57.65 ।।  
mahādhanurddharāścaiva tretāyāṃ cakravartinaḥ।  
sarvalakṣaṇasampannā nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalāḥ ।। 57.66 ।।  
nyagrodhau tau smṛtau bāhū vyāmo nyagrodha ucyate।  
vāmenaivocchrayādyasya sama ūrddhvantu dehinaḥ।  
samucchrayaḥ parīṇāho jñeyo nyagrodhamaṇḍalaḥ ।। 57.67 ।।  
cakraṃ ratho maṇirbhāryā nidhiraścāgajāstathā।  
saptātiśayaratnāni sarveṣāñcakravarttinām ।। 57.68 ।


---
title: 058

---
।।sūta uvāca ।।  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvāparasya vidhiṃ punaḥ।  
tatra tretāyuge kṣīṇe dvāparaṃ pratipadyate ।। 58.1 ।।  
  
dvāparādau prajānāntu siddhistratāyuge tu yā।  
parivṛtte yuge tasmiṃstataḥ sā saṃpraṇaśyati ।। 58.2 ।।  
  
tataḥ pravarttate tāsāṃ prajānāṃ dvāpare punaḥ।  
lobho'dhṛtirvaṇigyuddhaṃ tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ ।। 58.3 ।।  
  
tambhedaścaiva varṇānāṃ kāryāṇāñcā vinirṇayaḥ।  
yajñauṣadheḥ paśordaṇḍo mado dambho'kṣamā balam।  
eṣāṃ rajastamoyuktā pravṛttirdvāpare smṛtā ।। 58.4 ।।  
  
ādye kṛte ca dharmo'sti tretāyāṃ samprapadyate।  
dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge ।। 58.5 ।।  
  
varṇānāṃ viparidhvaṃsaḥ saṃkīrttyate tathāśramaḥ।  
dvaidhamutpadyate caiva yuge tasmin śrutau smṛtau ।। 58.6 ।।  
  
dvaidhāt śruteḥ smṛteścaiva niścayo nādhigamyate।  
aniścayādigamanāddharmatattvaṃ nigadyate।  
dharmatattve tu bhinnānāṃ matibhedo bhavennṛṇām ।। 58.7 ।।  
  
parasparavibhinnaistairdṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhrameṇa ca।  
ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti niścayo nābhigamyate ।। 58.8 ।।  
  
kāraṇānāñca vakailyāt kāraṇasyāpyaniścayāt।  
matibhede ca teṣāṃ vai dṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhramo bhavet ।। 58.9 ।।  
  
tato dṛṣṭivibhinnaistaiḥ kṛtaṃ śāstrakulantvidam।  
eko vedaśvatuṣpādastretāsviha vidhīyate ।। 58.10 ।।  
  
saṃrodhādāyuṣaścaiva dṛśyate dvāpareṣu ca ।  
vedavyāsaiścaturdhā tu vyasyate dvāparādiṣu ।। 58.11 ।।  
  
ṛṣiputraiḥ punarvedā bhidyante dṛṣṭivibhramaiḥ।  
mantrabrāhmaṇavinyāsaiḥ svaravarṇaviparyayaiḥ ।। 58.12 ।।  
  
saṃhitā ṛgyajuḥsāmnāṃ saṃhanyante śrutarṣibhiḥ।  
sāmānyādvaikṛtāccaiva dṛṣṭibhinnaiḥ vkacitvkacit ।। 58.13 ।।  
  
brāhmaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāṇi mantrapravacanāni ca।  
anye tu prahitāstīrthaiḥ kecittān pratyavasthitāḥ ।। 58.14 ।।  
  
dvāpareṣu pravarttante bhinnavṛttāśramā dvijāḥ।  
ekamādhvaryavaṃ pūrvamāsīddvaidhaṃ punastataḥ ।। 58.15 ।।  
  
sāmānyaviparītārthaiḥ kṛtaṃ śāstrakulantvidam।  
ādhvaryavasya prastāvairbahudhā vyākulaṃ kṛtam ।। 58.16 ।।  
  
tathaivātharvṛksāmnāṃ vikalpaiścāpyasaṃkṣayaiḥ।  
vyākulaṃ dvāpare bhinne kriyate bhinnadarśanaiḥ ।। 58.17 ।।  
  
taiṣāṃ bhedāḥ prabhedāśca vikalpaiścāpyasaṃkṣayāḥ ।  
dvāpare sampravartante vinaśyanti punaḥ kalau ।। 58.18 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ viparyayāścaiva bhavanti dvāpare punaḥ।  
avṛṣṭirmaraṇañcaiva tathaiva vyādhyupadvavāḥ ।। 58.19 ।।  
  
vāṅmanaḥkarmajairduḥkhairnirvedo jāyate punaḥ ।  
nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥkhamokṣa vicāraṇā ।। 58.20 ।।  
  
vicārāṇācca vairāgyaṃ vairāgyāddopadarśanam।  
doṣāṇāṃ darśanāccaiva dvāpare jñānasambhavaḥ ।। 58.21 ।।  
  
teṣāñca mānināṃ pūrvamādye svāyambhuve'ntare।  
utpadyante hi śāstrāṇāṃ dvāpare paripanthinaḥ ।। 58.22 ।।  
  
āyurvedavikalpāśca aṅgānāṃ jyautiṣasya ca।  
arthaśāstravikalpaśca hetuśāstravikalpanam ।। 58.23 ।।  
  
smṛtiśāstraprabhedāśca prasthānāni pṛthak pṛthak।  
dvāpareṣvabhivarttante matibhedāstathā nṛṇām ।। 58.24 ।।  
  
manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrā dvārttā prasiddhyati।  
dvāpare sarvabhūtānāṃ kāyakleśapuraskṛtā ।। 58.25 ।।  
  
lobhe'dhṛtirvaṇigyuddhaṃ tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ।  
vedaśāstrapraṇayanaṃ dharmāṇāṃ saṅkarastathā ।। 58.26 ।।  
  
dvāpareṣu pravarttante rogo lobho vadhastathā।  
varṇāśramaparidhvaṃsāḥ kāmadveṣau tathaiva ca ।। 58.27 ।।  
  
pūrṇe varṣasahasre dve paramāyustuthā nṛṇām।  
niḥśepe dvāpare tasmin tasya sandhyā tu pādataḥ ।। 58.28 ।।  
  
pratiṣṭhate guṇairhīno dharmo'sau dvāparasya tu ।  
tathaiva sandhyāpādena aṃśastasyāvatiṣṭhate ।। 58.29 ।।  
  
dvāparasya ca varṣe yā tiṣyasya tu nibodhata।  
dvāparasyāṃśaśeṣe tu pratipattiḥ kalerataḥ ।। 58.30 ।।  
  
hiṃsāsūyānṛtaṃ māyā vadhaścaiva tapasvinām।  
ete svabhāvāstiṣyasya sādhayanti ca vai prajāḥ ।। 58.31 ।।  
  
eṣa dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛtsno dharmaśca parihīyate।  
manasā karmaṇā stutyā vārttā siddhyati vā na vā ।। 58.32 ।।  
  
kalau pramārako rogaḥ satataṃ kṣudbhayāni vai।  
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ darśanañca viparyayam ।। 58.33 ।।  
  
na pramāṇaṃ smṛterasti tiṣye loke yuge yuge।  
garbhastho mriyate kaścidyauvanasthastathāparaḥ ।  
sthāvire madhyakaumāre mriyante vai kalau prajāḥ ।। 58.34 ।।  
  
adhārmikāstvanācārāstīkṣṇa kopālpatejasaḥ।  
anṛtabruvaśca satataṃ tiṣye jāyanti vai prajāḥ ।। 58.35 ।।  
  
duriṣṭairduradhītaiśca durācārairdurāgamaiḥ।  
viprāṇāṃ karmadoṣaistaiḥ prajānāṃ jāyate bhayam ।। 58.36 ।।  
  
hiṃsā māyā tatherṣyā ca krodho'sūyākṣamānṛtam।  
tiṣye bhavanti jantūnāṃ rāgo lobhaśca sarvaśaḥ ।। 58.37 ।।  
  
saṃkṣobho jāyate'tyarthaṃ kalimāsādya vai yugam।  
nādhīyante tadā vedā na yajante dvijātayaḥ।  
utsīdanti narāścaiva kṣatriyāḥ saviśaḥ kramāt ।। 58.38 ।।  
  
kṣudrāṇāmantyayonestu sambandhā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha।  
bhavantīha kalau tasmin śayanāsanabhojanaiḥ ।। 58.39 ।।  
  
rājānaḥ śūdrabhūyiṣṭā pāṣaṇḍānāṃ pravartakāḥ।  
bhrūṇahatyāḥ prajāstatra prajā evaṃ pravarttate ।। 58.40 ।।  
  
āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpaṃ kulañcaiva prahīyate।  
śūdrāśca brāhmaṇācārāḥ śūdrācārāśca brāhmaṇāḥ ।। 58.41 ।।  
  
rājavṛtte sthitāścaurāścauravṛttāśca pārthivāḥ।  
bhṛtyāśca naṣṭasuhṛdo yugānte paryupasthite ।। 58.42 ।।  
  
aśīlinyo'vratāścāpi striyo madyāmiṣapriyāḥ।  
māyāmātrā bhaviṣyanti yugānte pratyupasthite ।। 58.43 ।।  
  
śvāpadaprabalatvañca gavāñcaivāpyupakṣayaḥ।  
sādhūnāṃ vinivṛttiśca vidyāttasmin kalau yuge ।। 58.44 ।।  
  
tadā sūkṣme mahodarko durlabho bhogināṃ tathā।  
caturāśramaśaithilyāddharmaḥ pravicaliṣyati ।। 58.45 ।।  
  
tadā hyalpaphalā devī bhavedbhūmirmahīyasī।  
śūdrāstapaścariṣyanti yugānte pratyupaśthite ।। 58.46 ।।  
  
tadā hyaikāhiko dharmo dvāpare yaśca māsikaḥ।  
tretāyāṃ vatsarasthaśca ekāhādatiricyate ।। 58.47 ।।  
  
arakṣitāro harttāro balibhāgasya pārthivāḥ।  
yugānteṣu bhaviṣyanti svarakṣaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।। 58.48 ।।  
  
akṣatriyāśca rājāno viśaḥ śūdropajīvinaḥ।  
śūdrābhivādinaḥ sarve yugānte dvijasattamāḥ ।। 58.49 ।।  
  
patayaśca bhaviṣyanti bahavo'smin kalau yuge।  
citravarṣī tadā devo yadā syāttu yugakṣayaḥ ।। 58.50 ।।  
  
sarve vāṇijakāścāpi bhaviṣyantyadhame yuge।  
bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kūṭamānaiśca paṇyavikrītatejanaiḥ ।। 58.51 ।।  
  
kuśīlacaryā pāṣaṇḍairvṛthārūpaiḥ samāvṛtam।  
puruṣālpaṃ bahustrīkaṃ yugānte paryupasthite ।। 58.52 ।।  
  
bahuyācanako loko bhaviṣyati parasparam।  
kravyādanaḥ krūravākyo nārjavo nānasūyakaḥ ।। 58.53 ।।  
  
na kṛte pratikartā ca kṣīṇo loko bhaviṣyati।  
aśaṅkā caiva patite tadyugāntasya lakṣaṇam ।। 58.54 ।।  
  
naraśūnyā vasumatī śūnyā caiva bhaviṣyati।  
maṇḍalāni bhavantyatra deśeṣu nagareṣu ca ।। 58.55 ।।  
  
alpodakā cālpaphalā bhaviṣyati vasundharā।  
goptāraścāpyagoptāraḥ prabhaviṣyantyaśāsanāḥ ।। 58.56 ।।  
  
harttāraḥ pararatnānāṃ paradārapradharṣakāḥ।  
kāmātmāno durātmāno hyadharmāt sāhasapriyāḥ ।। 58.57 ।।  
  
anaṣṭacetanāḥ puṃso muktakeśāstu cūlikāḥ।  
ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣāśca prajāyante yugakṣaye ।। 58.58 ।।  
  
śukladantā jitākṣāśca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāyavāsasaḥ।  
śūdrā dharmañcariṣyanti yugānte paryupasthite ।। 58.59 ।।  
  
sasyacaurā bhaviṣyaṃti tathā cailābhimarśanāḥ।  
caurāścaurasya harttāro hanturharttāra eva va ।। 58.60 ।।  
  
jñānakarmaṇyuparate loke niṣkriyatāṅgate ।  
kīṭamūṣikasarpāśca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān ।। 58.61 ।।  
  
subhikṣaṃ kṣemamārogyaṃ sāmarthyaṃ durlabhaṃ bhavet।  
kauśikāḥ prativatsyanti deśān kṣudbhayapīḍitān ।। 58.62 ।।  
  
duḥkhenābhiplutānāñca paramāyuḥ śataṃ bhavet।  
dṛśyante na ca dṛśyante vedāḥ kaliyuge'khilāḥ ।। 58.63 ।।  
  
utsīdanti tathā yajñāḥ kevalā dharmapīḍitāḥ।  
kaṣāyiṇaśca nirgranthāstathā kāpālinaśca ha ।। 58.64 ।।  
  
vedavikrayiṇaścānye tīrthavikrayiṇo'pare ।  
varṇāśramāṇāṃ ye cānye pāṣaṇḍāḥ paripanthinaḥ ।। 58.65 ।।  
  
utpadyante tathā te vai saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge।  
nādhīyante tadā vedāḥ śūdrā dharmārthakovidāḥ ।। 58.66 ।।  
  
yajante nāśvamedhena rājānaḥ śūdrayonayaḥ।  
strīvadhaṃ govadhaṃ kṛtvā hatvā caiva parasparam।  
upahanyustadānyonyaṃ sādhayanti tathā prajāḥ ।। 58.67 ।।  
  
duḥkhapracārato'lpāyurdeśotsādaḥ sarogatā।  
moho glānistathāsaukhyaṃ tamovṛttaṃ kalau smṛtam ।। 58.68 ।।  
  
prajā tu bhrūṇahatyāyāmatha vai sampravarttate।  
tasmādāyurbalaṃ rūpaṃ kaliṃ prāpya prahīyate।  
duḥkhenābhiplutānāṃ vai paramāyuḥ śataṃ nṛṇām ।। 58.69 ।।  
  
dṛśyante nābhidṛśyante vedāḥ kaliyuge'khilāḥ।  
utsīdante tadā yajñāḥ kovalā dharmapīḍitāḥ ।। 58.70 ।।  
  
tadā tvalpena kālena siddhiṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ।  
dhanyā dharmañcariṣyanti yugānte dvijasattamāḥ ।। 58.71 ।।  
  
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ ye carantyanasūyakāḥ.  
tretāyāṃ vārṣiko dharmo dvāpare māsikaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
yathāśaktiṃ caran prājñastadahnā prāpruyāt kalau ।। 58.72 ।।  
  
eṣā kaliyuge'vasthā sandhyāṃśantu nibodha me ।  
yuge yuge tu hīyante trīṃstrīn pādāṃśca siddhayaḥ ।। 58.73 ।।  
  
yugasvabhāvātsandhyāstu tiṣṭhantīmāstu pādaśaḥ।  
sandhyāsvabhāvāccāṃśeṣu pādaśaste pratiṣṭitāḥ ।। 58.74 ।।  
  
evaṃ sandhyāṃśake kāle samprāpte tu yugāntike।  
teṣāṃ śāstā hyasādhūnāṃ bhṛgūṇāṃ nidhanotthitaḥ ।। 58.75 ।।  
  
gotreṇa vai candramaso nāmnā pramitirucyate।  
mādhavasya tu soṃśena pūrvaṃ svāyambhuve'ntare ।। 58.76 ।।  
  
samāḥ sa viṃśatiṃ pūrṇāḥ paryaṭan vai vasundharām।  
ācakarṣa sa vai senāṃ savājirathakuñjarām ।। 58.77 ।।  
  
pragṛhītāyudhairvipraiḥ śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ।  
sa tadā taiḥ parivṛto mlecchān hanti sahasraśaḥ ।। 58.78 ।।  
  
sa hatvā sarvagaścaiva rājñastān śūdrayonijāt।  
pāṣaṇḍān sa tataḥ sarvānniḥśeṣān kṛtavān prabhuḥ ।। 58.79 ।।  
  
nātyarthaṃ dhārmikā ye ca tān sarvān hanti sarvaśaḥ।  
varṇavyatyāsajātāṃśca ye ca tānupajīvinaḥ ।। 58.80 ।।  
  
udīcyānmadhyadeśāṃśca pārvatīyāṃstathaiva ca।  
prācyān pratīcyāṃśca tathā vindhyapṛṣṭāparāntikān ।। 58.81 ।।  
  
tathaiva dākṣiṇātyāṃśca draviḍān siṃhalaiḥ saha।  
gāndārān pāradāṃścaiva pahnavān yavanāṃstathā ।। 58.82 ।।  
  
tuṣārān varvarāṃścīnān śūlikān daradān khasān।  
lampākāntha ketāṃśca kirātānāñca jātayaḥ ।। 58.83 ।।  
  
pravṛttacakro balavān mlecchānāmantakṛdvibhuḥ।  
adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ cacārātha vasundharām ।। 58.84 ।।  
  
mādhavasya tu soṃśena devasya hi vijajñivān ।  
pūrvajanmavidhijñaiśca pramitirnāma vīryavān ।। 58.85 ।।  
  
gotreṇa vai candramasaḥ pūrve kaliyuge prabhuḥ।  
dvātriṃśe'bhyudite varṣe prakrānte viṃśatiṃ samāḥ ।। 58.86 ।।  
  
vinighnan sarvabhūtāni mānavāni sahasraśaḥ।  
kṛtvā vīryāvaśeṣāntu pṛthvīṃ ऱūḍhena karmaṇā ।  
parasparanimittena kopenākasmikena tu ।। 58.87 ।।  
  
sa sādhayitvā vṛṣalān prāyaśastānadhārmikān ।  
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye niṣṭāṃ prāptaḥ sahānugaḥ ।। 58.88 ।।  
  
tato vyatīte tasmiṃstu amātye satyasainike।  
utsādya pārthivān sarvān mlecchāṃścaiva sahasraśaḥ ।। 58.89 ।।  
  
tatra sandhyāṃśake kāle samprāpte tu yugāntike।  
sthitāsvalpāvaśiṣṭāsu prajāsviha vkacit vkacit ।। 58.90 ।।  
  
apragrahāstatastā vai lokaceṣṭāstu vṛndaśaḥ।  
upahiṃsanti cānyonyaṃ prapadyante parasparam ।। 58.91 ।।  
  
arājake yugavaśāt saṃśaye samupasthite।  
prajāstā vai tataḥ sarvāḥ parasparabhayārditāḥ ।। 58.92 ।।  
  
vyākulāśca pariśrāntāstyaktvā dārān gṛhāṇi ca।  
svān prāṇān samavekṣanto niṣṭāṃ prāptāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ ।। 58.93 ।।  
  
naṣṭe śraute smṛte dharme parasparahatāstadā।  
nirmaryādā nirākrandā niḥsnehā nirapatrapāḥ ।। 58.94 ।।  
  
naṣṭe varpe pratihatā hrasvakāḥ pañjaviṃśakāḥ।  
hitvā dārāṃśca putrāṃśca viṣādavyākulendriyāḥ ।। 58.95 ।।  
  
anāvṛṣṭihatāścaiva vārttāmutsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ।  
pratyantāṃstānnipevante hitvā janapadān svakān ।। 58.96 ।।  
  
saritaḥ sāgarān kūpān sevante parvatāṃstadā।  
madhumāṃsairmūlaphalairvarttayanti suduḥkhitāḥ ।। 58.97 ।।  
  
cīravastrājinadharā niṣpatrā niṣparigrahāḥ।  
varṇāśramaparibhraṣṭāḥ saṅkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ ।। 58.98 ।।  
  
etāḥ kāṣṭāmanuprāptā alpaśeṣāstathā prajāḥ ।  
jarāvyādhikṣudhāviṣṭā duḥkhānnirvedamāgaman ।। 58.99 ।।  
  
vicāraṇantu nirvedāt sāmyāvasthā vicāraṇāt।  
sāmyāvasthāsu sambodhaḥ sambodhāddharmaśīlatā ।। 58.100 ।।  
  
tāsupagamayuktāsu kaliśiṣṭāsu vai svayam।  
ahorātraṃ tadā tāsāṃ yugantu parivarttate ।। 58.101 ।।  
  
cittasammohanaṃ kṛtvā tāsāntaiḥ saptamantu tat।  
bhāvino'rthasya ca balāttataḥ kṛtamavartata ।। 58.102 ।।  
  
pravṛtte tu punastasmiṃstataḥ kṛtayuge tu vai।  
utpannāḥ kaliśiṣṭāstu kārtayugyaḥ prajāmtadā ।। 58.103 ।।  
  
tiṣṭhanti ceha ye siddhāḥ sudṛṣṭā vicaranti ca।  
sadā saptarṣayaścaiva tatra te ca vyavasthitāḥ ।। 58.104 ।।  
  
brahmakṣatraviśaḥ śūdrā bījārthaṃ ye smṛtā iha।  
kalijaiḥ saha te sarve nirviśeṣāstadābhavan ।। 58.105 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ saptarṣayo dharma kathayantītareṣu ca ।  
varṇā śramācārayuktaḥ śrautaḥ smārto dvidhā tu saḥ ।। 58.106 ।।  
  
tatasteṣu kriyāvatsu varttante vai prajāḥ kṛte ।  
śrautaḥ smārttaḥ kṛtānāntu dharmaḥ saptarṣidarśitaḥ ।। 58.107 ।।  
  
tāsu dharmavyavastārthaṃ tiṣṭhantīhāyugakṣayāt ।  
manvantarādhikāreṣu tiṣṭhanti munayastu vai ।। 58.108 ।।  
  
yathā dāvapradagdheṣu tṛṇeṣviha tape ṛtau ।  
navānāṃ prathamaṃ dṛṣṭasteṣāṃ mūle tu sambhavaḥ ।। 58.109 ।।  
  
evaṃ yugādyugasteha santānastu parasparam ।  
varttate hyavyavacchedādyāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ ।। 58.110 ।।  
  
sukhamāyurbalaṃ rūpaṃ dharmārthau kāma eva ca ।  
yugeṣvetāni hīyante trīṇi pādakrameṇa tu ।। 58.111 ।।  
  
sasandhyaṃśeṣu hīyante yugānāṃ dharmasiddhayaḥ।  
ityeṣa pratisandhirvaḥ kīrttitastu mayā dvijāḥ ।। 58.112 ।।  
  
caturyugānāṃ sarveṣāmetenaiva prasādhanam ।।  
eṣā caturyugāvṛttirāsahasrāt pravarttate ।। 58.113 ।।  
  
brahmaṇastadahaḥ proktaṃ rātriśca tāvatī smṛtā ।  
atrārjavaṃ jaḍībhāvo bhūtānāmāyugakṣayāt ।। 58.114 ।।  
  
etadeva tu sarveṣāṃ yugānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ smṛtam।  
eṣā caturyugānāntu gaṇanā hyekasaptatiḥ।  
krameṇa parivṛttā tu manorantaramucyate ।। 58.115 ।।  
  
caturyuge tathaikasmin bhavatīha yathāśrutam।  
tathā cānyeṣu bhavati punastadvai yathākramam ।। 58.116 ।।  
  
sarge sarge yathā bhedā utpadyante tathaiva tu ।  
pañcaviṃśatparimitā na nyūnā nādhikāstathā ।। 58.117 ।।  
  
tathā kalpayugaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhavanti samalakṣaṇāḥ।  
manvantarāṇāṃ sarveṣāmetadeva tu lakṣaṇam ।। 58.118 ।।  
  
tathā yugānāṃ parivarttanāni cirapravṛttāni yugasvabhavāt ।  
tathā na santiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivarttamānaḥ ।। 58.119 ।।  
  
ityetallakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yugānāṃ vai samāsataḥ।  
atītānāgatānāṃ vai sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi ।। 58.120 ।।  
  
anāgateṣu tadvacca tarkkaḥ kāryo vijānatā।  
manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha ।। 58.121 ।।  
  
manvantareṇa caikena sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi vai।  
vyākhyātāni vijānīdvaṃ kalpe kalpena caiva hi ।। 58.122 ।।  
  
asyābhimāninaḥ sarve nāmarūpairbhavantyuta।  
devā hyaṣṭavidhā ye ca iha manvantareśvarāḥ ।। 58.123 ।।  
  
ṛṣayo manavaścaiva sarve tulyāḥ prayojanaiḥ।  
evaṃ varṇāśramāṇāntu pravibhāgo yuge yuge ।। 58.124 ।।  
  
yugasvabhāvācca tathā vidhatte vai sadā prabhuḥ ।  
varṇāśramavibhāgaśca yugāni yugasiddhaye ।। 58.125 ।।  
  
anuṣaṅgaḥ samākhyātaḥ sṛṣṭisargannibodhata।  
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca sthitiṃ vakṣye yugeṣviha ।। 58.126 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte caturyugākhyānaṃ nāmāṣṭapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 58 ।


---
title: 059

---
।।sūta uvāca।।  
yugeṣu yāstu jāyante prajāstā vai nibodhata।  
āśurī sarpagopakṣipaiśācī yakṣarākṣasī।  
yasmin yuge ca sambhūtistāsāṃ yāvattu jīvitam ।। 59.1 ।।  
  
piśācāsuragandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ।  
yugamātrantu jīvanti ṛte mṛtyuvadhena te ।। 59.2 ।।  
  
mānuṣāṇāṃ paśūnāñca pakṣiṇāṃ sthāvaraiḥsaha।  
teṣāmāyuḥ parikrāntaṃ yugadharmeṣu sarvaśaḥ ।। 59.3 ।।  
  
asthitistu kalau dṛṣṭā bhūtānāmāyuṣastu vai।  
paramāyuḥ śatantvetanmanuṣyāṇāṃ kalau smṛtam ।। 59.4 ।।  
  
devāsurapramāṇāttu saptasaptāṅgulaṃ hrasat।  
ahgulānāṃ śataṃ pūrṇamaṣṭapañcāśaduttaram ।। 59.5 ।।  
  
devāsurapramāṇantaducchrāyaṃ kalijaiḥ smṛtam।  
catvāraścāpyaśītiśca kalijairaṅgulaiḥ smṛtam ।। 59.6 ।।  
  
svenāṅgulapramāṇena ūrddhvamāpādamastakam।  
ityeṣa mānuṣotsedho hrasatīha yugāntike ।। 59.7 ।।  
  
sarveṣu yugakāleṣu atītānāgateṣviha।  
svenāṅgulapramāṇena aṣṭatālaḥ smṛto naraḥ ।। 59.8 ।।  
  
āpādato mastakantu navatālo bhavettu yaḥ।  
saṃhatājānubāhustu sa surairapi pūjyate ।। 59.9 ।।  
  
gavāśvahastināñcaiva mahiṣa sthāvarātmanām।  
krameṇaitena yogena hrāsavṛddhī yuge yuge ।। 59.10 ।।  
  
ṣaṭsaptatyaṅgulotsedhaḥ paśūnāṃ kakudastu vai।  
aṅgulāṣṭaśataṃ pūrṇamutsedhaḥ kariṇāṃ smṛtaḥ ।। 59.11 ।।  
  
aṅgulānāṃ sahasrantu catvāriṃśāṅgulaṃ vinā ।  
pañcāśataṃ hayānāñca utsedhaḥ śākhināṃ smṛtaḥ ।। 59.12 ।।  
  
mānuṣasya śarīrasya sanniveśastu yādṛśaḥ।  
tallakṣaṇastu devānāṃ dṛśyate tattvarśanāt ।। 59.13 ।।  
  
buddhyātiśayayuktañca devānāṃ kāyamucyate ।  
devānatiśayañcaiva mānuṣaṃ kāyamucyate ।। 59.14 ।।  
  
ityete vai parikrāntā bhāvā ye divyamānuṣāḥ।  
paśūnāṃ pakṣiṇāñcaiva sthāvarāṇāṃ nibodhata ।। 59.15 ।।  
  
gāvo hyajā mahiṣyo'śvā hastinaḥ pakṣiṇo nagāḥ।  
upayūktāḥ kriyāsvete yajñiyāsviha sarvaśaḥ ।। 59.16 ।।  
  
devasthāneṣu jāyante tadrūpā eva te punaḥ ।  
yathāśayopabhogāstu devānāṃ śubhamūrttayaḥ ।। 59.17 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ rūpānurūpaistaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ sthāṇujaṅgamaiḥ।  
manojñaistattvabhāvajñaiḥ sukhino hyupapedire ।। 59.18 ।।  
  
ataḥ śiṣṭān pravakṣyāmi sataḥ sādhūṃstathaiva ca।  
saditi brahmaṇaḥ śabdastadvanto ye bhavantyuta।  
sāyujyaṃ brahmaṇo'tyantaṃ tena santaḥ prajakṣyate ।। 59.19 ।।  
  
daśātmake ye viṣaye kāraṇe cāṣṭalakṣaṇe ।  
na krudhyanti na hṛṣyanti jitātmānastu te smṛtāḥ ।। 59.20 ।।  
  
sāmānyeṣu ca dharmeṣu tathā vaiśeṣikeṣu ca।  
brahmakṣatraviśo yuktā yasmāttasmāddvijātayaḥ ।। 59.21 ।।  
  
varṇāśrameṣu yuktasya svargagomukhacāriṇaḥ।  
śrautasmārtasya dharmasya jñānāddharmaḥ sa ucyate ।। 59.22 ।।  
  
vidyāyāḥ sādhanātsādhurbrahmacārī gurorhitaḥ।  
kriyāṇāṃ sādhanāccaiva gṛhasthaḥ sādhurucyate ।। 59.23 ।।  
  
sādhanāttapaso'raṇye sādhurvaikhānasaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
yatamāno yatiḥ sādhuḥ smṛto yogasya sādhanāt ।। 59.24 ।।  
  
evamāśramadharmāṇāṃ sādhanāt sādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ।  
gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho'tha bhikṣukaḥ ।। 59.25 ।।  
  
na ca devā na pitaro munayo na ca mānavāḥ।  
ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti bruvanto'bhinnadarśanāḥ ।। 59.26 ।।  
  
dharmādharmāviha proktau śabdāvetau kriyātmakau।  
kuśalākuśalaṃ karma dharmā dharmāviti smṛtau ।। 59.27 ।।  
  
dhāraṇā dhṛtirityarthāddhātordharmaḥ prakīrttitaḥ ।  
adhāraṇe'mahattve ca adharma iti cocyate ।। 59.28 ।।  
  
atreṣṭaprāpakā dharmā ācāryairupadiśyate।  
vṛddhā hyalolupāścaiva ātmavanto hyadambhakāḥ।  
samyagvinītā ṛjavastānācāryān pracakṣate ।। 59.29 ।।  
  
svayamācarate yasmādācāraṃ sthāpayatyapi।  
ācinoti ca śāstrārthānyamaiḥ sanniyamairyutaḥ ।। 59.30 ।।  
  
pūrvebhyo vedayitveha śrautaṃ saptarṣayo'bruvan।  
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni brahmaṇo'ṅgāni ca śrutiḥ ।। 59.31 ।।  
  
manvantarasyātītasya smṛtvācāraṃ punarjagau।  
tasmātsmārtaḥ smṛto dharmo varṇāśramavibhāgajaḥ ।। 59.32 ।।  
  
sa eṣa dvividho dharmaḥ śiṣṭācāra ihocyate।  
śeṣaśabdāt śiṣṭa iti śiṣṭācāraḥ pracakṣyate ।। 59.33 ।।  
  
manvantareṣu ye śiṣṭā iha tiṣṭhanti dhārmikāḥ।  
manuḥ saptarṣayaścaiva lokasantānakāraṇāt।  
dharmārthaṃ ye ca śiṣṭa vai yāthātathyaṃ pracakṣyate ।। 59.34 ।।  
  
manvādayaśca ye śiṣṭā ye mayā prāgudīritāḥ।  
taiḥ śiṣṭaiścarito dharmaḥ samyageva yuge yuge ।। 59.35 ।।  
  
trayī vārtā daṇḍanītirijyā varṇāśramāstathā।  
śiṣṭairācaryate yasmānmanunā ca punaḥ punaḥ।  
pūrvaiḥ pūrvagatatvācca śiṣṭācāraḥ sa śāśvataḥ ।। 59.36 ।।  
  
dānaṃ satyantapo'lobho vidyejyāprajanī dayā।  
aṣṭau tāni caritrāṇi śiṣṭācārasya lakṣaṇam ।। 59.37 ।।  
  
śiṣṭā yasmāccarantyenaṃ manuḥ saptarṣayaśca vai।  
manvantareṣu sarveṣu śiṣṭācārastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 59.38 ।।  
  
vijñeyaḥ śravaṇāt śrautaḥ smaraṇāt smārtta ucyate।  
ijyā vedātmakaḥ śrautaḥ smārto varṇāśramātmakaḥ।  
pratyaṅgāni ca vakṣyāmi dharmasyeha tu lakṣaṇam ।। 59.39 ।।  
  
dṛṣṭvā prabhūtamarthaṃ yaḥ pṛṣṭo vai na nigūhati।  
yathā bhūtapravādastu ityetatsatyalakṣaṇam ।। 59.40 ।।  
  
brahmacaryaṃ japo maunaṃ nirāhāratvameva ca।  
ityetat tapaso mūlaṃ sughoraṃ taddurāsadam ।। 59.41 ।।  
  
paśūnāṃ dravyahaviṣāmṛksāmayajuṣāṃ tathā।  
ṛtvijāṃ dakṣiṇānāñca saṃyogo yoga ucyate ।। 59.42 ।।  
  
ātmavatsarvabhūteṣu yo hitāyāhitāya ca।  
samā pravarttate dṛṣṭiḥ kṛtsnā hyeṣā dayā smṛtā ।। 59.43 ।।  
  
ākruṣṭo'bhihato vāpi nākrośedyo na hanti vā।  
vāṅ‌manaḥkarmabhiḥ kṣāntistitikṣaiṣā kṣamā smṛtā ।। 59.44 ।।  
  
svāminārakṣyamāṇānāmutsṛṣṭānāñca mṛtsu ca।  
parasvānāmanādānamalobha iha kīrtyate ।। 59.45 ।।  
  
maithunasyāsamācāro hyacintanamakalpanam।  
nivṛttirbrahmacaryaṃ tadacchidraṃ dama ucyate ।। 59.46 ।।  
  
ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā indriyāṇīha yasya vai।  
na mithyā sampravartante śamasyai tattu lakṣaṇam ।। 59.47 ।।  
  
daśātmake yo viṣaye kāraṇe cāṣṭalakṣaṇe।  
na krudhyettu pratihataḥ sa jitātmā vibhāvyate ।। 59.48 ।।  
  
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenopāgatañca yat।  
tattadguṇavate deyamityetaddānalakṣaṇam ।। 59.49 ।।  
  
dānaṃ trividhamityetat kaniṣṭhajyeṣṭhamadhayamam ।  
tatra naiḥśreyasaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ svārthasiddhaye।  
kāruṇyātsarvabhūtebhyaḥ suvibhāgastu bandhuṣu ।। 59.50 ।।  
  
śrutismṛtibhyāṃ vihito dharmo varṇāśramātmakaḥ।  
śiṣṭācārāviruddhaśca dharmaḥ satsādhusaṅgataḥ ।। 59.51 ।।  
  
apradveṣo hyaniṣṭeṣu tatheṣṭānabhinandanam।  
prītitāpaviṣādebhyo vinivṛttirviraktatā ।। 59.52 ।।  
  
saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇo nyāsaḥ kṛtānāmakṛtaiḥ saha।  
kuśalākuśalānāñca prahāṇaṃ tyāga ucyate ।। 59.53 ।।  
  
 avyaktādyo'viśeṣācca vikāro'sminnacetane।  
cetanācetānyatvavijñānaṃ jñānamucyate ।। 59.54 ।।  
  
pratyaṅgānāṃ tu dharmasya ityetallakṣaṇaṃ smṛtam ।  
ṛṣibhirdharmatattvajñaiḥ pūrve svāyambhuve'ntare ।। 59.55 ।।  
  
atra vo varttayiṣyāmi vidhirmanvantarasya yaḥ ।  
itaretaravarṇasya cāturvarṇasya caiva hi।  
pratimanvantarañcaiva śrutiranyā vidhīyate ।। 59.56 ।।  
  
ṛco yajūṣiṃ sāmāni yathāvat pratidaivatam।  
ābhūtasaṃplavasyāpi varjyaikaṃ śatarudriyam ।। 59.57 ।।  
  
vidhirhotraṃ tathā stotraṃ pūrvavatsampravartate।  
dravyastotraṃ guṇastotraṃ karma stotraṃ tathaiva ca।  
caturthamābhijanikaṃ stotrametaccaturvidham ।। 59.58 ।।  
  
manvantareṣu sarveṣu yathā devā bhavanti ye।  
pravarttayati teṣāṃ vai brahmastotraṃ caturvidham।  
evaṃ mantraguṇānāñca samutpattiścaturvidhā ।। 59.59 ।।  
  
atharvayajuṣāṃ sāmnāṃ vedeṣviha pṛthak pṛthak ।  
ṛṣīṇāntapyatāmugrantapaḥ paramaduścaram ।। 59.60 ।।  
  
mantrāḥ prādurbabhūvurhi pūrvamanvantareṣviha।  
paritoṣādbhayādduḥkhātsukhācchokācca pañcadhā ।। 59.61 ।।  
  
ṛṣīṇāṃ tapaḥkārtsnyena darśanena yadṛcchayā।  
ṛṣīṇāṃ yadṛṣitvaṃ hi tadvakṣyāmīha lakṣaṇaiḥ ।। 59.62 ।।  
  
atītānāgatānāntu pañcadhā ṛṣirucyate।  
atastvṛṣīṇāṃ vakṣyāmi hyārṣasya ca samudbhavam ।। 59. 63 ।।  
  
guṇasāmye varttamāne sarvasampralaye tadā।  
aticāre tu devānāmatideśe tayoryathā ।। 59.64 ।।  
  
abuddhipūrvakaṃ tadvai cetanārthaṃ pravarttate ।  
tena hyabuddhipūrvaṃ taccetanena hyadhiṣṭitam ।। 59.65 ।।  
  
varttate ca yathā tau tu yathā matsyodake ubhe।  
cetanādhiṣṭitaṃ tattvaṃ pravarttati guṇātmanā ।। 59.66 ।।  
  
karaṇatvāttathā kāryaṃ tadā tasya pravarttate।  
viṣaye viṣayitvācca hyarthe'rthitvāttathaiva ca ।। 59.67 ।।  
  
kālena prāpaṇīyena bhedāstu kāraṇātmakāḥ।  
saṃsidhyanti tadā vyaktāḥ krameṇa mahadādayaḥ ।। 59.68 ।।  
  
mahataśvāpyahaṅkārastasmādbhūtendriyāṇi ca।  
bhūtabhedāstu bhedebhyo jajñire te parasparam।  
saṃsiddhikāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ sadya eva vivarttate ।। 59.69 ।।  
  
yatholmukasruṭannūrddhvamekakālaṃ pravarttate।  
tathā vivṛtaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kālenaikena karmaṇā ।। 59.70 ।।  
  
yathāndhakāre khadyotaḥ sahasā sampradṛśyate।  
tathā vivṛtto hyavyaktāt khadyota iva celvaṇaḥ ।। 59.71 ।।  
  
sa mahān saśarīrastu yatraivāgre vyavasthitaḥ।  
tatraiva saṃsthito vidvān dvāraśālāmukhe sthitaḥ ।। 59.72 ।।  
  
mahāṃstu tamasaḥ pāre vailakṣaṇyādvibhāvyate ।  
tatraiva saṃsthito vidvāṃstamaso'nta iti śrutiḥ ।। 59.73 ।।  
  
buddhirvivarttamānasya prādurbhūtā caturvidhā ।  
jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ dharmaśceti catuṣṭayam ।। 59.74 ।।  
  
sāṃsiddikānyathaitāni supratīkāni tasya vai ।  
mahataḥ saśarīrasya vaivarttyāt siddhirucyate ।। 59.75 ।।  
  
atra śete ca yatpuryāṃ kṣetrajñānamathāpi vā।  
purīśayatvātpuruṣaḥ kṣetrajñānāt sucyate ।। 59.76 ।।  
  
kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetravijñānāt bhagavān matirucyate।  
yasmādbuddhyā tu śete ha tasmādbodhātmakaḥ sa vai ।  
saṃsiddhaye parigataṃ vyaktāvyaktamacetanam ।। 59.77 ।।  
  
evaṃ nivṛttiḥ kṣetrajñā kṣetrajñenābhisaṃhitā।  
kṣetrajñena parijñāto bhogyo'yaṃ viṣayastviti ।। 59.78 ।।  
  
ṛṣītyeṣa gatau dhātuḥśrutau satye tapasyatha।  
etatsanniyate tasmin brahmaṇā sa ṛṣiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 59.79 ।।  
  
nivṛttisamakālaṃ tu buddhyāvyaktamṛṣiḥ svayam।  
paraṃ hi ṛṣate yasmātparamarṣistataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 59.80 ।।  
  
gatyarthādṛṣaterddhātornāmanirvṛttirāditaḥ ।  
yasmādeṣa svayambhūtastasmāccātmarṣitā smṛtā।  
īśvarāḥ svayamudbhūtā mānasā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।। 59.81 ।।  
  
yasmānna hanyate mānairmahān parigataḥ puraḥ।  
yasmādṛṣanti ye dhīrā mahāntaṃ sarvato guṇaiḥ।  
tasmānmaharṣayaḥ proktā buddheḥ paramadarśinaḥ ।। 59.82 ।।  
  
īśvarāṇāṃ śubhāsteṣāṃ mānasāntarasāśca te।  
ahaṅkāraṃ tamaścaiva tyaktvā ca ṛṣitāṅgātāḥ ।। 59.83 ।।  
  
tasmāttu ṛṣayaste vai bhūtādau tattvadarśanāḥ।  
ṛṣiputrā ṛṣīkāstu maithunādgarbhasambhavāḥ ।। 59.84 ।।  
  
tanmātrāṇi ca satyañca ṛṣante te mahaujasaḥ।  
satyarṣayastataste vai paramāḥ satyadarśanāḥ ।। 59.85 ।।  
  
ṛṣīṇāñca sutāste tu vijñeyā ṛṣiputrakāḥ ।  
ṛṣanti vai śrutaṃ yasmādviśeṣāṃścaiva tattvataḥ।  
tasmāt śrutarṣayaste'pi śrutasya paridarśanāḥ ।। 59.86 ।।  
  
avyaktātmā mahātmā cāhaṅkārātmā tathaiva ca।  
bhūtātmā cendriyātmā ca teṣāṃ tajjñānamucyate ।  
ityetā ṛṣijātīstu nāmabhiḥ pañca vai śrṛṇu ।। 59.87 ।।  
  
bhṛgurmarīciratriśca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥkratuḥ।  
manurdakṣo vasiṣṭhaśca pulastyaśceti te daśa।  
brahmaṇo mānasā hyete udbhūtāḥ svayamīśvarāḥ ।। 59.88 ।।  
  
pravarttante ṛṣeryasmānmahāṃstasmānmaharṣayaḥ।  
īśvarāṇāṃ sutāstvete ṛṣayastānnibodhata ।। 59.89 ।।  
  
kāvyo bṛhaspatiścaiva kaśyapaścośanāstathā।  
utathyo vāmadevaśca apojyaścaiśijastathā ।। 59.90 ।।  
  
karddamo viśravāḥ śaktirvālakhilya stathā dharāḥ।  
ityete ṛṣayaḥ proktā jñānato ṛṣitāṅgatāḥ ।। 59.91 ।।  
  
ṛṣiputrānṛṣikāṃstu garbhotpannānnibodhata।  
vatsaro nagrahūścaiva bhāradvājastathaiva ca ।। 59.92 ।।  
  
bṛhadutthaḥ śaradvāṃśca agastyaścauśijastathā।  
ṛṣirdīrghatamāścaiva bṛhadukthaḥ śaradvataḥ ।। 59.93 ।।  
  
vājaśravāḥ suvittaśca suvāgveṣaparāyaṇaḥ।  
dadhīcaḥ śaṅkhamāṃścaiva rājā vaiśravaṇastathā।  
ityete ṛṣikāḥ proktāste satyādṛṣitāṅgatāḥ ।। 59.94 ।।  
  
īśvarā ṛṣikāścaiva ye cānye vai tathā smṛtāḥ।  
ete mantrakṣakṛtaḥ sarve kṛtsnaśastānnibodhata ।। 59.95 ।।  
  
bhṛguḥ kāvyaḥ pracetāstu dadhīco hyātmavānapi ।  
aurvo'tha jamadagniśca divaḥ sārasvata stathā ।। 59.96 ।।  
  
adviṣeṇa hyarūpaśca vītahavya sumedhasaḥ।  
vainyaḥ pṛthurdivodāsaḥ praśvāro gṛtsamānnabhaḥ।  
ekonaviṃśadityete ṛṣayo mantravādinaḥ ।। 59.97 ।।  
  
aṅgirā vedhasaścaiva bhāradvājo'tha bāṣkaliḥ।  
tathāmṛtastathā gārgyaḥ śenī saṃhṛtireva ca ।। 59.98 ।।  
  
purukutso'tha māndhātā ambarīṣastathaiva ca।  
āhāryothājamīḍhaśca ṛṣabho valireva ca ।। 59.99 ।।  
  
pṛṣadaśvo virūpaśca kaṇvaścaivātha mudgalaḥ।  
yuvanāśvaḥ paurukutsastrasaddasyuḥ sadasyumān ।। 59.100 ।।  
  
utathyaśca bharadvājastathā vājaśravā api ।  
āyāpyaśca suvittiśca vāmadevastathaiva ca ।। 59.101 ।।  
  
augajo bṛhadukthaśca ṛṣirdīrghatapāstathā।  
kakṣīvāṃśca trayastriṃśat smṛtā aṅgiraso varāḥ।  
ete mantrakṛtaḥ sarve kāśyapāṃstu nibodhata ।। 59.102 ।।  
  
kāśyapaścaiva vatsāro vibhramo raibhya eva ca।  
asito devalaścaiva ṣaḍete brahmavādinaḥ ।। 59.103 ।।  
  
atrirarccisanaścaiva śyāmāvāṃścātha niṣṭuraḥ।  
valgūtako munirddhīmāṃstathā pūrvātithiśca yaḥ।  
ityete cātrayaḥ proktā mantrakārā maharṣayaḥ ।। 59.104 ।।  
  
vasiṣṭhaścaiva śaktiśca tathaiva ca parāśaraḥ।  
caturtha indrapramatiḥ pañcamastu bharadvasuḥ ।। 59.105 ।।  
  
ṣaṣṭhastu maitrāvaruṇāḥ kuṇḍinaḥ saptamastathā।  
sudyumnaścāṣṭamaścaiva navamo'tha bṛhaspatiḥ।  
daśamastu bharadvājau mantrabrāhmaṇakārakāḥ ।। 59.106 ।।  
  
ete caiva hi kartāro vidharmadhvaṃsakāriṇaḥ।  
lakṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇaścaitadvihitaṃ sarvaśākhinām ।। 59.107 ।।  
  
heturhiteḥ smṛto dhātoryannihantyuditamparaiḥ।  
atha vārthapari prāpterhinotergatikarmaṇaḥ ।। 59.108 ।।  
  
tathā nirvacanaṃ brūyādvākyārthasyāvadhāraṇam ।  
nindāṃ tāmāhurācāryā yaddoṣannindyate vacaḥ ।। 59.109 ।।  
  
praṣūrvācchaṃsaterdhātoḥ praśasāṃ guṇavattayā।  
idantvidamidaṃ nedamityaniścitya saṃśayaḥ ।। 59.110 ।।  
  
idameva vidhātavyamityayaṃ vidhirucyate ।  
anyasyānyasya coktatvād‌budhaiḥ parakṛtiḥ smṛtā ।। 59.111 ।।  
  
yo hyatyantataroktaśca purākalpaḥ sa ucyate।  
purāvikrāntavācitvāt purākalpasya kalpanā ।। 59.112 ।।  
  
mantrabrāhmaṇakalpaistu nigamaiḥ śuddhavistaraiḥ ।  
aniścitya kṛtāmāhurvyavadhāraṇakalpanām ।। 59.113 ।।  
  
yathā hīdaṃ tathā tadvai idaṃ vāpi tathaiva tat।  
ityeṣa hyupadeśo'yaṃ daśamo brāhmaṇasya tu ।। 59.114 ।।  
  
ityetadbrāhmaṇasyādau vihitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ budhaḥ ।  
tasya tadvṛttiruddiṣṭā vyākhyāpyanupadaṃ dvijaiḥ ।। 59.115 ।।  
  
mantrāṇāṃ kalpanaṃ caiva vidhidṛṣṭeṣu karmasu।  
mantro mantrayaterdhātorbrāhmaṇo brahmaṇo'vanāt ।। 59.116 ।।  
  
alpākṣaramasandigdhaṃ sāravadviśvatomukham।  
astobhamanavadyañca sūtraṃ sūtravido viduḥ ।। 59.117 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte ṛṣilakṣaṇaṃ nāmonaṣaṣṭitamo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 59 ।


---
title: 060

---
।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
ṛṣayastadvacaḥ śrutvā sūtamāhuḥ sudustaram।  
kathaṃ vedā purā vyastāstanno brūhi mahāmate ।। 60.1 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca ।।  
dvāpare tu parāvṛtte manoḥ svāyambhuve'ntare ।  
brahmā manumuvācedaṃ tadvadiṣye mahāmate ।। 60.2 ।।  
  
parivṛtte yuge tāta svalpavīryā dvijātayaḥ।  
saṃvṛttāṃ yuga doṣeṇa sarve caiva yathākramam ।। 60.3 ।।  
bhraśyamānaṃ yugavaśādalpaśiṣṭaṃ hi dṛśyate।  
daśasāhasrabhāgena hyavaśiṣṭaṃ kṛtādidam ।। 60.4 ।।  
  
vīryaṃ tejo balaṃ vākyaṃ sarvañcaiva praṇaśyati।  
vedavedā hi kāryāḥ syurmābhūdvedavināśanam ।। 60.5 ।।  
  
vede nāśamanuprāpte yajño nāśaṃ gamiṣyati।  
yatre naṣṭe devanāśastataḥ sarvaṃ praṇaśyati ।। 60.6 ।।  
  
ādyo vedaścatuṣpādaḥ śatasāhasrasaṃjñitaḥ।  
punardaśaguṇaḥ kṛtsno yajño vai sarvakāmadhuk ।। 60.7 ।।  
  
evamuktastathetyuktvā manurlokahite rataḥ।  
vedamekaṃ catuṣpādaṃ caturdhā vyabhajatprabhuḥ ।। 60.8 ।।  
  
brahmaṇo vacanāttāta lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā।  
tadidaṃ varttamānena yuṣmākaṃ vedakalpanam ।। 60.9 ।।  
  
manvantareṇa vakṣyāmi vyatītānāṃ prakalpanam।  
pratyakṣeṇa parokṣaṃ vai tannibodhata sattamāḥ ।। 60.10 ।।  
  
asmin yuge kṛto vyāsaḥ pārāśaryaḥ parantapaḥ।  
dvaipāyana iti khyāto viṣṇoraṃśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 60.11 ।।  
  
brahmaṇā coditaḥ so'smin vedaṃ vyastuṃ pracakrame।  
atha śiṣyān sa jagrāha caturo vedakāraṇāt ।। 60.12 ।।  
  
jaiminiñca sumantuñca vaiśampāyanameva ca।  
pailanteṣāṃ caturthantu pañcamaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।। 60.13 ।।  
  
ṛgvedaśrāvakaṃ pailañjagrāha vidhivad dvijam ।  
yajurvedapravaktāraṃ vaiśampāyanameva ca ।। 60.14 ।।  
  
jaiminiṃ sāmavedārthaśrāvakaṃ so'nvapadyata।  
tathaivātharvavedasya sumantumṛṣisattamam ।। 60.15 ।।  
  
itihāsapurāṇasya vaktāraṃ samyageva hi।  
māñcaiva pratijagrāha bhagavānīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।। 60.16 ।।  
  
eka āsīdyajurvedastañcaturddhā vyakalpayat।  
caturhotramabhūttasmiṃstena yajñamakalpayat ।। 60.17 ।।  
  
ādhvaryavaṃ yajurbhistu ṛgbhirhotraṃ tathaiva ca।  
udgātraṃ sāmabhiśvakre brahmatvañcāpyatharvabhiḥ।  
brahmatvamakarodyajñe vedenātharvaṇena tu ।। 60.18 ।।  
  
tataḥ sṛcamuddhṛtya ṛgvedaṃ samakalpa yat।  
hotṛkaṃ kalpyate tena yajñavāhaṃ jagaddhitam ।। 60.19 ।।  
  
sāmabhiḥ sāmavedañca tenodgātramarocayat ।  
rājñastvatharvavedena sarvakarmāṇyakārayat ।। 60.20 ।।  
  
ākhyānaiścāpyupākhyānairgāthābhiḥ kulakarmabhiḥ।  
purāṇasaṃhitāścakre purāṇārthaviśāradaḥ ।। 60.21 ।।  
  
yacchiṣṭantu yajurvede tena yajñamathāyujat।  
yuñjānaḥ sa yajurvede iti śāstraviniścayaḥ ।। 60.22 ।।  
  
padānāmuddhṛtatvācca yajūṃṣi viṣamāṇi vai ।  
sa tenoddhṛtavīryastu ṛtvigbhirvedapāragaiḥ।  
prayujyate hyaśvamedhastena vā yujyate tu saḥ ।। 60.23 ।।  
  
ṛco gṛhītvā pailastu vyabhajattad vidhā punaḥ ।  
dviṣkṛtvā saṃyuge caiva śiṣyābhyāmadadatprabhuḥ ।। 60.24 ।।  
  
indrapramataye caikāṃ dvitīyāṃ bāṣkalāya ca।  
catasraḥ saṃhitāḥ kṛtvā bāṣkalirdvijasattamaḥ।  
śiṣyānadhyāpayāmāsa śuśrūṣābhiratān hitān ।। 60.25 ।।  
  
bodhantu prathamāṃ śākhāṃ dvitīyāmagnimāṭharam।  
pārāśaraṃ tṛtīyāntu yājñavalkyāmathāparām ।। 60.26 ।।  
  
indrapramatirekāntu saṃhitāṃ dvijasattamaḥ।  
adhyāpayanmahābhāgaṃ mārkaṇḍeyaṃ yaśasvinam ।। 60.27 ।।  
  
satyaśravasamagryantu putraṃ sa tu mahāyaśāḥ।  
satyaśravāḥ satyahitaṃ punaradhyāpayad dvijaḥ ।। 60.28 ।।  
  
so'pi satyataraṃ putraṃ punaradhyāpayadvibhuḥ।  
satyaśriyaṃ mahātmānaṃ satyadharmaparāyaṇam ।। 60.29 ।।  
  
abhavaṃstasya śiṣyā vai trayastu sumahaujasaḥ ।  
satyaśriyastu vidvāsaḥ śāstragrahaṇatatparāḥ ।। 60.30 ।।  
  
śākalyaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ tasmādanyo ratha(ā)ntaraḥ ।  
bāṣkaliśca bharadvāja iti śākhāpravartakāḥ ।। 60.31 ।।  
  
devamitrastu śākalyo jñānāhaṅkāragarvitaḥ।  
janakasyasa yajñe vai vināśamagamad dvijaḥ ।। 60.32 ।।  
  
।।śāṃśapāyana uvāca।।  
kathaṃ vināśamagamatsa munirjñānagarvitaḥ।  
janakasyāśvamedhena kathaṃ vādo babhūva ha ।। 60.33 ।।  
  
kimarthañcābhavadvādaḥ kena sārddhamathāpi vā।  
sarvametadyathāvṛttamācakṣva viditantava।  
ṛṣīṇāntu vacaḥ śrutvā taduttaramathābravīt ।। 60.34 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca।।  
janakasyāśvamedhe tu mahānāsītsamāgamaḥ।  
ṛṣīṇāntu sahasrāṇi tatrājagmuranekaśaḥ।  
rājarṣerjanakasyātha taṃ yajñaṃ hi didṛkṣavaḥ ।। 60.35 ।।  
  
āgatān brāhmaṇān dṛṣṭvā jijñāsāsyābhavattataḥ।  
konveṣāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kathaṃ me niścayo bhavet।  
iti niścitya manasā buddhiṃ cakre janādhipaḥ ।। 60.36 ।।  
  
gavāṃ sahasramādāya suvarṇamadhikaṃ tataḥ।  
grāmān ratnāni dāsāṃśca munīn prāha narādhipaḥ।  
sarvānahaṃ prapannano'smi śirasā śreṣṭhabhāginaḥ ।। 60.37 ।।  
  
yadetadāhṛtaṃ vittaṃ ye vaḥ śreṣṭhatamo bhavet।  
tasmai tadupanītaṃ hi vidyāvittaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 60.38 ।।  
  
janakasya vacaḥ śrutvā munayaste śrutikṣamāḥ।  
dṛṣṭvā dhanaṃ mahāsāraṃ dhanavṛddhyā jighṛkṣavaḥ ।  
śraddhayāñcakruranyonyaṃ vedajñānamadolbaṇāḥ ।। 60.39 ।।  
  
manasā gatavittāste mamedaṃ dhanamityuta।  
mamaivaitanna vetyanyo brūhi kiṃ vā vikalṣyate।  
ityevaṃ dhanadoṣeṇa vādāṃścakruranekaśaḥ ।। 60.40 ।।  
  
tathānyastatra vai vidvān brahmavāhasutaḥ kaviḥ।  
yājñavalkyo mahātejāstapasvī brahmavittamaḥ ।। 60.41 ।।  
  
brahmaṇo'ṅgāt samutpanno vākyaṃ provāca susvaram।  
śiṣyaṃ brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭo dhanametad gṛhāṇa bho ।। 60.42 ।।  
  
nayasva ca gṛhaṃ vatsa mamaitannātra saṃśayaḥ।  
sarvavedeṣvahaṃ vaktā nānyaḥ kaścittu matsamaḥ।  
yovā na prīyate vipraḥ sa me hyavatu mā'ciram ।। 60.43 ।।  
  
tato brahmārṇavaḥ kṣubdhaḥ samudra iva samplave ।  
tānuvāca tataḥ svastho yājñavalkyo hasanniva ।। 60.44 ।।  
  
krodha mākārṣuvidvāṃso bhavantaḥ satyavādinaḥ।  
vadāmahe yathāyuktaṃ jijñāsantaḥ parasparam ।। 60.45 ।।  
  
tato'bhyupāgamaṃsteṣāṃ vādā jagmuranekaśaḥ।  
sahasradhā śubhairarthaiḥ sūkṣmadarśanasambhavaiḥ ।। 60.46 ।।  
  
loke vede tathādhyātme vidyāsthānairalaṃkṛtāḥ।  
śāpottamaguṇairyuktā nṛpaughaparivarjanāḥ ।  
vādāḥ samabhavaṃstatra dhanahetormahātmanām ।। 60.47 ।।  
  
ṛṣayastvekataḥ sarve yājñavalkyastathaikataḥ।  
sarve te munayastena yājñavalkyena dhīmatā ।  
ekaikaśastataḥ pṛṣṭā naivottaramathāvruvan ।। 60.48 ।।  
  
tānvijitya munīn sarvān brahmarāśirmahādyutiḥ।  
śākalyamiti hovāca vādakarttāramañjasā ।। 60.49 ।।  
  
śākalya vada vaktavyaṃ kiṃ dhyāyannavatiṣṭase।  
pūrṇastvaṃ jaḍamānena vātādhmāto yathā dṛtiḥ ।। 60.50 ।।  
  
evaṃ sa dharṣitastena roṣāttāmrāsyalocanaḥ।  
provāca yājñavalkyaṃ taṃ puruṣaṃ munisannidhau ।। 60.51 ।।  
  
tvamasmāṃstṛṇavattyaktvā tathaivemān dvijottamān।  
vidyādhanaṃ mahāsāraṃ svayaṃgrāhaṃ jighṛkṣasi ।। 60.52 ।।  
  
śākalyenaivanuktaḥ syādyājñavalkyaḥ samabravīt।  
brahmiṣṭānāṃ balaṃ viddhi vidyātattvārthadarśanam ।। 60.53 ।।  
  
kāmaścārthena sambaddhastenārthaṃ kāmayāmahe ।  
kāmapraśradhanā viprāḥ kāmapraśrānvadāmahe ।। 60.54 ।।  
  
paṇaścaiṣo'sya rājarṣestasmānnītaṃ dhanaṃ mayā।  
etacchrutvā vacastasya śākalyaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ।  
yājñavalkyamathovāca kāmapraśrārthamadvacaḥ ।। 60.55 ।।  
  
brūhīdānīṃ mayoddiṣṭān kāmapraśrān yathārthataḥ।  
tataḥ samabhavadvādastayorbrahmavidormahān ।। 60.56 ।।  
  
sāgraṃ praśnasahasrantu śākalyastamucūcudat।  
yājñavalkyo'bravītsarvān ṛṣīṇāṃ śrṛṇvatāṃ tadā ।। 60.57 ।।  
  
śākalye cāpi nirvāde yājñavalkyastamabravīt ।  
praśramekaṃ mamāpi tvaṃ vada śākalya kāmikam।  
śāpaḥ paṇo'sya vādasya abruvan mṛtyumāvrajet ।। 60.58 ।।  
  
atha sannoditaṃ praśraṃ yājñavalkyena dhīmatā ।  
śākalyastamavijñāya sadyo mṛtyumavāpnuyāt ।। 60.59 ।।  
  
evaṃ mṛtaḥ sa śākalyaḥ praśravyākhyānapīḍitaḥ।  
evaṃ vādaśca sumahānāsītteṣāṃ dhanārthibhiḥ।  
ṛṣīṇāṃ munibhiḥ sārddhaṃ yājñavalkyasya caiva hi ।। 60.60 ।।  
  
sarvaiḥ pṛṣṭāṃstu sampraśrān śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ।  
vyākhyāya vai mune teṣāṃ praśrasāraṃ mahāgatiḥ ।। 60.61 ।।  
  
yājñavalkyo dhanaṃ gṛhya yaśo vikhyāpya cātmanaḥ।  
jagāma vai gṛhaṃ svasthaḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto vaśī ।। 60.62 ।।  
  
devamitrastu śākalyo mahātmā dvijasattamaḥ।  
cakāra saṃhitāḥ pañcabuddhimān padavittamaḥ ।। 60.63 ।।  
  
tacchiṣyā abhavan pañca mudghalo golakastathā।  
khālīyaśca tathā matsvaḥ śaiśireyastu pañcamaḥ ।। 60.64 ।।  
  
provāca saṃhitāstisraḥ śākapūrṇarathītaraḥ।  
niruktañca punaścakre caturthaṃ dvijasattamaḥ ।। 60.65 ।।  
  
tasya śiṣyāstu catvāraḥ ketavo dālakistathā।  
dharmaśarmā devaśarmā sarve vratadharā dvijāḥ ।। 60.66 ।।  
  
śākalye tu mṛte sarve brahmaghnāste babhūvire।  
tadā cintāṃ parāṃ prāpya gatāste brahmaṇo'ntikam ।। 60.67 ।।  
  
tān jñātvā cetasā brahmā preṣitaḥ pavanaḥpure।  
tatra gacchata yūyaṃ vaḥsadyaḥ pāpaṃ praṇaśyati ।। 60.68 ।।  
  
dvādaśārkaṃ namaskṛtyā tathā vai vālukeśvaram ।  
ekādaśa tathā rudrān vāyuputraṃ viśeṣataḥ।  
kuṇḍe catuṣṭaye snātvā brahmahatyāṃ tariṣyatha ।। 60.69 ।।  
  
sarve śīghratarā bhūtvā tatpuraṃ samupāgatāḥ।  
snānaṃ kṛtaṃ vidhānena devānāṃ darśanaṃ kṛtam ।। 60.70 ।।  
  
uttareśvaraṃ namaskṛtya vāḍavānāṃ prasādataḥ।  
sarve pāpavinirmuktā gatāste sūryamaṇḍalam ।। 60.71 ।।  
  
tadā prabhṛti tattīrthaṃ jātaṃ pātakanāśanam।  
vāyoḥ puraṃ pavitrañca vāyunā nirmitaṃ purā ।। 60.72 ।।  
  
añjanāgarbhasambhūtahanumānpavanātmajaḥ।  
yadā jāto mahādevohanumānsatyavikramaḥ।  
tadevaṃ nirmitaṃ tīrthaṃ vāyunā brahmayoninā ।। 60.73 ।।  
  
ūrvyāṃ jātāstu ye śūdrā brāhmaṇānāṃ niveditāḥ।  
vṛttyarthaṃ brahmayajñārthaṃ karasteṣu kṛto mahān ।। 60.74 ।।  
  
anena vidhinā jātaṃ viprāṇāṃ śāsanaṃ mahat ।  
goghno vāpi kṛtaghno vā surāpī gurūtalpagaḥ।  
vāḍādityaṃ namaskṛtya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 60.75 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte mahāsthānatīrthavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭitamo'dyāyaḥ ।। 60 ।


---
title: 061

---
।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
bhāradvājo yājñavalkyo gālakiḥ sālakistathā।  
dhīmān śatabalākaśca naigamaśca dvijottamaḥ ।। 61.1 ।।  
  
bāṣkaliśca bharadvājastisraḥ provāca saṃhitāḥ।  
rathītaro niruktañca punaścakre caturthakam ।। 61.2 ।।  
  
trayastasyābhavañchiṣyā mahātmāno guṇānvitāḥ।  
dhīmānnandāyanīyaśca pannagāriśca buddhimān।  
tṛtīyaścāryavaste ca tapasā śaṃsitavratāḥ ।। 61.3 ।।  
  
vītarāgā mahātejāḥ saṃhitājñānapāragāḥ।  
ityete bahvṛcāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ pravarttitāḥ ।। 61.4 ।।  
  
vaiśampāyanagotro'sau yajurvedaṃ vyakalpayat।  
ṣaḍaśītiśca tasyāpi saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakāḥ ।। 61.5 ।।  
  
śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau tāśca jagṛhuste vidhānataḥ।  
ekastatra parityakto yājñavalkyo mahātapāḥ।  
ṣaḍaśītiśca tasyāpi saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakāḥ ।। 61.6 ।।  
  
sarveṣāmeva teṣāṃ vai tridhā bhedāḥ prakīrttitāḥ।  
tridhā bhedāstu te proktā bhede'sminnavame śubhe ।। 61.7 ।।  
  
udīcyā madhyadeśāśca prācyāścaiva pṛthagvidhāḥ।  
śyāmāyanirudīcyānāṃ pradhānaḥ sambabhūva ha ।। 61.8 ।।  
  
madhya deśapratiṣṭānāmāruṇiḥ prathamaḥ stutaḥ।  
ālambirādiḥ prācyānāntrayodaśyādayastu te ।। 61.9 ।।  
  
ityete carakāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitāvādino dvijāḥ।  
ṛṣaya stadvacaḥ śrutvā sūtaṃ jijñāsavo'bruvan ।। 61.10 ।।  
  
carakādhvaryavaḥ kena kāraṇaṃ brūhi tattvataḥ।  
kiñcīrṇaṃ kasya hetośca vācakatvañca bhejire।  
ityuktaḥ prāha teṣāṃ sa carakatvamabhūdyathā ।। 61.11 ।।  
  
।।sūta uvāca ।।  
kāryamāsīdṛṣīṇāñca kiñcidbrāhmaṇasattamāḥ।  
merupṛṣṭhaṃ samāsādya taistadā tviti mantritam ।। 61.12 ।।  
  
yo no'tra saptarātreṇa nāgacched dvijasattamāḥ।  
sa kuryādbrahmavadhyāṃ vai samayo naḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 61.13 ।।  
  
tataste sagaṇāḥ sarve vaiśampāyana varjitāḥ।  
prayayuḥ saptarātreṇa yatra sandhiḥ kṛto'bhavat ।। 61.14 ।।  
  
brāhmaṇānāntu vacanād‌brahmavadhyāñcakāra saḥ ।  
śiṣyānatha samānīya sa vaiśaṇpāyano'bravīt ।। 61.15 ।।  
  
brahmavadyāñcaradhvaṃ vai matkṛte dvijasattamāḥ।  
sarve yūyaṃ samāgamya brūta me taddhitaṃ vacaḥ ।। 61.16 ।।  
  
।।yājñavalkya uvāca।।  
ahameva cariṣyāmi tiṣṭhantu munayastvime।  
balañcotthāpayiṣyāmi tapasā svena bhāvitaḥ ।। 61.17 ।।  
  
evamuktastataḥ kruddho yājñavalkyamathābravīt ।  
uvāca yattvayādhītaṃ sarvaṃ pratyarpayasva me ।। 61.18 ।।  
  
evamuktaḥ sa rūpāṇi yajūṃṣi pradadau guroḥ।  
rudhireṇa tathāktāni charditvā brahmavittamaḥ ।। 61.19 ।।  
  
tataḥ sa dhyānamāsthāya sūryamārādhayad dvijāḥ ।  
sūryabrahma yaducchinnaṃ khaṃ gatvā pratitiṣṭhati ।। 61.20 ।।  
  
tato yāni gatānyūrddhvaṃ yajūṃṣyādityamaṇḍalam।  
tāni tasmai dadau tuṣṭaḥ sūryo vai brahmarītaye।  
aśva rūpāya mārtaṇḍo yājñavalkyāya dhīmate ।। 61.21 ।।  
  
yajūṃṣyadhīyante yāni brāhmaṇā yena kena ca।  
aśvarūpāya dattāni tataste vājino'bhavan ।। 61.22 ।।  
  
brahmahatyā tu yaiścīrṇā caraṇāccarakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
vaiśampāyanaśiṣyāste carakāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ।। 61.23 ।।  
  
ityete carakāḥ proktā vājinastānnibodhata।  
yājñavalkyasya śiṣyāste kaṇvavaidheyaśālinaḥ ।। 61.24 ।।  
  
madhyandinaśca śāpeyī vidigdhaścāpya uddalaḥ।  
tāmrāyaṇaśca vātsyaśca tathā gālavaśaiśirī।  
āṭavī ca tathā parṇī vīraṇī saparāyaṇaḥ ।। 61.25 ।।  
  
ityete vājinaḥ proktā daśa pañca ca saṃsmṛtāḥ।  
śatamekādhikaṃ kṛtsnaṃ yajuṣāṃ vai vikalpakāḥ ।। 61.26 ।।  
  
putramadhyāpayāmāsa sumantumatha jaiminiḥ।  
sumantuścāpi sutvānaṃ putramadhyāpayatprabhuḥ।  
sukarmāṇaṃ sutaṃ sutvā putramadhyāpayatprabhuḥ ।। 61.27 ।।  
  
sa sahasramadhītyāśu sukarmāpyatha saṃhitāḥ।  
provācātha sahasrasya sukarmā sūryavarcasaḥ ।। 61.28 ।।  
  
anadhyāyeṣvadhīyānāṃstāñjaghāna śatakratuḥ।  
prāyopaveśamakarottato'sau śiṣyakāraṇāt ।। 61.29 ।।  
  
kruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tataḥ śakro varamasmai dadau punaḥ।  
bhāvinau te mahāvīryau śiṣyāvanalavarcasau ।। 61.30 ।।  
  
adhīyānau mahāprājñau sahasraṃ sahitāvubhau।  
etau surau mahābhāgau mā krudhya dvijasattama ।। 61.31 ।।  
  
ityuktvā vāsavaḥ śrīmānsukarmāṇaṃ yaśasvinam।  
śāntakrodhaṃ dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। 61.32 ।।  
  
tasya śiṣyo bhaveddhīmānpauṣyañjī dvijasattamāḥ।  
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśikyau dvitīyo'bhūnnarādhipaḥ ।। 61.33 ।।  
  
adhyāpayattu pauṣyañjī sahasrārddhantu saṃhitāḥ।  
tenānyodīcyasāmānyāḥ śiṣyāḥ pauṣyañjinaḥ śubhāḥ ।। 61.34 ।।  
  
śatāni pañca kauśikyaḥ saṃhitānāñca vīryavān।  
śiṣyā hiraṇyanābhasya smṛtāste prācyasāmagāḥ ।। 61.35 ।।  
  
lokākṣī kuthumiścaiva kuśītī lāṅgalistathā।  
pauṣyañjiśiṣyāścatvārasteṣāṃ bhedānnibodhata ।। 61.36 ।।  
  
rāṇāyanīyaḥ sa hi taṇḍiputrastasmādanyo mūlacārī suvidvān।  
sakatiputraḥ sahasātyaputra etān bhedān vitta lokākṣiṇastu ।। 61.37 ।।  
  
trayastu kuthumeḥ putrā auraso rasapāsaraḥ।  
bhāgavittiśca tejasvī trividhāḥ kauthumāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 61.38 ।।  
  
śauridyuḥ śrṛṅgiputraścadvāvetau caritavratau।  
rāṇāyanīyaḥ saumitriḥ sāmavedaviśāradau ।। 61.39 ।।  
  
provāca saṃhitāstisraḥ śrṛṅgiputro mahātapāḥ।  
cailaḥ prācīnayogaśca surālaśca dvijottamāḥ ।। 61.40 ।।  
  
provāca saṃhitāḥ ṣaṭtu pārāśaryastu kauthumaḥ।  
āsurāyaṇavaiśākhyau vedavṛddhaparāyaṇau ।। 61.41 ।।  
  
prācīnayogaputraśca buddhimāṃśca patañjaliḥ।  
kauthumasya tu bhedāste pārāśaryasya ṣaṭ smṛtāḥ।  
lāṅgaliḥ śālihotraśca ṣaṭ ṣaṭ provāca saṃhitāḥ ।। 61.42 ।।  
  
bhālukiḥ kāmahāniśca jaiminirlomagāyinaḥ।  
kaṇḍaśca kolahaścaiva ṣaḍete lāṅgalāḥ smṛtāḥ।  
ete lāṅgalinaḥ śiṣyāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ prasādhitāḥ ।। 61.43 ।।  
  
tato hiraṇyanābhasya kṛtaśiṣyo nṛpātmajaḥ ।  
so'karocca caturviṃśatsaṃhitā dvipadāṃ varaḥ ।  
provāca caiva śiṣyebhyo yebhyastāṃśca nibodhata ।। 61.44 ।।  
  
rāḍaśca mahavīryaśca pañcamo vāhanastathā।  
tālakaḥ pāṇḍakaścaiṣa kāliko rājikastathā।  
gautamaścājabastaśca somarājāpatattataḥ ।। 61.45 ।।  
  
pṛṣṭhagnaḥ parikṛṣṭaśca ulūkhalaka eva ca।  
yavīyasaśca vaiśālo aṃgulīyaśca kauśikaḥ ।। 61.46 ।।  
  
sālimañjarisatyaśca kāpīyaḥ kānikaśca yaḥ।  
parāśaraśca dharmātmā iti krāntāstu sāmagāḥ ।। 61.47 ।।  
  
sāmagānāntu sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭau dvau tu prakīrttitau।  
pauṣyañjiśca kṛtiścaiva saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakau ।। 61.48 ।।  
  
atharvāṇaṃ dvidhā kṛtvā sumanturadadad dvijāḥ ।  
kabandhāya punaḥ kṛtsraṃ sa ca vidyādyathākramam ।। 61.49 ।।  
  
kabandhastu dvidā kṛtvā pathyāyaikaṃ punardadau।  
dvitīyaṃ vedasparśāya sa caturddhākarot punaḥ ।। 61.50 ।।  
  
modo brahmabalaścaiva pippalādastathaiva ca।  
śaukāyaniśca dharmajñaścaturthastapanaḥ smṛtaḥ।?  
vedasparśasya catvāraḥ śiṣyāstvete dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। 61.51 ।।  
  
punaśca trividhaṃ viddhi pathyānāṃ bhedamuttamam।  
jājaliḥ kumudādiśca tṛtīyaḥ śaunakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 61.52 ।।  
  
śaunakastu dvidhā kṛtvā dadāvekantu babhrave।  
dvitīyāṃ saṃhitāṃ dhīmānsaindhavāyanasaṃjñite ।। 61.53 ।।  
  
saindhavo muñjakeśāya bhinnā sā ca dvidhā punaḥ।  
nakṣatra kalpo vaitānastṛtīyaḥ saṃhitānidhiḥ।  
caturtho'ṅgirasaḥ kalpaḥ śāntikalpaśca pañcamaḥ ।। 61.54 ।।  
  
śreṣṭhastvatharvaṇo hyete saṃhitānāṃ vikalpanāḥ।  
ṣaṭśaḥ kṛtvā mayāpyuktaṃ purāṇamṛṣisattamāḥ ।। 61.55 ।।  
  
ātreyaḥ sumatirdhīmānkāśyapo hyakṛtavraṇaḥ।  
bhāradvājo'gnivarcāśca vasiṣṭo mitrayuśca yaḥ ।  
sāvarṇiḥ somadattistu suśarmā śāṃśapāyanaḥ ।। 61.56 ।।  
  
ete śiṣyā mama brahman purāṇeṣu dṛḍhavratāḥ।  
tribhistisraḥ kṛtāstisraḥ saṃhitāḥ punareva hi ।। 61.57 ।।  
  
kāśyapaḥ saṃhitākarttā sāvarṇiḥ śāṃśapāyanaḥ।  
sāmikā ca caturthīsyātsā caiṣā pūrvasaṃhitā ।। 61.58 ।।  
  
sarvāstā hi catuṣpādāḥ sarvāścaikārthavācikāḥ।  
pāṭāntare pṛthagbhūtā vedaśākhā yathā tathā।  
catuḥsāhasrikāḥ sarvāḥ śāṃśapāyanikāmṛte ।। 61.59 ।।  
  
lomaharṣaṇikā mūlāstataḥ kāśyapikāḥ parāḥ।  
sāvarṇikāstṛtīyāstā yajurvākyārthapaṇḍitāḥ ।। 61.60 ।।  
  
śāṃśapāyanikāścānyā nodanārthavibhūṣitāḥ ।  
sahasrāṇi ṛcāmaṣṭau ṣaṭśatāni tathaiva ca ।। 61.61 ।।  
  
etāḥ pañacadaśānyāśca daśānyā daśabhistathā।  
vālakhilyāḥ samapraikhāḥ (ṣāḥ) sasāvarṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। 61.62 ।।  
  
aṣṭau sāmasahasrāṇi sāmāni ca caturddaśa।  
āraṇyakaṃ sahomañca etādgāyanti sāmagāḥ ।। 61.63 ।।  
  
dvādaśaiva sahasrāṇi chanda ādhvaryavaṃ smṛtam।  
yajuṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāñca yathā vyāso vyakalpayat ।। 61.64 ।।  
  
sagrāmyāraṇyakantatsyātsamantrakaraṇaṃ tathā।  
ataḥ paraṃ kathānāntu pūrvā iti viśeṣaṇam ।। 61.65 ।।  
  
grāmyāraṇyaṃ samantrañca ṛgbrāhmaṇayajuḥ smṛtam।  
tathā hāridravīyāṇāṃ khilānyupakhilāni ca।  
tathaiva taittirīyāṇāṃ parakṣudrā iti smṛtam ।। 61.66 ।।  
  
dve sahasre śatanyūne vede vājasaneyake।  
ṛggaṇaḥ pari saṃkhyāto brāhmaṇantu caturguṇam ।। 61.67 ।।  
  
aṣṭau sahasrāṇi śatāni cāṣṭau aśītiranyānyadhikaśca pādaḥ।  
etatpramāṇaṃ yajuṣāmṛcāñca saśukriyaṃ sākhila yājñavalkyam ।। 61.68 ।।  
  
tathā caraṇavidyānāṃ pramāṇaṃ saṃhitāṃ śrṛṇu।  
ṣaṭsāhasramṛcāmuktamṛcaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ punaḥ ।  
etāvadadhikaṃ teṣāṃ yajuḥ kāmaṃ vivakṣati ।। 61.69 ।।  
  
ekādaśa sahasrāṇi daśa cānyā daśottarāḥ ।  
ṛcāndaśa sahasrāṇi aśītitriśatāni ca ।। 61.70 ।।  
  
sahasramekaṃ mantrāṇāmṛcāmuktaṃ pramāṇataḥ।  
etāvadbhṛguvistāramanyaccātharvikaṃ bahu ।। 61.71 ।।  
  
ṛcāmatharvaṇāṃ pañca sahasrāṇi viniścayaḥ।  
sahasramanyadvijñeyamṛṣibhirviṃśatiṃ vinā ।। 61.72 ।।  
  
etadaṅgirasā proktanteṣāmāraṇyakaṃ punaḥ।  
iti saṃkhyā prasaṃkhyātā śākhābhedāstathaiva ca ।। 61.73 ।।  
  
karttāraścaiva śākhānāṃ bhede hetustathaiva ca।  
sarvamanvantareṣvevaṃ śākhābhedāḥ samāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 61.74 ।।  
  
prājāpatyā śrutirnityā tadvikalpāstvime smṛtāḥ।  
anityabhāvāddevānāṃ mantrotpattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। 61.75 ।।  
  
manvantarāṇāṃ kriyate surāṇāṃ nāmaniścayaḥ।  
dvāpareṣu punarbhedāḥ śrutānāṃ parikīrttitāḥ ।। 61.76 ।।  
  
evaṃ vedaṃ tadānyasya bhagavānṛṣisattamaḥ।  
śiṣyebhyaśca punardattvā tapastaptuṃ gato vanam।  
tasya śiṣyapraśiṣyaistu śākhābhedāstvime kṛtāḥ ।। 61.77 ।।  
  
aṅgāni vedāścatvāro mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥ।  
dharma śāstraṃ purāṇañca vidyāstvetāścaturdaśa ।। 61.78 ।।  
  
āyurvedo dhanurvedo gāndharvaścaiva te trayaḥ।  
arthaśāstraṃ caturthantu vidyāstvaṣṭādaśaiva tu ।। 61.79 ।।  
  
jñeyā brahmarṣayaḥ pūrvantebhyo devarṣayaḥ punaḥ।  
rājarṣayaḥ punastebhya ṛṣiprakṛtayastrayaḥ।  
tebhya ṛṣiprakṛtayo munibhiḥ saṃsitavrataiḥ ।। 61.80 ।।  
  
kaśyapeṣu vasiṣṭeṣu tathā bhṛgvahaṅagiro'triṣu।  
pañcasveteṣu jāyante gotreṣu brahmavādinaḥ।  
yasmādṛṣanti brahmāṇantena brahmarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 61.81 ।।  
  
dharmasyātha pulastyasya kratośca pulahasya ca।  
pratyūṣasya prabhāsasya kaśyapasya tathā punaḥ ।। 61.82 ।।  
  
devarṣayaḥ sutāsteṣāṃ nāmatastānnibodhata।  
devarṣī dharmaputrau tu naranārāyaṇānubhau ।। 61.83 ।।  
  
vālakhilyāḥ kratoḥ putrāḥ kardamaḥ pulahasya tu।  
kuberaścaiva paulastyaḥ pratyūṣasyācalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 61.84 ।।  
  
parvato nāradaścaiva kaśyapasyātmajāvubhau।  
ṛṣanti devān tasmātte tasmāddevarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 61.85 ।।  
  
mānave vaiṣaye vaṃśe ailavaṃśe ca ye nṛpāḥ।  
ailā aikṣvākanābhāgā jñeyā rājarṣayastu te ।। 61.86 ।।  
  
ṛṣanti rañjanādyasmātprajā rājarṣayastataḥ ।  
brahmalokapratiṣṭāstu smṛtā brahmarṣayo matāḥ ।। 61.87 ।।  
  
devalokapratiṣṭāśca jñeyā devarṣayaḥ śubhāḥ।  
indralokapratiṣṭāstu sarve rājarṣayo matāḥ ।। 61.88 ।।  
  
abhijātyā ca tapasā mantravyāharaṇaistathā।  
evaṃ brahmarṣayaḥ proktā divyā rājarṣayastu ye ।। 61.89 ।।  
  
devarṣayastathānye ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam।  
bhūtabhavyabhavajñānaṃ satyābhivyāhṛtaṃ tathā ।। 61.90 ।।  
  
sambuddhāstu svayaṃ ye tu sambuddhā ye ca vai svayam।  
tapaseha prasiddhā ye garbheyaiśca praṇoditam ।। 61.91 ।।  
  
mantravyāhāriṇo ye ca aiśvaryātsarvagāśca ye।  
ityete ṛṣibiryuktā devadvijanṛpāstu ye ।। 61.92 ।।  
  
etān bhāvānadhīyānā ye caita ṛṣayo matāḥ।  
saptaite saptabhiścaiva guṇaiḥ saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 61.93 ।।  
  
dīrghāyuṣo mantrakṛta īśvarā divyacakṣuṣaḥ।  
buddhāḥ pratyakṣadharmāṇo gotrapravartakāśca ye ।। 61.94 ।।  
  
ṣaṭkarmābhiratā nityaṃ śālino gṛhamedhinaḥ।  
tulyairvyavaharanti sma adṛṣṭaiḥ karmahetubhiḥ ।। 61.95 ।।  
  
agrāmyairvarttayanti sma rasaiścaiva svayaṃkṛtaiḥ।  
kuṭumbina ṛdvimanto bāhyāntaranivāsinaḥ ।। 61.96 ।।  
  
kṛtādiṣu yugākhyeṣu sarveṣveva punaḥ punaḥ।  
varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ kriyante prathamantu vai ।। 61.97 ।।  
  
prāptai tretāyugamukhe punaḥ saptarṣayastviha।  
pravarttayanti ye varṇā nāśramāṃścaiva sarvaśaḥ।  
teṣāmevānvaye vīrā utpadyante punaḥ punaḥ ।। 61.98 ।।  
  
jāyamāne pitā putreputraḥ pitari caiva hi।  
evaṃ sametyāvicchedādvarttayantyāyugakṣayāt।  
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi proktāni gṛhamedhinām ।। 61.99 ।।  
  
aryamṇo dakṣiṇā ye tu pitṛyāṇaṃ samāśritāḥ।  
dārāgnihotriṇaste vai ye prajāhetavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 61.100 ।।  
  
gṛhamedhināñca saṃkhyeyāḥ śmaśānānyāśrayanti te।  
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi nihitā uttarāyaṇe ।। 61.101 ।।  
  
ye śrūyante divaṃ prāptā ṛṣayo hyūrdvaretasaḥ।  
mantrabrāhmaṇakarttāro jāyante ha yugakṣaye ।। 61.102 ।।  
  
evamāvarttamānāste dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ।  
kalpānāṃ bhāṣyavidyānāṃ nānāśāstrakṛtaḥ kṣaye ।। 61.103 ।।  
  
bhaviṣye dvāpare caiva droṇirdvaipāyanaḥ punaḥ ।  
vedavyāso hyatīte'smin bhavitā sumahātapāḥ ।। 61.104 ।।  
  
bhaviṣyanti bhaviṣyeṣu śākhāpraṇayanāni tu।  
tasmai tadbrahmaṇā brahmatapasā prāptamavyayam ।। 61.105 ।।  
  
tapasā karma samprāptaṃ karmaṇā hi tato yaśaḥ।  
yaśasā prāpya satyaṃ hi satyenāpto hi cāvyayaḥ ।। 61.106 ।।  
  
avyayādamṛtaṃ śukramamṛtāt sarvameva hi।  
dhruvamekākṣaramidaṃ svātmanyeva vyavasthitam।  
bṛhattvādbṛṃhaṇāccaiva tadbrahmetyabhidhīyate ।। 61.107 ।।  
  
praṇavāva sthitaṃ bhūyo bhūrbhuvaḥsvariti smṛtam।  
ṛgyajuḥ sāmātharvarūpiṇe brahmaṇe namaḥ ।। 61.108 ।।  
  
jagataḥ pralayotpattau yattatkāraṇasaṃjñitam।  
mahataḥ paramaṃ guhyaṃ tasmai subrahmaṇe namaḥ ।। 61.109 ।।  
  
agādhāparamakṣayyaṃ jagatsammohanālayam।  
saprakāśapravṛttibhyāṃ puruṣārthaprayojanam ।। 61.110 ।।  
  
sāṅkhyajñānavatāṃ niṣṭā gatiḥ saṅgadamātmanaḥ।  
yattadavyaktamamṛtaṃ prakṛtibrahma śāśvatam ।। 61.111 ।।  
  
pradhānamātmayoniśca guhyaṃ sattvañca śabdyate।  
avibhāgastathā śukramakṣaraṃ bahu vācakam।  
paramabrahmaṇe tasmai nityameva namo namaḥ ।। 61.112 ।।  
  
kṛte punaḥ kriyā nāsti kuta evākṛtakriyā।  
sakṛdeva kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ yadvai loke kṛtākṛtam ।। 61.113 ।।  
  
śrotavyaṃ vai śrutaṃ vāpi tathaivāsādhusādhutā।  
jñātavyañcātha mantavyaṃ spraṣṭavyaṃ bhojyameva ca।  
draṣṭavyañcātha śrotavyaṃ jñātavyaṃ vātha kiñcana ।। 61.114 ।।  
  
darśitaṃ yadanenaiva jñānaṃ tadvai surarṣiṇām ।  
yadvai darśitavāneṣa kastadanveṣṭumarhati ।  
sarvāṇi sarvānsarvāṃśca bhagavāneva so'bravīt ।। 61.115 ।।  
  
yadā yatkriyate yena tadā tatso'bhimanyate।  
yenedaṃ kriyate pūrvaṃ tadanyena vibhāvitam ।। 61.116 ।।  
  
yadā tu kriyate kiñcitkenacidvāṅmayaṃ kvacit।  
tenaiva tatkṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ karttṝṇāṃ pratibhāti vai ।। 61.117 ।।  
  
viraktañcātiriktañca jñānājñāne priyāpriye।  
dharmādharmau sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ mṛtyuścāmṛtameva ca।  
ūrddhvantiryagadhobhāgastasyaivādṛṣṭakāraṇam ।। 61.118 ।।  
  
svāyambhuvo'tha jyeṣṭhasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭinaḥ।  
pratyekavidyambhavati tretāsviha punaḥ punaḥ ।। 61.119 ।।  
  
vyasyate hyekavidyantaddvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।  
brahmā caitaduvācādau tasmin vaivasvate'ntare ।। 61.120 ।।  
  
āvarttamānā ṛṣayo yugākhyāsu punaḥ punaḥ।  
kurvanti saṃhitā hyete jāyamānāḥ parasparam ।। 61.121 ।।  
  
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi śrutarṣīṇāṃ smṛtāni vai।  
tā eva saṃhitā hyete āvarttante punaḥ punaḥ ।। 61.122 ।।  
  
śritā dakṣiṇapanthānaṃ ye śmaśānāni bhejire।  
yuge yuge tu tāḥ śākhā vyasyante taiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। 61.123 ।।  
  
dvāpareṣviva sarveṣu saṃhitāśca śrutarṣibhiḥ।  
teṣāṃ gotreṣvimāḥ śākhā bhavantīha punaḥ punaḥ।  
tāḥ śākhāstatra karttāro bhavantīha yugakṣayāt ।। 61.124 ।।  
  
evameva tu vijñeyaṃ vyatītānāgateṣviha।  
manvantareṣu sarveṣu śākhāpraṇayanāni vai ।। 61.125 ।।  
  
atīteṣu atītāni varttante sāmprateṣu ca।  
bhaviṣyāṇi ca yāni syurvarṇyante'nāgateṣvapi ।। 61.126 ।।  
  
pūrveṇa paścimaṃ jñeyaṃ varttamānena cobhayam।  
etena kramayogena manvantaraviniścayaḥ ।। 61.127 ।।  
  
evaṃ devāśca pitara ṛṣayo manavaśca ye।  
mantraiḥ sahorddhvaṃ gacchanti hyāvarttante ca taiḥ saha ।। 61.128 ।।  
  
janalokātsurāḥ sarve paśukalpātpunaḥ punaḥ।  
paryāptakāle samprāpte sambhūtā naiva nasya (?) tu ।। 61.129 ।।  
  
avaśyambhāvinārthena sambadhyante tadā tu te।  
tataste doṣavajjanma paśyante rāgapūrvakam ।। 61.130 ।।  
  
nivarttate tadā vṛttisteṣāmādoṣadarśanāt ।  
evaṃ deva yugānīha daśakṛtvā nivarttate ।। 61.131 ।।  
  
janalokāttapolokaṃ gacchantīhānivarttanam।  
evaṃ devayugānīha vyatītāni sahasraśaḥ।  
nidhanaṃ brahmaloke vai gatāni munibhissaha ।। 61.132 ।।  
  
na śakyamānupūrvyeṇa teṣāṃ vaktuṃ savistarān ।  
anāditvācca kālasya asaṅkhyānācca sarvaśaḥ।  
manvantarāṇyatītāni yāni kalpaiḥ purā saha ।। 61.133 ।।  
  
pitṛbhirmunibhirdevaiḥ sārddhaṃ saptārṣibhiśca vai।  
kālena pratisṛṣṭānāṃ yugānāñca nivartanam ।। 61.134 ।।  
  
etena kramayogena kalpamanvantarāṇi tu।  
saprajāni vyatītāni śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ।। 61.135 ।।  
  
manvantarānte saṃhāraḥ saṃhārānte ca sambhavaḥ।  
devatānāmṛṣīṇāñca manoḥ pitṛgaṇasya ca ।। 61.136 ।।  
  
na śakyamānupūrvyeṇa vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi।  
vistarastu nisargasya saṃhārasya ca sarvaśaḥ।  
manvantarasya saṃkhyāṃ tu mānuṣeṇa nibodhata ।। 61.137 ।।  
  
devatānāmṛṣīṇāñca saṅkhyānārthaniśāradaiḥ।  
triṃśatkoṭyastu saṃpūrṇāḥ saṅkhyātāḥ saṅkhyayā dvijaiḥ ।। 61.138 ।।  
  
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutāni ca saṅkhyayā।  
viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi kālo'yaṃ sodhikān vinā ।। 61.139 ।।  
  
manvantarasya saṅkhyaiṣā mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitā।  
vatsareṇaiva divyena pravakṣyāmyantarammanoḥ ।। 61.140 ।।  
  
aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi divyayā saṅkhyayā smṛtam।  
dvipañcāśattathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni tu ।। 61.141 ।।  
  
caturddaśaguṇo hyeṣa kāla āhūtasaṃplavaḥ।  
pūrṇaṃ yugasahasraṃ syāttadaharbrahmaṇaḥ smṛtam ।। 61.142 ।।  
  
tatra sarvāṇi bhūtāni dagdhānyādityaraśmibhiḥ।  
brahmāṇamagrataḥ kṛtvā saha devarṣidānavaiḥ।  
praviśanti suraśreṣṭhaṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।। 61.143 ।।  
  
sa sraṣṭā sarvabhūtāni kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ।  
ityeṣa sthitikālo vai manordevarṣibhiḥ saha ।। 61.144 ।।  
  
sarvamanvantarāṇāṃ vai pratisandhiṃ nibodhata।  
yugākhyā yā samuddiṣṭā prāgevāsmin mayā tava ।। 61.145 ।।  
  
kṛtatretādi saṃyuktaṃ caturyugamiti smṛtam।  
tadekasaptatiguṇaṃ parivṛttaṃ tu sādhikam।  
manorekamadhīkāraṃ provāca bhagavān prabhuḥ ।। 61.146 ।।  
  
evaṃ manvantarāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāmeva lakṣaṇam।  
atītānāgatānāṃ vai varttamānena kīrttitam ।। 61.147 ।।  
  
ityeṣa kīrttitaḥ sargā manoḥ svāyambhuvasya ha।  
prati sandhintu vakṣyāmi tasya vai cāparasya tu ।। 61.148 ।।  
  
manvantaraṃ yathā pūrvamṛṣibhirdaivataiḥ saha।  
avaśyambhāvinārthena yathā tadvai nivarttate ।। 61.149 ।।  
  
asmin manvantare pūrvaṃ trailokyasyeśvarāstu ye।  
saptarṣayaśca devāste pitaro manavastathā।  
manvantarasya kāle tu sampūrṇe sādhakāstathā ।। 61.150 ।।  
  
kṣīṇādhikārāḥ saṃvṛttā buddhvā paryāyamātmanaḥ।  
maharlokāya te sarve unmukhā dadhire gatim ।। 61.151 ।।  
  
tato manvantare tasmin prakṣīṇā devatāstu tāḥ।  
sampūrṇe sthitikāle tu tiṣṭhantyekaṃ kṛtaṃ yugam ।। 61.152 ।।  
  
utpadyante bhaviṣyāśca yāvanmanvantareśvarāḥ।  
devatāḥ pitaraścaiva ṛṣayo manureva ca ।। 61.153 ।।  
  
manvantare tu sampūrṇe yadyanyadvai kalau yuge।  
sampadyate kṛtaṃ teṣu kaliśiṣṭeṣu vai tadā ।। 61.154 ।।  
  
yathā kṛtasya santānaḥ kalipūrvaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ।  
tathā manvantarānteṣu ādirmanvantarasya ca ।। 61.155 ।।  
  
kṣīṇe manvantare pūrve pravṛtte cāpare punaḥ।  
mukhe kṛtayugasyātha teṣāṃ śiṣṭāstu ye tadā ।। 61.156 ।।  
  
sptarṣayo manuścaiva kālāvekṣāstu ye sthitāḥ।  
manvantaraṃ pratīkṣante kṣīyante tapasi sthitāḥ ।। 61.157 ।।  
  
manvantaravyavasthārthaṃ santatyarthañca sarvaśaḥ।  
pūrvavat sampravarttante pravṛtte vṛṣṭisarjjane ।। 61.158 ।।  
  
dvandveṣu sampravṛtteṣu utpannāsvauṣadhīṣu ca।  
prajāsu ca niketāsu saṃsthitāsu kvacit kvacit ।। 61.159 ।।  
  
vārttāyāntu pravṛttāyāṃ saddharme ṛṣibhāvite ।  
nirānande gate loke naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।। 61.160 ।।  
  
agrāmanagare caiva varṇāśramavivarjite।  
pūrvamanvantare śiṣṭe ye bhavantīha dhārmikāḥ ।  
saptarṣayo manuścaiva santānārthaṃ vyavastitāḥ ।। 61.161 ।।  
  
prajārthaṃ tapatāṃ teṣāṃ tapaḥ paramaduścaram।  
utpadyantīha sarveṣāṃ nidhaneṣviha sarvaśaḥ ।। 61.162 ।।  
  
devāsurāḥ pitṛgaṇā munayo manavastathā।  
sarpā bhūtāḥ piśācāśca gandharvā yakṣarākṣasāḥ ।। 61.163 ।।  
  
tatasteṣāṃ tu ye śiṣṭā śiṣṭācārān pracakṣate ।  
saptarṣayo manuścaiva ādau manvantarasya ha।  
prārambhante ca karmāṇi manuṣyā daivataiḥ saha ।। 61.164 ।।  
  
manvantarādau prāgeva tretāyugamukhe tataḥ ।  
pūrvaṃ devāstataste vai sthite dharme tu sarvaśaḥ ।। 61.165 ।।  
  
ṛṣīṇāṃ brahmacaryeṇa gatvā''nṛṇyantu vai tataḥ।  
pitṝṇāṃ prajayā caiva devānāmijyayā tathā ।। 61.166 ।।  
  
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇi dharme varṇātmake sthitāḥ।  
trayīṃ vārttāṃ daṇḍanītiṃ dharmān varṇāśramāṃstathā।  
sthāpayitvāśramāṃścaiva svargāya dadhire matīḥ ।। 61.167 ।।  
  
pūrvaṃ deveṣu teṣveva svargāya pramukheṣu ca।  
pūrvaṃ devāstataste vai sthitā dharmeṇa kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। 61.168 ।।  
  
manvantare parāvṛtte sthānānyutsṛjya sarvaśaḥ।  
mantraiḥ sahordhvaṅgacchanti maharlokamanāmayam ।। 61.169 ।।  
  
vinivṛttavikārāste mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ।  
avekṣamāṇā vaśinastiṣṭhantyābhūtasaṃplavam ।। 61.170 ।।  
  
tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu sarveṣveteṣu sarvadā।  
śūnyeṣu devasthāneṣu trailokye teṣu sarvaśaḥ।  
upasthitā ihaivānye devā ye svargavāsinaḥ ।। 61.171 ।।  
  
tataste tapasā yuktā sthānānyāpūrayanti vai।  
satyaina brahmacaryeṇa śrutena ca samanvitāḥ ।। 61.172 ।।  
  
saptarṣīṇaṃ manoścaiva devānāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha।  
nidhanānīha pūrveṣāmādinā ca bhaviṣyatā ।। 61.173 ।।  
  
teṣāmatyantaviccheda iha manvantarakṣayāt।  
evaṃ pūrvānupūrvyeṇa sthitireṣānavasthitā।  
manvantareṣu sarveṣu yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। 61.174 ।।  
  
evaṃ manvantarāṇāntu pratisandhānalakṣaṇam।  
atītānāgatānāntu proktaṃ svāyambhuvena tu ।। 61.175 ।।  
  
manvantareṣvatīteṣu bhaviṣyāṇāṃ tu sādhanam ।  
evamatyantavicchinnaṃ bhavatyābhūtasaṃplavāt ।। 61.176 ।।  
  
manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttanāni ekāntatastāni mahargatāni।  
maharjanañcaiva janantapaśca ekāntagāni sma bhavanti satye ।। 61.177 ।।  
  
tadbhāvināṃ tatra tu darśanena nānātvadṛṣṭena ca pratyayena।  
satye sthitānīha tadā tu tāni prapte vikāre pratisargakāle ।। 61.178 ।।  
  
manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttanāni muñcanti satyantu tato'parānte।  
tato'bhiyogādviṣamapramāṇaṃ viśanti nārāyaṇameva devam ।। 61.179 ।।  
  
manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttaneṣu cirapravṛtteṣu nidhisvabhāvāt।  
kṣaṇaṃ rasaṃ tiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivandamānaḥ ।। 61.180 ।।  
  
ityuttarāṇyevamṛṣistutānāṃ dharmātmanāṃ divyadṛśāṃ manūnām।  
vāyupraṇītānyupalabhya dṛśyaṃ divyaujasā vyāsasamāsayogaiḥ ।। 61.181 ।।  
  
sarvāṇi rājarṣisurarṣimanti brahmarṣidevoragavanti caiva।  
sureśasaptarṣipitṛprajaiśairyuktāni samyak parivarttanāni ।। 61.182 ।।  
  
udāravaṃśābhijanadyutīnāṃ prakṛṣṭamedhābhisamedhitānām।  
kīrtidyutikhyātibhiranvitānāṃ puṇyaṃ hi vikhyāpanamīśvarāṇām ।। 61.183 ।।  
  
svargīyametat paramaṃ pavitraṃ putrīyametacca paraṃ rahasyam।  
japyaṃ mahatparvasu caitadagryaṃ duḥsvapnaśāntiḥ paramāyuṣeyam ।। 61.184 ।।  
  
prajeśadevarṣimanupradhānāṃ puṇyaprasūtiṃ prathitāmajasya।  
mamāpi vikhyāpanasaṃyamāya siddhiṃ juṣadhvaṃ sumaheśatatvam । 61.185 ।।  
  
ityetadantaraṃ proktaṃ manoḥ svāyambhuvasya tu।  
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmyaham ।। 61.186 ।।  
  
iti mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte prajāpativaṃśānukīrttanaṃ nāmaikaṣaṣṭitamo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 61 ।।  
  
।। iti śrīmadvāyupurāṇe pūrvārddhaṃ samāptam ।
